waman.
-  Alemmas deg-sen yessufeɣ-d aqerru-is si ṭtaq…
1-1-4-2- Aglam n tɣawsiwin
-  Udem-is yewlelles, werraɣ…
1-1-4-3- Aglam n yiwudam
-  Taqcict  tuzwaɣ,  iqder  d  tikelt  tamezwarut  a  tsel  awal  am  wa.  Tebra  i
wallen-is, tḥar ma tergem wagi s teɛriqt-is neɣ s sseka-is.
-  Tqcict terra-d nnehta…
-  Taqcict ur teṭṭif ara iman-is temkerfaf
-  Ccix  n  taddart  d  win  yeɣran  leqran  armi ijmmel  settin  ḥizb  iceggex  yerna
icax.
-  Basel d mmi-s n ccix aḥecraruf d azerbuḍ, yeɣra ciṭ mbaɣd yeṭaxer si lakul,
… basel yerra-tt kan i tcematin, d ssekran yal ass yerna ula d tissit n lkif…
-  Wrida ɣas akken tesṭuqqut ameslay am teblɛacret…
1-1-5- Tadiwennit
Deg  tullist  Taninna  amaru  yessemres  aṭas  n  tdiwennit,  tella-d  gar  yiwudam  n
1-1-5-1- Tadiwennit yellan gar Tninna d yiwen n uqcic i tḥuza di lkar
tullist, ad naf :
Taninna : suref-iyi.
Aqcic : uh ulac aɣilif…
59
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
1-1-5-2- Tadiwennit yellan gar wrida d tninna mi ruḥent ɣer salon de
thé
Wrida : […] ayen akk a tesleḍ tura seg imi-iw, ḥsu s nnig wul-iw ad am-t-iniɣ.
D  timeddukal  i  nella  seg  wasmi  nekcem  s  aɣerbaz,  ass-a  ur  bɣiɣ  ara  ad  am
seččeɣ  terẓeg  di  tlemmast  n  tiẓeṭ  maca  d  tadukli-nni  yekkan  gar-aneɣ  acḥal  d
aseggas i d-yessawlen…
Skud  ur  ifat  lḥal,  yewwi-d  ad  tedduḍ  yid-i  ɣer  wadi  yeznuzen  rriḥa,  bɣiɣ  ad
waliɣ ma yella kra i d-yewwi d amaynut.
Taninna  :  ḥuq  iɛǧeb-am-d  bu  tḥanut-inna  neɣ  yella  kra  n  weqcic  imelḥen  i  d-
temlaleḍ dahin iseḥḥer-ikem s wallen-is daɣen!
Wrida : waah! A taninna! Mačči ḥala aẓerbuḍ-inna i yid-d-yeqqimen ! Maca ilaq
ad tissineḍ weltma-s Litisyz d nettat a twaliḍ tura.
Mi iwḍen-t ɣer tḥanut:
Wrida :  rǧu, ur nkeččem ara tura, rǧu ciṭ, tessusmeḍ…
Wrida : iḥu ɣer daxel!
ksanen ara msakit !
Wrida : aha, tura dayen, maḥsub ur teẓriḍ ara akka i ggan waṭas n warrac ? Ur
1-1-5-3- Tadiwennit i yellan gar Tninna d Ḥend
Ḥend : melmi akka ara temzawaǧem a nečč seksu ?
Taninna : ur … Ur nettemzawaǧ ara, xaṭi ur nettemzawaǧ ara…
1-1-5-4- Tadiwennit i yellan gar Basel d Tninna
Basel : acuɣer i tenniḍ akka ? Ayɣer i s-tenniḍ i Ḥend ur netemzawaǧ ara ?
Taninna : i Litisya meskint anwa a tt-yaɣen ma mačči d kečč? Anwa i tettraǧǧu
yal ass di tḥanut-is ? ...
60
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
Basel : d lekdeb di leɛmer-iw ur ẓriɣ tagi i ɣef d-tettmeslayeḍ d timdukal-im i d-
yesnulfan aya akken a kem-ǧǧeɣ, ad lḥuɣ yid-sent.
Taninna  :  di  laɛna-ak  a  Basel,  ttu-yi  amek  akken  iyi-tettettuḍ  ma  tesuduneḍ
Litisya. Ulac tin iyi-d-iɛawden, d nekk i k-iwalan s wallen-iw mačči d abrid neɣ
sin…
Taninna mi d- tuɣal-d seg Tizi-Wezzu, iwala-tt Basel :
Basel  :  aah!  A  taqjunt  tuggiḍ-iyi!  Isaḥḥ-ikem  ad  tḍebreḍ  ɣef  yergazen…  bla
Rebbi ar d nekk a taɣeḍ ! …
1-1-5-5- Tadiwennit i yellan gar Lewnis d baba-s n Basel (ccix)
Lewnis : yelli ur tt-ttakeɣ ara arma cawraɣ-tt. Ma teqbel ad tezweǧ d mmit-wen,
a lxir a rrbeḥ. Ma tugi-t, rebbi ad isahel, ur yeqqris uyeddid, ur nɣilen waman.
Ccix : amek akka d tilawin ara yettextirin irgazen ara yaɣent !
Lewnis : aah! Mačči d rray i ɣer iɣ-d-iwessa rasul Allah salla Llah ɛalayhi wa
sallam.  Anɛam  a  ccix!  Maca  d  yelli  a  izewǧen  mačči  d  nekk,  ihi  d  nettat  s
yiman-is a yextiren, ḥala win tebɣa a taɣ…
Mi yelḥaq lexber ɣer Lewnis yelli-s iregem-itt Basel, yeɛna-t s axxam-nsen
Lewnis : sufeɣ-d izem-agi i tesɛiḍ, bla ddin n Rebbi, ar d a d-ddmeɣ leɛmer-is!
Aḥuḥan! Ad yettnekker ad ireggem yessi-s n yergazen…
Ccix : sṭafir Llah! Sɛu leɛqel…
Lewnis : a sɛiɣ leɛqel axir-ik! D kenwi i yeffeɣ, tebɣam ad teččem ddunit!
Ccix : aawwah! Kenwi s Leqbayel truḥem deg-sent, d tilawin a yettḍebiren fell-
awen…
61
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
Lewnis : yehwa-yasent! I yeṭreṭren d kenwi! Yelli mačči fell-i i tḍebber, tḍebber
ɣef tmeddurt-is, ɣef ussan-is as-d-iteddun.
Ccix : sṭafir Llah! Tkefrem! A ken-tečč tmes n lǧahennama asmi a tawḍem ɣer
ifassen n Sidi Rebbi!
Lewnis : times aql-aɣ tečč-yaɣ! Yella wayen yugaren aya…
Ccix : ur tuksaneḍ ara a mmi! Rebbi ɣafurun raḥim…
Lewnis : ḥessu a ccix ḥala leqder i gar-aneɣ ! Nugi-ken i nnesba, ifukk wawal,
yegzem,  yefra!  ...  Twalaḍ  tura  ɣer  ttrebga  n  mmi-k  a  Ccix  !  Yerna  a  teqqared
aken-id-rreɣ s abrid ! wissen kan ma d nekni i yeffeɣen seg-s neɣ d mmi-k…
1-1-4-6- Tadiwennit i yellan gar unelmad d yiwen n (Uɛafniḍ)
Aɛafniḍ  :  dabur  lukan  di  yi-ḥess  Basel,  nniɣ-as  taqbaylit  jjami  ad  d-tekcem  s
ixxamen-nneɣ, d Imrabḍen i nella bunsu! ...
Anelmad  :  lukan  fehmen akk  ilemeẓyen  i  k-yecban attih teqqel tmurt-nneɣ am
D ttaki d-tadiwennit d yeddan deg tullist « Taninna »
tmura irebḥen…
1-1-6-  Iwudam
ineḍruyen n tullist.
Iwudam  akken  nuɣ  tanumi  d  nutni  i  d  lsas  n  tullist,  d  wid  yesselḥayen
Deg  tullist  «  Taninna  »,  ad  naf  ṭṭuqten  yiwudam  deg-s,  llan  igejdanen  d
yinaddayen, ad ten i d-nebder yiwen yiwen.
1-1-6-1- Iwudam igejdanen
Taninna : d tin yesselḥan ineḍruyen n tullist, d nettat i d awadem agejdan, d tin
iruḥen ad d-tɣer deg tesdawit n Bab-Zwar (Lezzayer),  maca dina i d-temmuger
62
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
kra n wugguren, tuɣal-d ɣer tesdawit n Tizi-Wezzu, deg tmurt-is i tessen yiwen
n uselmad n umezruy, ixadeɛ-itt, terra-as-d ttar tesmaḥ deg-s.
Basel  :  d  aselmad  n  umezruy,  d  netta  i  yellan  d  amdakkel  n  Tninna  deg
tesdawit, yal tamedit yettruḥu ɣur-s ɣer tmezduɣt n tnelmadin, maca mi iruḥ ad
tt-id- yexḍeb tuggit imi teẓẓera dakken ixadɛ-itt d yiwet n teqcict.
1-1-6-2- Iwudam inaddayen
Wrida : d tamdakelt n Tninna, akken i ɣran-tt seg uɣerbaz amenzu almi leḥqent
ɣer  tesdawit,  yal  yiwet  d  acu  itt-cegɛen  ad  d-tɣer,  maca  tikwal  ttemlalent,  d
nettat  i  yefkan  afus  n  lemɛawna  i  Tninna,  mi  twala  Basel  d  win  ara  ixedɛen
Tannina,  tewwi-tt  twala  Basel  s  walen-is  yeqqim  d  yiwet  n  teqcict  deg  tḥanut
yesudun-itt.
Ḥend : d win yuɣen Taninna, yesɛa-d aqcic isema-as Saɛid.
Lewnis  : d baba-s  n Tninna, d win  yugin  ad d-yefk  yell-is biɣir  ma  icawer-itt,
yella-d umenuɣ gar-as d baba-s n Basel.
Ccix aḥecraruf : d baba-s n Basel, d win iruḥen s axxam n Tninna akken ad tt-id-
yexḍeb i mmi-s, yella-d umenuɣ gar-as d baba-s n Tninna.
Aɛafniḍ  :  d  amdakel  n  Basel,  d  win  yellan  deg  umenuɣ  yeḍran  gar  Lewnis  d
Ccix, yenna-as i Basel dakken taqbayli ur ilaq ara ad tt-taɣeḍ, d imrabḍen i nella.
Qasi-Aɛbruc : iberra-d si Tninna d Wrida zik mi qqarent tteɛadint deg wayla-is.
Nna Cabḥa : tesɛa tibḥirt n ufaqus, ttakrent-tt Wrida d Tninna.
Taseɛdit :ttakrent-as Wrida d Tninna iniɣman.
Si lḥaǧ : d win yettaɣen iniɣman i d-ttakrent Wrida d Tninna.
Anelmad : d win yerran sserf i wɛafniḍ akken iwata.
63
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
Tigawin d ineḍruyen iɣef tettwabna tullist, tullist « Taninna » tebna ɣef kraḍ
1-1-7- Tigawin
n tegnatin am yal tullist taqbaylit :
1-1-7-1- Tagnit n tazwara
Deg  tegnit  tamezwarut,  yefka-d  umaru  tamuɣli  ɣef  tudert  n  Tninna  mi
tella deg tesdawit n Bab-Zwar, syin akkin tuɣal ɣer tesdawit n Tizi-Wezzu anda
tessen Basel, akken tuɣal tettidir deg tayri akked talwit.
1-1-7-2- Tagnit n tigawin
Tebda-d  tagnit  n  tigawin  deg  tullist-agi  «  Taninna  »,  asmi  teɛreḍ  Wrida
Taninna  akken  ad  d-swent  lqahwa,  syin  tewwi-tt  Wrida  ɣer  yiwen  n  wemkan
anda  twala  Basel  win  akken  tḥemmel  d  yiwet  n  teqcict,  tuɣal  Tninna  teǧǧa-t,
ɛeddan kra n wussan ruḥen-d imawlan n Basel ad xeḍben Taninna, maca nettat
tugi ad t-teqbel, Basel mi yesla belli tugi-t yuɣal iḥbes-itt-id deg webrid, yennuɣ
yid-s yerna irgem-itt.
1-1-7-3- Tagnit n taggara
Deg tegnit-a yessebgen-d umaru tifrat n taluft, asmi i iruḥ baba-s n Tninna
ɣer baba-s n Basel, imi yergem yelli-s, syin yuɣal Basel yettuxeṭṭa deg tejmiɛt,
ɣer taggara Taninna tezweǧ, ma d Basel yunag.
1-1-8- Tasiwelt
Deg  tullist-agi  «  Taninna  »,  amaru  deg  wayen  yeɛnan  tasiwelt  tikwal  d
netta  i  d-iḥekkun  i  d-yettalsen  ɣef  yiwudam,  yerna  yesselḥaw  ineḍruyen,  dɣa
yella-d d azɣaray* deg  tullist-agi  imi  ur  yelli ara  gar  iwudam  n tullist, amedya
ɣef waya ad naf :
- Uuk ! Terra-d nnehta, xussent ḥala turin-is…
64
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
- Ara tetteddu lkar…
- Taqcict tuzwaɣ iqder d tikelt tamezwarut ara a tsel awal am wa.
- Aqcic yeṭṭeyiḥ, imeddukal-is ttaḍsan, netta simi irennu…
- Ccix n taddart yeɣra leqran armi ijemmel settin ḥizeb…
Ad  naf  tikwal-nniḍen,  amaru  deg  tsiwelt  yettban-d  am  akken  mačči  d
netta  i  yesselḥawen  iwudam,  acku  d  nitni  i  d-iḥekkun  ɣef  wayen  i  ten-yuɣen,
yefka-asen  tilelli  ad  lḥun  wa  ad  xedmen  akken  id-asen-yehwa,  aya-a  yettban-d
deg umqim awsil ‘nekk’ akked umatar udmawan …(ɣ) d …(n), ad neddem kra n
yimedyaten i d-yemmalen aya-agi :
- Asmi myussaneɣ d Basel, mmuteɣ si lferḥ…
- Akka i ddreɣ di lferḥ, smeckukuleɣ tirga anda ttwaliɣ kan mḥemmaleɣ nekk d
Basel.
- Cfiɣ asmi mezziyit, neddukul akken sked tin ur nexdim…
- Neɣra akken di llisi armi newweḍ ɣer tesdawit.
1-2-  Tulmisin n tullist « Laman d leɣder »
Ad neɛreḍ ad d-nekkes akk tulmisin i ɣef tebna tullist « Laman d laɣder »,
ama  dayen  yeɛnan  tutlayt  yesmres,  adeg,  akud,  iwudam,  aglam,  tigawin,
tasiwelt.
1-2-1- Tutlayt
Tutlayt  yessemres  umaru  deg  tullist-a  d  tutlayt  tushilt  ad  yefhem  yal
yiwen, d tin ttemaslayen yemdanen deg tudrin n Leqbayel, d tutlayt n yal ass.
Amaru  yettextiri  awalen-is,  amawal  n  yinan-is  yeččur  d  aṭas  n  lemɛani,
akken  daɣen  ad  t-id  naf  yessexdem  awalen  ijenṭaḍen,  ama  d  wid  n  tefransist,
65
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
ama  d  wid  n
taɛrabt,  akked  kra  n  yinzan  d  wawalen
iqburen  d
yimaynuten.Tikwal yella anda yessexdam tumnayt d userwes.
  Asemres n wawalen ijenṭaḍen
-  Awalen  ijenṭaḍen  i  d-yewwi  seg  taɛrabt:  lxir,  aɛaskriw,  axsim,  leqnaɛa,
-  Awalen ijenṭaḍen i d-yewwi seg tferransist: lgirra, sserbis, tribunal, lkarṭa,
tiḥila, ssem, lmaɛun
bagar, ssmana.
1-2-2- Adeg
Deg tullist-a « Laman d leɣder », ad d-naf kra n wawalen d yemmalen anda
ḍerrunt tigawin d yineḍruyen n tullist, amedya :
-  Taddart : amaru ur d-yudir ara isem-is taddart-a.
-  Axxam  n  Uwejhan  :  d  adeg  anda  yettidir  Uwejhan  akked  tmeṭṭut-is  d
warraw-is (sin warrac d snat teqcicin).
-  Tala  :  d  adeg  anda  llan  waman,  ɣer  din  i  tettruḥu  Wezna  ad  d-tɛemmer
-  Tribinal  n  Draɛ  Lmizan  :  d  amkan  uɣur  iruḥ  Ujendi,  yessufeɣ-d  lkarṭa  i
aman.
Yidir syen.
-  Aẓaɣar  :  d  adeg  uɣur  iruḥ  Meqran  ad  yekrez,  imi  tameṭṭut-is  texdeɛ-it
texdem-as asečči, din i yemmut ɣef lmaɛun.
-  Axxam  n  Ujendi  :  d  adeg  anda  yezdeɣ  Ujendi  d  tmeṭṭut-is,  ɣer  din  i  truḥ
Wazna  mi  tenɣa  argaz-is  teḍmeɛ  ad  tt-yaɣ  Ujendi,  taggara-nni  yefka-as
-  Abrid  n  tniri  : d adeg anda d-yerra Uwejhan ttar-is,  yeffer-as  i  Ujendi deg
abeqqa truḥ ad tettru.
ubrid-a yenɣat.
-  Tamazirt  n  uxxam Ujendi  : Wazna syen i  tɛedda,  mi truḥ s axxam Ujendi,
akken ad as-tinni melmi ad mzawaǧen.
66
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
1-2-3- Akkud
Deg  tullist  «  Laman  d  leɣder  »  llan  yimerna  n  wakud  i  d-yettbegginen
akud ideg ḍran yineḍruyen n tullist, llan wid d-yusan s udem usrid, amedya :
-  Yiwen n wass, yeẓra-tt tɛedda ɣer tala…
-  Kra n wussan akken yenṭel Aɛmer…
-  Zrin wussan…
-  Yiweḍ-d wass n yinig n Ujendi…
Akken  daɣen  llan  yimerna  d  yimattaren-nniḍen,  d  wid  d-nefhem  seg
tɣuri-nneɣ s telqayt i tullist, ussan-d s udem arusrid :
-  Zik  : d amernu  n wakkud  i d-yessekanen  akud  ideg teḍra tullist-a, d win d-
yusan s udem arusrid, amernu-a ur t-id yebdir ara deg uḍris, maca llan kra n
yineḍruyen sebganen-d dakken tullist-a teḍra zik-nni, amaru yefka-d nɛut i d-
yeskanen annect-a. Md :
-  Akka  i  tella  tmeddut  n  twacult  asmi  i  d-tewweḍ  Lgira  n  Lalman.  Awejhan
tessels-as Fransa d aɛsekriw, iruḥ ad yennaɣ ɣet tmurt-nni…
-
I lukan am tura, a d-tinim i wumi ttar, tella ddewla ad teḥkem s lḥebs ɣef win
yenɣan…
Ihi  akken  d-nefhem  tullist-a  d  tin  yeḍran  zik,  abeɛda  mi  tettruḥu  Wazna
yal  tikelt  ɣer  tala,  di  tallit-a  ur  d-ggrin  ara  yemdanen  ur  yesɛin  ara  aman  deg
uxxam, akken daɣen i d-yedda yakkan deg imedyaten ufella, ttar yella kan ɣer
wat  zik,  tura  win  ixedmen  kra,  yella  unabaḍ*  ara  yḥekmen  deg-s  abeɛda  win
yenɣan  am  tmenɣiwt-a  n  Meqran,  d  lḥebs  ɣer  lebda,  acku  ulac  deg  yisuḍaf
tikelxi.
Tagrest : d amatar i d-yemmalen akud ideg ḍran-tt kra n tigawin n tullist, yusa-d
s wudem arusrid, nefhem-it-id seg kra n wawalen i d-yeddan deg uḍris, amedya
: lkanun, qqajar, ad tseḥmuḍ…
67
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
1-2-4- Aglam
Deg  yal  tullist  nettaf-d aglam  n  yineḍruyen, tiɣawsiwin akked  yiwudam,
deg  tullist-a  amaru  yessemres  aglam  aya-agi  ad  tid  naf  deg  imedyaten  i  d-
nekkes seg uḍris :
1-2-4-1- Aglam n yineḍruyen
-  Ajendi iruḥ ɣer tribinal n Draɛ-Lmizan, yessufeɣ-as-d lkarṭa i Yidir.
-  Yeẓra-tt tɛedda ɣer tala weḥd-s yezwar-as s abrid ihder-as…
-  Tegga-as acečči-nni i Aɛmer, yiweḍ s azaɣer ad yekrez, yemmut ɣef lmaɛun…
-  Yiweḍ-d  wass-nni  n  yinig  n  Ujendi,  kkreɣ  deg  yiḍ  ruḥaɣ  zwareɣ  s  abrid  n
tniri…
-  Ajendi yerra afus-is ɣer deffir, yewwet s kra n ufud yellan deg iɣil-is.
-  … Yiwet n tcabcaqt teččur d akeffay yettkufut akken kan i t-id-teẓẓeg si taɣat.
1-2-4-2 Aglam n tɣawsiwin
1-2-4-3- Aglam n yiwudam
-  Di taddart, ala kra n yemɣaren iwessuren… id yeqqimen.
-
Ihi, Ajendi-a yesɛa sin n warrac d snat n teqcicin, d afellaḥ…
-  Ferḥen imawlan-nsen imi d-uɣalen d imuddiren…
-  Yidir aɛziz ḥala netta a d-yegrin d awrit.
-  Wazna tuɣal d tazeggaɣt.
1-2-5- Tadiwennit
1-2-5-1- Tadiwennit yellan gar Ujendi d Aɛmer
Ajendi a d-yettqeẓiẓ ɣer Aɛmer
Aɛmer  : bla Rebbi,  Ar d  nekk a d-yeddmen  leɛmer-ik,  ḥala anda  ur  k-ufiɣ  !  D
nekk a k-yenɣen !...
68
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
1-2-5-2- Tadiwennit yella gar Uwejhan d yidir
Yidir : anɛam a baba ! acu tebɣiḍ ?
Awejhan : qqim a mmi ad tesseḥmuḍ, ahat yenɣa-k qajjar, qim !
Awejhan : A mmi, tura gma-k yemmut, ad yettwarḥem, yessetma-k aten-tan akk
s yexxamen-nnsent, ḥala kečč i d-yeqqimen d ilemẓi…
1-2-5-3- Tadiwennit yellan gar Uwejhan d temɣart-is d mmi-tsen
Awejhan : acu i tenniḍ a tamɣart ? ...
Tamɣart : d tidet ! D tidet ay amɣar ! D ayen iwulmen…
Awejhan : ihi a mmi rray attan ɣur-k, muqqel ma tebɣid ad tzewǧeḍ aseggas-a
neɣ ad terǧuḍ ar qabel… Muqel tin i k-yehwan di teqcicin n taddart-a…
Tamɣart : annaɣ ay amɣar, acuɣer a nessexser idrimen di tmeɣra-nniḍen, ad yerr
kan yanegma-s, yefra ssuq…
Awejhan : ahat d ssuq-nni-nkent s tlawin i yefran, ssuq-nneɣ nekni urɛad…
Tamɣart : annaɣ ay argaz, acu i txuss yanegma-s ?
Awejhan  :  nniɣ-as  ad  yefren  netta,  mačči  d  kemm  i  wumi  nniɣ  fren-as-d  tin  a
yaɣ…
Tamɣart : ay amɣar ula d nekk d mmi, ilaq ad ḍebbreɣ fell-as…
Awejhan  :  ula  d  nekk  d  mmi,  maɛna  ur  cerrḍeɣ  ara  fell-as  ad  yaɣ  ta  neɣ  tin,
bɣiɣ d netta a izewǧen i iman-is…
Tamɣart : hhee! Xaṭi ! Nekk bɣiɣ ad yerr yanegma-s !
Awejhan: Ur t-testeqsaḍ ara ula akken ad am-d-yini ma yebɣa-tt neɣ xaṭi…
Tamɣart : ḥala beqqu a tt-yebɣu, ur tufiḍ acu i txuss yanegma-s…
69
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
Awejhan : aa wi ! Isar akka ! D aya kan i twalaḍ, ur twalaḍ ara yanegma-s-agi
tugar-it di leɛmer…
Tamɣart : acexlaf ! Ula d kečč tuggareḍ-iyi xemsa iseggasen maca tuɣeḍ-iyi…
Awejhan  : a ddin Rreb  ! D argaz  i  ilaq ad  yagger  tameṭṭut  mačči d tameṭṭut a
yuggaren argaz…
Tamɣart : xaṭi ! ... Ihi, nekk ad yerr yanegma-s…
Awejhan : bla Rebbi ma yuɣ-itt i lukan a tekk dunit yiwwas ! Ad iruḥ netta a d-
yextir tin i yas-yehwan, d tin a yaɣ ! …
Tamɣart : aha a nẓer ! Ma mačči d yanegma-s a yaɣ !…
Awejhan : a tamcumt henni-yaɣ, inaɣ kemm mačči bessif i iyi-tuɣad…
1-2-5-4- Tadiwennit yella gar Wezna d Ujendi
Ajendi : ihi a Wezna !... Amek telliḍ ?!!...Acu i kem-id-yecqan ?...
Wazna : nekk si tama-iw dayen xedmaɣ akken iyi-tenniḍ, usiɣ-d a k-ẓreɣ…
Ajendi : mreḥba yiss-m, acu i tebɣiḍ ?
Wazna  :  ihi,  nekk  Aɛmer  dayen  nɣiɣ-t…Ihi,  tura  usiɣ-d  akken  a  nehder  ɣef
Ajendi : aha tura a taqjunt, d kemm ara aɣeɣ ! Argaz-im amezwaru tenɣiḍt anef-
zzwaǧ-nneɣ…
Ajendi : tebɣiḍ ad uɣaleɣ d argaz-im, dɣa d tidet ? …
Wazna : ayagi teẓriḍ-t, teẓriḍ d kečč i bɣiɣ a yi-taɣeḍ…
ɛad wis sin…
Wazna tekker a d-teffeɣ.
1-2-5-5- Tadiwennit yella gar Wezna d Tasaɛdit
70
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
Tasaɛdit : ruḥ temneɛḍ, ur nessufuɣ ara awal tenɣiḍ Aɛmer…
1-2-5-6- Tadiwennit yellan gar Uwejhan d Wazna
Wazna tufa-d iman-is sdat n yemɣaren-is d ulews-is
Awejhan : uɣal s axxam n baba-m a yelli, yexḍa-kem ccɣel fell-aneɣ….
1-2-5-7- Tadiwennit yella gar Uwejhan d Ujendi
Awejhan : cihed, ma d ineslem i telliḍ ass-agi ad temmteḍ… Akken tenɣiḍ…
Ajendi  :  a  dda  Awejhan,  inaɣ  ur  tufiḍ  acu  i  k-xedmeɣ…  Aɛmer  d  Wazna  i  t-
Ihi d wiki d imedyaten n tdiwennit yellan deg tullist « Laman d leɣder »
yenɣan…
1-2-6- Iwudam
Ma nuɣal ɣer iwudan n tullist « Laman d leɣder » ad naf :
1-2-6-1- Iwudam igejdanen
Aɛmer : d mmi-s Uwejhan, d win tewwi Fransa di lawan-nni n lgira n Lalman,
asmi  d-yuɣal  s  axxam  yufa-d  Ajendi  yebɣa  ad  as-iḥwes  yiwet  n  tferka  n
uzemmur,  imi  Awejhan  yesɛa  ttbut  dakken tamurt-nni-ines, dɣa  yerbeḥ ccreɛ,
tegrad cceḥna  gar  Aɛmer d  Ujendi almi  yessaweḍ uneggaru-a  yenɣa  Aɛmer s
tḥila.
Wazna  :  d  tameṭṭut  n  Aɛmer,  d  tin  i  wumi  ikellex  Ujendi  s  tikarkas-is,  tenɣa
argaz-is s usečči i as-d-yewwi Ujendi.
1-2-6-2- Iwudam inaddayen
Awejhan  :  yesɛa  sin  warrac  d  snat  teqcicin,  d  afellaḥ,  yesɛa  aṭas  n  wurtan,  d
win d-yerran ttar, yenɣa Ajendi akken is-yenɣa mmi-s Aɛmer.
71
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
Ajendi : d mmi-s n lqayed, yeǧǧa-as-d baba-s aṭas n lxir : lmɛansra n uzemmur,
urtan, cci… Ikellex-as s tkerkas-is i Wazna tenɣa argaz-is.
Yidir : d mmi-s amaẓuẓ n Uwejhan, iqqim-d deg uxxam mi iruḥ baba-s d gma-
s  amenzu  ɣer  Fransa  ad  ḥarben,  Ajendi  yebɣa  asen-yeḥwes  yiwet  n  tfekka  n
uzemmur imi Yidir inuda amek ad iḥer ayla n baba-s si tkerḍa.
Tasaɛdit  :  d  tameṭṭut  n  Ujendi,  d  tin  is-yennan  i  Wazna  dakken  temneɛ  mu
sufɣen ara awal tenɣa Aɛmer.
Tamɣart n Uwejhan : tessker amenuɣ d Uwejhan ɣef Wazna, as-teqqqar Yidir
ad d-yerr yanegma-s Wezna bessif, Awejhan yegguma ad yeqqebel s wayen is-
tenna.
1-2-7- Tigawin
Tigawin d ineḍruyen iɣef tettwabna tullist, tullist « Laman d leɣder » tebna
ɣef kraḍ n tegnatin am yal tullist taqbaylit :
1-2-7-1 Tagnit n Tazwara
Deg  tegnit  tamezwarut  n  tullist-agi,  yewwi-d  deg-s  umaru  awal  ɣef
Uwejhan d twacult-is yettidiren deg talwit, yernu d argaz ḥemmlen akk medden
acku d win yelhan leɛmer yiwiḍ albeɛḍ, izweǧ-as i mmi-s ameqqran, dɣa akka i
sɛeddan ussan-nsen.
1-2-7-2- Tagnit n tigawin
Tebda-d mi i iruḥ Uwejhan d mmi-s Aɛmer ɣer lgirra, dɣa Ajendi yebɣa
ad as-yekkes taferka, imi  ḥala  mmi-s amecṭuḥ  i d-yegran deg wexxam.  Armi d
yuɣal  Uwejhan  tefra  taluft  maca  mazal  taɛdawet  gar  Aɛmer  d  Ujendi,  dɣa
Ajendi yeɛreḍ ad yerbeḥ tameṭṭut n Aɛmer akken ad t-tɛawen ad tekkes argaz-is
seg ddunit, ɣer taggara tenɣa argaz-is, ajendi yertaḥ wul-is.
72
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
1-2-7-3- Tagnit taggara
Tagnit taneggarut deg tullist-agi, tella-d deg wamur wis sin anda Awejhan
yefra  taluft  s  tririt  n  ttar  i  Ujendi,  dɣa  yufa-d  tamɣart  Ḥnini  tɛawent-it  yefra-d
ugur-is, yerra-d ttar, yenɣa Ajendi.
1-2-8- Tasiwelt
Deg  tullist-agi,  amaru  deg  tsiwelt-is  d  netta  i  yesselḥuyen  ineḍruyen,  d
netta i d-iḥekkun ɣef yiwudam d wayen i ten-iceɣben, meḥsub iwudam mačči d
nutni i d-yettmeslayen mačči d nutni i d-iḥekkun ɣef yiman-nsen, amaru ur sen-
yefki ara tilelli, maca amaru daɣen deg tullist-agi yella-d d azɣaray* imi ur yelli
ara seg yiwudam, amedya ɣef wa-aya :
- Awejhan yesɛa sin n warraw-is…
- Yeẓra-tt tɛedda ɣer tala weḥd-s, yezwar-as s abrid ihder-as…
- Tegga-as asečči-nni i Aɛmer…
Ma deg  wamur wis sin  n  tullist-agi  «  Laman d  leɣder  », ad d-naf amaru
yefka-asen  i  yiwudam  tagnit  ad  ḥkun  nutni  ɣef  yiman-nsen,  anida  Awejhan
ihder-d ɣef temɣart-nni i t-iɛawnen ad yerr ttar, ameday ɣef waya :
- … Ihi d Ḥnini-nni i ḥeqqren akk medden iyi-yefkan ttawil rriɣ-d ttar i mmi.
- Zriɣ tekreh Ajendi…
- Ruḥeɣ zriɣ-tt-id nniɣ-as akk ayen yellan.
1-3-  Tulmisin n « Tadyant n mmi-s uciban »
Ad neɛred ad nekkes tulmisin i ɣef tebna tullist « Tadyant n mmi-s uciban
», ama dayen yeɛnan tutlayt, akud, adeg, iwudam, aglam, tadiwennit, tigawin d
tsiwelt.
73
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
1-3-1- Tutlayt
Tutlayt yessemres umaru deg tullist-a d tutlayt tushilt ara ad d-yefhem yal
yiwen,  d  tin  ttemeslayen  yemdanen  deg  tudrin  n  Leqbayel,  d  tutlayt  n  yal  ass.
Tutlayt  deg  tullist-a  tettbeggin-d  dakken  timetti  d  taqburt,  aya  iban-d  deg
wawalen yessemres umaru : taddart, lkanun, aciban… Akken daɣen tella yiwet
-  Tadyant-agi  i  d-iteddun  cfiɣ  qqaren-tt-id  asmi  lliɣ  meẓẓiyeɣ  deg  taddart-
Amaru  deg  tullist-a  «  Tadyant  n  mmi-s  uciban  »  yessemres  kra  n  wawalen
n tenfalit :
nneɣ.
ijenṭaḍen:
  Asemres n wawalen ijenṭaḍen
-  Awalen  d-yewwi  seg  tutlayt  Taɛrabt:  lḥerma,  albaɛḍ,  taḥanut,  lqewa,  lǧib,
-  Awalen  d-yewwi  seg  tutlayt  tafransist  :  diminu,  lkarta,  llatay,  ṭṭabla,
meyyez, yesber.
yekmanda, akuntwar, icanṭiyen.
1-3-2- Adeg
Deg  tullist-a  «  Tadyant  n  mmi-s  uciban  »  ad  d-naf  kra  n  wawalen  i  d-
yemmalen adeg anda d-ḍran yineḍruyen n tullist :
Axxam n uciban : d adeg anda yezdeɣ Uciban d tmeṭṭut-is d mmi-s Meẓyan.
Lqahwa  :  d  adeg  anda  i  ixedem  Meẓyan,  yella  zik  d  aɛiwen  kan  i  yettɛawan
baba-s, zrin wussan tuɣal-ines.
Azniq n tejmaɛt : D adeg anda yeggan meẓyan mi t-iḥawez baba-s seg uxxam.
74
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
1-3-3- Akkud
amedya :
Deg  tullist  «  Tadyant  n  mmi-s  uciban  »  llan  yimerna  n  wakud  i  d-
yettbegginen  akud  ideg  ḍran  yineḍruyen,  llan  wid  d-yusan  s  udem  usrid,
-  Ass-agi ens deg uxxam, ma d azekka tameddit, ur k-ḥlaǧeɣ ara ad  d-
terreḍ ɣer da…
-  Azekka-nni, Meẓyan yegga akken das-yenna baba-s…
-  Mi yuli wass yerra ɣer lqahwa…
-  Tameddit n wass Meẓyan yerra s axxam.
-  A mmi yella waci i k-id-yeḍran iḍinizeryen neɣ xaṭi ?
-  A mmi yella kra i yeḍran yid-k iḍelli deg yiḍ ?
Akken daɣen llan imerna d yimataren nniḍen, d wid d-nefhem seg tɣuri-
nneɣ s telqayt i tullist, ussan-d s udem arusrid :
Zik : d amernu n wakkud i d-yessekanen akud ideg teḍra tullist-a, d win d-yusan
s udem arusrid, amernu-a ur d-yeddi ara deg uḍris, maca llan kra n yineḍruyen
sbegnen-d  dakken  tullist-a  teḍra  zik-nni,  amaru  yefka-d  nɛut  i  d-teskanen
annect-a. Md :
-  Tadyant-agi i d-iteddun cfiɣ qqaren-tt-id asmi lliɣ meẓẓiyeɣ di taddart-nneɣ
-  Seg wasmi meẓẓiy yettɛawan baba-s di lqahwa…
Iḍ : d amatar n wakkud i d-yusan s wudem arusrid, nefhem-it-id seg tefyart-a :
-  Yeɣli-d ṭṭlam berra mi d-yekcem yiwen wergaz ɣer lqehwa.
Tagrest : d amatar i d-yemmalen dakken tullist teḍra deg tegrest, d win d-yusan
s wudem arusrid, yedda-d deg tefyar-a :
-  Meẓyan  iɣil  d  yiwen  i  d-yewwi  webrid,  yenɣa-t  usemmiḍ  dɣa  yekcem-d,
axaṭer di tegrest ciṭ n yemdanen i yettɛeṭilen ɣer wurar n ddiminu…
75
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
-  Γas yenɣa-t usemmiḍ yesber.
-  Awi tafersaḍit neɣ kra nniḍen tenseḍ deg wezniq n tejmiɛt…
1-3-4- Aglam
Ma nuɣal ɣer uglam d-yeddan deg tullist-a ad t-id naf :
1-3-4-1- Aglam n yineḍruyen
-  Ad xedmeɣ ayen yelhan
-  Yeɣli-d ṭṭlam berra mi d-yekcem yiwen n wergaz ɣer lqehwa.
-
Meẓyan yettmuqul-it kan, winna ikemmel awal.
1-3-4-2- Aglam n tɣawsiwin
-  Yemma-s terdem-d seksu akken yettfuru.
-  Ala tijeɣlin i wumi ara tesleḍ ttennalent tabaqit.
-  …yerna yerfed ussu-nni n tmara.
1-3-4-3- Aglam n yiwudam
-  Aciban  d  yiwen  n  urgaz  ur  d-yettwabder  ara  di  taddart  ḥala  deg  wayen
yelhan…
-  Meẓyan,  yemmal-as  baba-s  leqder…Yesɛeda  ussan-is  di  lehna.  Seg  wasmi
meẓẓiy  yettɛawan  baba-s  di  lqahwa:  yettɛawan-it  deg  uheggi,  di  tardan
leḥwal, deg wefraḍ n tḥanut…
1-3-5- Tadiwennit
1-3-5-1- Tadiwennit gar Meẓyan d Urgaz i d-yussan ɣur-s ɣer lqahwa
Meẓyan : ihi ilaq ad teffeɣ-ḍ akken a d-ḍummeɣ agens, ad sekkreɣ…
Argaz : ulac uɣilif, maca d kečč i d-usiɣ ad k-ẓreɣ !
Meẓyan : inaɣ, d lxir kan.
76
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
Argaz : ala lxir i ger-aneɣ.
Meẓyan : acu i k-id-yecqan ihi ?
Argaz : acḥal aya i sɛiɣ yiwet n taluft ḥala kečč i izemren ad iyi-tɛiwweneḍ deg-
Meẓyan : d lxir kan, inaɣ ?
Argaz : d lxir kan a mmi ! ihi tamsalt-a tewɛer aṭas maca ma tɛawneḍ-iyi ad ak-
muddeɣ azal n wayen ara d-tḥarreḍ di 10 neɣ 15 iseggasen n lxedma di lqehwa-
s…
inek.
Meẓyan : d acu-tt temsalt-a ?
Argaz : tamsalt-inu teshel ma tɛawneḍ-iyi aṭas n yedrimen ara d-trebḥeḍ deg-s.
Mebla ma ntezzi ntenneḍ ad ak-tt-id-iniɣ d acu-tt : d yiwen i yellan d axsim-iw,
bɣiɣ ad t-kkseɣ si dunit…
Meẓyan : alaṭif, ad aɣ-yemneɛ Rebbi si temgart !
Argaz : maca, ad trebḥeḍ ayen swayes ara tesɛeddiḍ ddunit-ik merra !
Meẓyan : xaṭi, xdiɣ, ḥala aya ur xeddmeɣ ara !
Argaz  :  ax  tura  wigi  ṭṭef-iten,  a  tt-ih  tqerɛet-agi  deg-s  bla  ma  nniɣ-ak…
Xemmem, meyyez, ma isuɛd-ik i hayen, mulac err-iyi-ten-id. Ma yella tqebleḍ,
ad ak d-rnuɣ ɛecra neɣ ɛecrin imuren am win.
1-3-5-2-Tadiwennit yellan gar Meẓyan d baba-s
Meẓyan : a baba ! Ass-a yusa-d yiwen yessewhem-iyi yessuter-iyi-d yiwen n cci
aqli ḥareɣ amek ara xedmeɣ…
Baba-s : Acu yellan a mmi ? D lxir kan ?
Meẓyan : ur ẓriɣ ara ma d lxir neɣ amek ara das-semmiɣ, aqlin ḥesleɣ.
77
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
Baba-s  :  ini-iyi-d  a  mmi  d  acu  yellan  !  Ahat  zemreɣ  ad  k-iniɣ  awal  ara  k-
yessuffɣen di taluft-agi.
Meẓyan yuls-as taluft
Baba-s : yerna teṭṭefeḍ-d idrimen.
Meẓyan : yeǧǧa-ten-id ɣef ukuntwar.
Baba-s  :  ass-agi  ens  deg  uxxam,  ma  d  azekka  tameddit,  ur  k-ḥlaǧeɣ  ara  ad  d-
terreḍ ɣer da…
Mi d-yuɣal azekka-nni s axxam Meẓyan…
Baba-s : a mmi, yella kra i k-id-yeḍran iḍinizeryen neɣ xaṭi?
Meẓyan : xaṭi a baba, acemma ur d-yeḍri.
Baba-s : yella win i d-yekkren ad-k-yewwet, neɣ ad k-yennaɣ ?
Meẓyan : ula yiwen ur d-ikkir ad iyi-wwet neɣ ad iyi yennaɣ.
Baba-s : ihi, uɣal ula tameddit-a ens din…
Yerna yusad Meẓyan s axxam
ad k-yewwet, neɣ ad k-yeḥqer di tejmiɛt ?
Meẓyan : ula yiwen ur d-yerri. Acuɣer a baba ?
Baba-s : ihi, ula tameddit-a ruḥ ens daɣen din ad teẓreḍ…
Yerna yuɣal-d Meẓyan s axxam
Baba-s : a mmi, yella kra yeḍran yid-k iḍelli deg yiḍ ?
Meẓyan : acemma wer d-yelli a baba.
78
Baba-s :  iḍinizeryen, yella kra n win d-yerran ad k-id yeḍreq seg wezniq, neɣ
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
Baba-s : ulac win k-id-yennulen neɣ k-id yeɛnan ?
Meẓyan : xaṭi a baba, ula yiwen ur iyi-d-isuma…
Baba-s : twalaḍ a mmi ! I yeswa mi ara yili ur teḍlimeḍ ara imdanen…
Ulac tullist melba iwudam, acku d wid iɣef tebna tullist, ihi iwudam d yesselḥan
1-3-6- Iwudam
ineḍruyen n tullist-a d wigi :
1-3-6-1- Iwudam igejdanen
Meẓyan  :  d  netta  i  d  awadem  agejdan,  yesalḥan  ineḍruyen  n  tullist,  d  win
iɛaweqqen amek ara yexdem sdat n talluft i t-id-yussan.
Aciban :  d win iwerran abrid iseḥan i mmi-s.
1-3-6-2- Iwudam inaddayen
Argaz : d win i d-yusan ɣer lqahwan n Meẓyan, iḍelb-as ad as-yenɣ axsim-is.
Kra n yemdanen n taddart : mi yeqqim meẓyan deg yiḍ deg berra almi yuli wass,
seqsan fell-as.
Meẓyan deg berra.
Lɛmum d lexwal n Meẓyan : ruḥen ɣer uciban akken ad d-ẓẓren aɣer yettnusu
Ṭṭemman n wedrum d iderman-nniḍen : ruḥen ɣer uciban akken ad yerr mmi-s s
axxam neɣ ad d-tawin leɛmum-is neɣ xwal-is.
Tameṭṭut n uciban : tettak-as imensi i Meẓyan yal tikelt mi ara yejbu seg berra,
ad yečč akken ad yuɣal ad yens daw n rref n lǧameɛ n taddart.
79
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
1-3-7- Tigawin
Tigawin  d  ineḍruyen  iɣef  tettwabna  tullist,  tullist  «  Tadyant  n  mmi-s
uciban» tebna ɣef kraḍ n tegnatin am yal tullist taqbaylit :
1-3-7-1- Tagnit n tazwara
Deg tullist-agi, amaru yewwi-d awal ɣef tedyant n mmi-s uciban, d tin d-
ḥekkun  zik  i  warraw-nsen,  yerna  yemmeslay-d  ɣef  Uciban  yellan  d  argaz
yettwassnen deg taddart, d win i d-yettwabdaren ḥala deg wayen yelhan, d win
yesɛan  mmi-s  irebba-t  am  warrac  n  taddart,  yemla-as  ḥala  ayen  yelhan,  ddren
deg talwit.
1-3-7-2- Tagnit n tigawin
Tella-d asmi  i d-yusa  yiwen  n wergaz ɣer lqehwa  n Meẓyan,  yessuter-as
ad as-yenɣ axsim-is, dɣa yesseḍmeɛ-it s wedrim, mi yuɣal Mezyan ɣer wexxam
yemla-as i baba-s ayen d-yeḍran yid-s, dɣa Aciban yessufeɣ mmi-s seg wexxam
Tefra taluft n mmi-s Uciban, mi yeffeɣ seg wexxam yeṭṭes acḥal n wussan
deg berra maca ula d yiwen ur d-yenṭiq yid-s, dɣa din yemla-as Uciban i mmi-s
dakken  win  yeṭṭfen  sser  deg  iman-is  ulac  d  acu  ara  yeggad,  anda  s  yehwa  ad
ad yeṭṭes deg tejmiɛt.
1-3-7-3- Tagnit n taggra
iruḥ, anda s yehwa ad yeqqim.
1-3-8-Tasiwelt
Amedya ad naf :
- Aciban yesɛa yiwen n mmi-s.
80
Amaru  deg  tullist-agi,  d  netta  i  d-yeḥkan  tadyant,  d  netta  i  yesselḥan
ineḍruyen, iwudam d netta i d-ihedren fell-asen, yettales-d ayen i iɛeddan yakan.
- Mezyan yegga akken yennum, yensa ddaw n tdanit n lǧameɛ n taddart.
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
- Mezyan mmi-s Uciban yeḍfer kra id-as-yemla baba-s..
- Llan kra n leɛmum-is d xwal-is yerzan ɣer baba-s…
1-4- Tulmisin n tullist « Ad gen tameɣra »
Ad neɛred ad nekkes tulmisin i ɣef tebna tullist « Ad gen tamaɣra », ama
dayen  yeɛnan  tutlayt,  adeg,  akkud,  iwudam,  aglam,  tadiwennit,  tigawin,  d
tsiwelt.
1-4-1- Tutlayt
Tutlayt  yessemres  umaru  deg  tullist-a  d  tutlayt  tushilt  ara  ad  yefhem  yal
yiwen, d tin ttemaslayen yemdanen deg tudrin n Leqbayel, d tutlayt n yal ass.
Amaru deg tullis-a ɣas yessemres awalen ijenṭaḍen imi maci s waṭas am tullist
Taninna :
  Asemres n wawalen ijenṭaḍen
-  Awalen d-yewwi seg tutlayt taɛrabt : tiswiɛin, leḥmeq, leɛmum, lferḥ, lweḥy.
-
Awalen d-yewwi seg tutlayt tasransist : mitru.
1-4-2- Adeg
deg-sen :
Imataren  n  wadeg  i-yeddan  deg  tullist-a  seg  mi  bdan  ineḍruyen-is  almi
fukken,  nekkes-iten-id  akken  ma  llan  yerna  nuder-d  kra  n  yineḍruyen  yeḍran
Fransa  :  d  adeg  uɣur  iruḥ  Akli-u-Muḥ,  d  lmizirya-nni  n  isggasen  n  30-40  i  t-
yewwin ad d-ixeddem dina.
Axxam n wakli : deg-s i ḍran-t kran n tigawin n tullist, xedmen deg-s tameɣra n
sin warraw-is, ɣur-s i yettara Wakli yal anebdu mi d-yettas seg Fransa acku dina
i ttidiren waraw-is d tmeṭṭut-is.
81
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
Tibucicin  yellan  deffir  n  uxxam  :  d  adeg  anda  tella  teslent  uɣur  iɛellaq  Wakli
Tullist-a  d  tin  yeḍran  deg  yiseggasen  n  62  acku  Akli  deg  yiseggasen  n  30-40
iman-is s wemrar.
1-4-3- Akud
yella deg Fransa.
1-4-4- Aglam
Deg  tullist  amaru  ur  d-nufi  ara  yessemres  aglam  n  tɣawsiwin  acku
ineḍruyen  n  tullist  d  wid  yesseḥzanen,  ulac  deg-sen  tiɣawsiwin  ara  d-yeglem
umaru,  ma  d  aglam  n  yineḍruyen  d  yiwudam  nefka-d  fell-asen  kra  n
yimedyaten:
1-4-4-1- Aglam n yineḍruyen
-  Yewweḍ-d wass n tmeɣra, taddart akk teggugi-d ɣer uxxam n Wakli…
-  Ufan-t  iɛelleq  iman-is  s  umrar  ɣer yiwet  n  teslent  gar  tbucicin  yellan  deffir
wexxam.
1-4-4-2- Aglam n yiwudam
-  Arrac d tullas ttaḍsan.
-
Imdanen akk ɛyan.
1-4-5- Tadiwennit
U Muḥ d sin warraw-is
-  Akli yezder di ttexmam, yettezzi rewint deg wallaɣ-is.
Deg tullist-a amaru ur yessemres yiwet n tdiwennit d tin d-yellan gar Akli
Akli : bɣiɣ ad d-necdeɣ atmaten-iw ɣer tmaɣra.
Arraw-is : ḥala tagi ur d-iḍerrun ara, u, ma llan di tmeɣra a-t-an nekni ḥsu si tura
tilin nneɣ tebṭel…
82
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
1-4-6- Iwudam
Akken neẓra, iwudam sɛan azal d ameqqran deg tullist, fell-asen i tebna,
acku  d  nutni  i  yeselḥayen  ineḍruyen-is.  Ihi  deg  tullist-a  «  Ad  gen  tameɣra  »
iwudam ɣef ayed tebna d wigi :
1-4-6-1- Iwudam igejdanen
Akli  :  D  awadem  agejdan,  d  netta  i  yesalḥan  ineḍruyen  n  tullist,  yebda-d  s
trebga  n  watmaten-is,  yerfed  imawlan-is  akken  iwata,  maca  mi  yesɛa  sin
warraw-is ffɣen-as i webrid ur s-uɣen ara awal.
Arraw n wakli : llan deg sin deg-sen, d nutni i d sseba mi yenɣa baba-tsen iman-
1-4-6-2- Iwudam inadayen
Lexwal  n  warraw  n  wakli  :  d  nutni  i  wumi  yehder  wakli  akken  ad  as-inin  i
warraw n watma-tsen akken ad d-ǧǧen Akli ad d-yeɛred atmaten-is.
Atmaten n wakli :  d wid ur neḥḍir ara tameɣra n warraw n xuya-tsen.
Tilawin i d-necden : ta tekkat amendayer, ta teceṭṭeḥ.
Lxalat : d tid i d-yewwin cnawi n ɣeẓẓiɣ aberwaq, A Qsenṭina, serbi-d lbira, rfed
aḍar-im a Yamna…
Arrac d tullas : d wid yettaḍsan ɣef umhaw-nni itettin awalen di cnawi.
Amhaw : d win iḥamlen ad yesseḍs inebgawen, itetti awalen deg cnawi.
is.
83
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
Tigawin d ineḍruyen iɣef tettwabna tullist, tullist « Ad gen tameɣra» tebna
1-4-7- Tigawin
ɣef kraḍ n tegnatin am yal tullist taqbaylit :
1-4-7-1- Tagnit n tazwara
Amaru  yefka-d  tamuɣli  ɣef  Wakli  u  Muḥ  d  twacult-is,  imi  yunag  ɣer
tmurt n Fransa akken ad yexdem fell-asen, yettuɣal-d kan deg unebdu, zewǧen-
as wexxam-nsen, kra n yiseggasen akken yesɛa-d sin n warrac.
1-4-7-2- Tagnit n tigawin
Asmi meqqer-it warraw n Wakli uɣalen ur d-myezgen ara d leɛmum-nsen,
teɣli-d teɛdawt gar-asen, asmi kkren ad xedmen tameɣra taddart akk terza-d ḥala
atmaten  n  Wakli  ugin warraw-is ad ten-id-ɛerḍen,  ulac d acu  ur  yexdim Wakli
maca ugin.
1-4-7-3- Tagnit n taggara
Imi atmaten n Wakli ur  ḥdiren ara tameɣra n warraw-is, Akli iɣaḍ-it lḥal
ɣef wannect-a, dɣa ur yezmir ara ad yesber, iruḥ yenɣa iman-is s wemrar.
1-4-8- Tasiwelt
Tasiwelt,  ɣef  akken  i  d-tusa  deg  tullist-agi  tella-d  am  tid  iɛeddan  imi
amaru  yella-d  d  azɣaray  meḥsub  ur  yelli  ara  seg  yiwudam,  maca  d  netta  iten-
yesselḥawen,  d  netta  i  d-yettalsen  ineḍruyen,  ur  d  asen-yefki  ara  tilelli  i
yiwudam ad ssenfali wa ad  ḥkun nutni ɣef yiman-nsen akken id-asen-yehwa, d
amaru i yemlan iḥulfan-nsen d tiktiwin-nsen, aya-agi yettban-d deg yimedyaten-
agi :
- Akli u Muḥ d argaz i tewwi lmizirya-nni n iseggasen n 30-40…
- Yennuɣ d tlufa d laẓ armi i d-yessas kra swayes yesfeḍ llaẓ…
84
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
- Atmaten-is rran ixxamen mbaɣd mi mmuten yemɣaren.
- Ufan-t iɛelleq iman-is s umrar ɣer yiwet n teslent…
- Akka i teḍra d wid ikkren ad d-gen tameɣra…
1-5- Tulmisin n tullist « Tuɣalin »
Ad  neɛred  ad  nekkes  tulmisin  n  tullist  «  Tuɣalin  »,  ama  dayen  yeɛnan
tutlayt, adeg, akkud, iwudam, aglam, tadiwennit, tigawin d tsiwelt.
1-5-1- Tutlayt
Tutlayt  yessemres  umaru  deg  tullist-a  d  tutlayt  tushilt  ara  ad  yefhem  yal
yiwen, d tin ttemaslayen yemdanen deg tudrin n Leqbayel, d tutlayt n yal ass.
Tutlayt-a d tin d-yemmalen dakken timetti d taqburt, aya iban-d deg kra n
wawalen  yessemres  umaru,  amedya:  lkanun,  times,  isɣaren,  abbu,  inyen,
amegruc, addaynin, aḥnay. Zik i ssewayen yemdanen ɣef lkanun imi ur sɛin ara
lgaz, akken daɣen seḥmay ɣer lkanun.
  Asemres n wawalen ijenṭaḍen
-  Awalen  d-yewwi  seg  tutlayt  taɛrabt  :  wlidem,  tfehmeḍ,  amaḥbus,  xalt-as,
lexber, lɛasker, asenduq, aberrani.
  Asemres n wawalen iqburen : aɣalad, acabcaq, tesfacceṭ, tebbeẓ.
1-5-2- Adeg
Ad naf axxam anda tettidir Sekura d wergaz-is, sin warraw-is d yemɣaren-
is, amaru ur t-id yebdir ara s wuden usrid imi nefehmit-id si tɣuri-neɣ i tullist-a.
Addaynin : yella daxel n yexxamen ɣer wat zik, dina i tella taɣaṭ, Sekkura tmud-
as tummeẓt n uslen akken ad tezhu deg-s, ad teẓẓeg akkefay i warraw-is.
Afrag  :  d  amkan  yellan  tama  n  uxxam,  Sekkura  tettqeddir    isɣaren  dinna  deg
lawan n tegrest.
Tamazirt : d amkan anda Sekkura d wergaz-is Lmulud jerḍen asaɣur.
85
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
1-5-3- Akud
Ad  naf  amaru  yessexdem  aṭas  n  imerna  n  wakud  mi  d-yettemeslay  ɣef
yineḍruyen n tullist-a, aya ad t-id-naf deg imedyaten i d-nekkes seg uḍris :
-  kra  n  useggas  akken,  yemzawaǧ  meqran  mmi-s  amenzu  n  Qasi  akked
Sekkura.
-  Tafsut id-yezzin mbaɛd zzwaǧ-nnsen, ilul-d Weɛmer.
-  Sin  wagguren  akken  ilul  Weɛmer,  Meqran  yeṭṭef-d  lkaɣeḍ  ad  d-yesɛeddi
lɛasker neɣ tiwizi n tmara, akken qqaren.
-  Aseggas-nni amezwaru sya ɣer da a d-ṭṭfen tabrat-is wat-wexxam.
-  Yiwen n wass deg ussan n tegrest, ddunit akk tettban-d tacebḥant seg wedfel
ur tettwaliḍ ara ula yiwen di berra, yal wa yennelmeɛ.
-  Ɛeddan kraḍ iseggasen seg wasmi d-yewweḍ usenduq s axxam.
-
Iseggasen mbaɛd yena weqcic ɣer Lmilud isemma-yas Saɛid.
-  Tameddit mi d-uɣalen s axxam ufan yusa-d Lḥaǧ Qasi d temɣart-is si leɛzib-
nni i ɣer ruḥen deg wedrar.
-  Ad tili d ttesɛa n yiḍ, slan i wesḍebṭeb di tewwurt n berra.
-  Azekka-nni Meqran yeddem agelzim d telwaḥt yerra ɣer tmeqbert.
Akken ad d-naf daɣen llan yimataren i d-yusan s wudem arusrid:
-  Ekker, a-t-an waggur n yiṭij deg igeni, amaru yebɣa ad yini yuli wass.
Ma  nuɣal  ɣer  uglam  d-yeddan  deg  tullist-a,  ad  tid  naf  yeɛna  ineḍruyen,
1-5-4- Aglam
tiɣawsiwin d yiwudam :
1-5-4-1- Aglam n yineḍruyen
-  Teṭṭerḍeq tewwurt.
-  Run madden ɣef wergaz i ssnen.
-  Wardia,teɣli tesṛeɛ ur teẓri anda tedda.
86
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
1-5-4-2- Aglam n tɣawsiwin
-  Ddunit akk tettban-d d tacebḥant seg wedfel.
1-5-4-2- Aglam n yiwudam
-  Sekura tecbeḥ tezyen, terna d tasusam.
-  Ferḥen yemɣaren ula d nutni.
-  Aqcic-a iḥeml-it aṭas baba-s.
-  Lmulud yezɛef.
1-5-5-Tadiwennit
1-5-5-1- Tadiwennit gar Sekura d wergaz-is Lmulud
Sekura : kker ! A-t-an waggur n yiṭij yuli deg igenni ! Ilaq ass-agi ad nefru ajraḍ
usaɣur deg inyen n waɣzen.
Lmulud : aah ! Aɛni ɛerqent-am ssbeḥ-agi daɣ…?
Sekura : a wlidi henna-yi, mačči ḥala kečč i iyi-iqqimen…
Lmulud : ur lliɣ ara d wliḍim, tfehmeḍ ?
1-5-5-2- Tadiwennit gar lmulud d waɛmer
Lmulud : eeeh ! I kemmini aniwer ara truḥeḍ ? …ruḥ bru-d i gma-k, ay aɣyul.
Weɛmer yerra s adaynin as d yebru.
1-5-5-3- Tadiwennit gar Meqran d baba-s lḥaǧ Qasi
Meqran ad yesḍebṭib deg tewwurt.
Lhaǧ qasi : d anwa ?
Meqran : d nekk a baba, d meqran…
87
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
Lḥaǧ qasi : ini-d d anwa ur ttmesxir ara neɣ wellah ar d-n-ffeɣ ɣer-k ma tsellkeḍ
seg ifassen-iw.
Meqran : d nekk a baba, d Meqran
1-5-6-Iwudam
iwudam i ɣef tebna tullis-a:
1-5-6-1- Iwudam igejdanen
Lḥaǧ qasi : ɣur-k a d-teqerrebeḍ ɣuri ! Aẓ akkin ! Aẓ akkin !
Iwudam bḍan ɣef snat  n  tewsatin;  igejdanen d  yinaddayen.  Ad  neɛred ad  nefk
Sekura : d awadem yesselḥan ineḍruyen n tullist, d tin ḥettmen yemɣaren-is ad
taɣ alews-is.
Meqran : d win i iruḥen ɣer lɛesker, ṭfen-t din 14 n yiseggasen, mi d-yuɣal fkan-
as  axxam  deg  Tizi-wezzu,  meɛna  tameṭṭut-is  yufa-d  yuɣ-it  gma-s  Lmulud,  dɣa
Meqran yerna-tt kan i ssekran.
1-5-6-2- Iwudam inaddayen
Lḥaǧ Qasi d Werdiya : d imawlan n Meqran, d nutni i t-id-irebban almi yuɣal d
argaz,  ḥeznen  fell-as  mi  ɣilen  d  mmi-tsen  Meqran  i  d-iwwin  lɛasker    deg
usenduq-nni yeččuren d ijdi, ɣilen yemmut.
Lmulud  :  d  gma-s  n  Meqran,  d  win  yuɣen  yanegma-s  mi  d  yeffeɣ  lexber
yemmut gma-s Meqran , mi d yesɛa mmi-s yuɣal yettaḥeqqar mmi-s n gma-s.
Weɛmer  d  Saɛid  :  Weɛmer  d  mmi-s  n  Meqran,  Saɛid  d  mmi-s  n  Lmulud,  d
Weɛmer i yesseqdac Lmulud, yettruḥu yettsariḥ-as-d i weɣyul.
Ḥemmama : d tajaret n Sekura, tettas-d tettɣimi yid-s.
88
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
Lǧiran n lḥaǧ Qasi : ussan-d ɣer lǧanaza yellan ɣer Lḥaj Qassi akken daɣen d-
ussan mi d-iban win yemmuten, di tazwara d aɣlad i ɣelden deg-s.
Tigawin d ineḍruyen iɣef tettwabna tullist, tullist « Tuɣalin» tebna ɣef kraḍ
1-5-7- Tigawin
n tegnatin am yal tullist taqbaylit :
1-5-7-1-Tagnit n tazwara
lehna i wat wexxam.
1-5-7-2- Tagnit n tigawin
Amaru yewwi-d ɣef Meqran d zwaǧ-is akked Sekkura, d wamek sɛaddan
ussan  n  tayri  d  lehna  ladɣa  seg-mi  d-yerna  ɣur-sen  Weɛmer,  yerna-d  lferḥ  d
Tebda tegnit-a seg  mi yeṭṭef Meqran lkaɣeḍ ad yesɛeddi lɛesker, aseggas
amezwaru  yettceggiɛ-d  tibratin  yuɣal  seg  imiren  yenneqḍaɛ  lexber-is,  yers-d
usenduq  deg  uxxam  ɣillen  d  Meqran  i  yemmuten,  kra  n  yiseggasen  Sekkura
yerra-tt  ulews-is  sɛan-d  Saɛid,  Lmulud  ixeddem  meḥyaf  gar-as  d  Waɛmer,
Sekkura  tesɛedda-d  lemḥayen  yellan  deg  ddunit  maca  tesber,  yuɣal  iban-d
Meqran s tuɣalin-is seg lɛesker, ziɣ ur yemmut ara.
1-5-7-3- Tagnit n taggara
Deg  tullit-agi  «  Tuɣalin  »,  amaru  yemmeslay    ɣef  Meqran  yuɣal-d  ɣer
uxxam-is, ur yemmut ara akken ɣilen imawlan-is.
1-5-8- Tasiwelt
Deg  tullist-agi,  yewwi-d  umaru  tasiwelt  am  tullisin  yezrin  daɣen,  imi  d
netta i d-yettalsen ineḍruyen i d-iḥekkun ɣef yiwudam, ur d asen-yefki ara tagnit
ad ḥkun nutni ɣef yiman-nsen d yiḥulfan-nsen, maca amaru deg tullist-agi daɣen
yella-d d azɣaray imi mačči seg yiwudam n tullist, imi netta d analas kan, yeḥka-
d kan tullist. Deg yimedyeten-d ad iban waya-agi :
89
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
- Akken kan i d-tekker seg wusu, Sekkura terra biha-biha ɣer s aɣalad.
- Saɛid yuẓa ɣer baba-s yettqessir yid-s…
- Yezweǧ Meqran mmi-s ameqqran n Qasi…
- Ma d Sekkura ur tetteg ara meḥyaf gar warraw-is.
- Azekka-nni Meqran yeddem agelzim d telwaḥt yerra ɣer tmeqbert.
1-6- Tulmisin n tullist « Ɛecrin duru »
1-6-1- Tutlayt
Tutlayt  yessemres  umaru  deg  tullist-a  d  tutlayt  tushilt  ara  ad  yefhem  yal
yiwen,  d  tin  ttemaslayen  yemdanen  deg  tudrin  n  Leqbayel,  d  tutlayt  n  yal  ass.
Deg tulist-a ad d-naf amaru yessemres kra n wawalen ijenṭaḍen, inzan, tumnayt
d userwes. Seg uḍris ad nekkes imadyaten iwulmen :
  Asemres n wawalen ijenṭaḍen
-  Awalen  d-yewwi  seg  tutlayt  taɛrabt  :  lmakla,  ddqayeq,  sswayeɛ,  msakit,
-  Awalen  d-yewwi  seg  tutlayt  tafransist  :  lbiru,  asalu,  akarti,  lbista,  abalku,
lmaktub.
ṭṭabla, tabiyirt, lgirra.
1-6-2- Adeg
Ttberna : d adeg uɣur yettruḥu Urezqi akken ad d-isew kra n tbeyirin.
Lezzayer : D tamdint anda yezdeɣ Urezqi d Feṭṭa.
Lbaṭima  : d axxam anda  llan aṭas n wannagen, yezdeɣ  urezqi deg wannag wis
ukuz.
Lbiru : d amkan n uxxedim n Urezqi.
Takuzint : d amkan uɣur tekcem Feṭṭa ad tessebb latay i yemawlan-is.
90
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
Abalku : s yen i-d-tzelli Feṭṭa iman-is, temmut.
Asalu : din nejmaɛen akk imawlan n Feṭṭa d Urezqi qqimen ad tqessiren.
Amkan  uqbel  lbatima-nni  anda  yezdeɣ  Urezqi  :  din  yella  yiwen  ubeḥḍaḥ  ideg
rsen iqudas n waman, yusa-d deg lewhi n uxxam n Urezqi, yeffer deg-s Urezqi
iɛus aqcic-nni yettruḥun yal tikelt s axam-is.
1-6-3- Akud
nekkes seg uḍris :
Ad  d-naf  amaru  Saɛid  Cemmax  yessexdem  aṭas  n  imerna  n  wakkud,  mi  d
yettmeslay  ɣef  yineḍruyen  n  tullist,  aya-agi  ad  t-id  naf  deg  yimedyaten  i  d-
-  Ula ass-a yusa-d uqcic-nni ɣef i ak-id-mmeslayeɣ iḍelli…
-  Azekka-nni, akken yuɣ tannumi, yeffeɣ iruḥ…
-  Tikelt-nni iwala feṭṭa teffeɣ-d s abalku
-  Arzqi yerǧa azal n mraw n ddqayeq, yekker yeḍfer-it.
-  Yemmeɣ ɣer lǧib n lbista yeddem-d tasarut tis snat n tewwurt, tin akken i d-
ihegga iḍen-izeryen.
-  Yal ass d ssekran
-  Azal n ssmana i iɛeddan Arezqi ur yeggan ara ɣer tmeṭṭut-is.
-  Heggi-d imekli i uzekka, ad d-asen imawlan-im.
-  Azekka-nni  mi d-ussan imawlan n  Feṭṭa, yefreḥ yis-sen mačči d kra, am zik
Amaru mi d-yettales ineḍruyen n tullist-a yessemres aglam n yineḍruyen d
neɣ ugar.
1-6-4- Aglam
yiwudam :
1-6-4-1- Aglam n yineḍruyen
-  Yeqqur s ibeddi.
91
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
-  Yebda yettargigi.
-  Feṭṭa tettru tuggi ad tesusem, tebra i tmelḥaft ɣer temurt.
-  Arezqi… a-t-an yekcem am wergaz ihajen.
-  Feṭṭa  akka  i  d  isem  n  teqcict-nni  yuɣ,  ur  teɣri  ara,  ur  tessin  ara  d  acu  i  d
lakul.
1-6-4-2- Aglam n yiwudam
-  Tullas msakit ttɣimant deg uxxam
-  Aqcic am win a d-tekkseḍ seg imi n lmut.
1-6-5- Tadiwennit
1-6-5-1- Tadiwennit gar uɛessas n tewwurt n lbaṭima d urezqi
Aɛesas  :  mselxir ay  Arezqi, ass-agi  yusa-d ɣur-k  yiwen weqcic s axxam,  ur  t-
ssineɣ ara iqder d gma-s n tmeṭṭut-ik.
Arezqi : saḥḥa a Dda Čučan !
Aɛesas  :  mselxir  ay  Arezqi,  ula  d  ass-a  yusa-d  uqecic-nni  i  ak-id-mmeslayeɣ
iḍelli…
Arezqi : Ah ! Ttuɣ ur ak-d-nniɣ ara : d mmi-s uḍeggal-iw maca ur ttessineḍ ara
acku werǧin d-yusa ɣer da, armi d tallit-agi…
Aɛesas : semeḥ-iyi ay Arezqi deg leɛna n tɛebbuṭ-nni i k-id yefkan, ur t-ssineɣ
weqcic-nni d mmi-s udeggal-ik…
1-6-5-2-  Tadiwennit  yellan  gar  Urezqi  d  weqcic-nni  ukud  texdeɛ
tmeṭṭut-is
Arezqi : els iceṭṭiden-ik !
Aqcic yelsa-ten
92
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
Arezqi : awi-d ɛecrin duru…
Aqcic yefka-as-d
Arezqi : tura, nnejli, acu tettraǧuḍ ? Geffel !
1-6-5-3- Tadiwennit gar Urezqi d Feṭṭa
Arezqi : aah ! Tura dayen ! Susem ! Yya-d ɣur-i ! …
Arezqi : serreḥ tura i tmelḥeft-nni swayes tɣumeḍ tafekka-m ! Aha bru-yas ! Ɛni
Feṭṭa truḥ ɣur-s
tessetḥaḍ-iyi ?
Feṭṭa tebra-as
Feṭṭa truḥ ɣer usalu
Γurem ad truḍ…
Arezqi : els iceṭṭiḍen-im ! Ad iyi-d-tafeḍ deg usalu.
Arezqi  :  qqim  !  Rfed  allen-im  muqel-iyi-d,  tiniḍ-iyi-d  d  acu  i  kem  ixussen  ?
Feṭṭa : ulac ! Semmeḥ-iyi ay Arezqi ! Di leɛnaya-k…
Arezqi : xaṭi ! Ini yi-d acu i kem ixussen ? Limer ur kem ixuss wacemma, yili ur
txeddmeḍ ara akka.
Feṭṭa : ulac acu i xussaɣ, di leɛnaya-k semmeḥ-iyi…
Arezqi  :  inaɣ  seg  wasmi  i  kem-uɣeɣ  kra  ur  kem  ixuss…  Tferḥeḍ  mačči  d  kra
ahat di leɛmer-im ur tefriḥed am wasmi i telliḍ yid-i.
1-6-5-4- Tadiwennit yellan gar imawlan n Feṭṭa d Urezqi
Arezqi  :  anwa  seg-wen  ara  yi-d-yinin  ansi  iyi-d-kkant  ɛecrin  duru-agi,  ad  as-
fkeɣ ayen i das-yehwan ?
93
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
Baba-s n Feṭṭa : a ɛcrin duru-nni, iban d tid i yak-d-iqqimen, seg wayen i yak-
yefka baba-k, ad yettwarḥem, asmi yedder…
Gma-s ameqqran : Ihi ! Iban tufiḍ-tent asmi telliḍ meẓẓiyeḍ, teffreḍ-tent armi d
Yemma-s : a mmi ɛzizen, ihi ɛecrin duru-nni d tid ak-id-yeqqimen seg wayen i
yak-d-teǧǧa  yemma-k  ɛzizen  uqbel  ad  tsahl  s  anda  akken  ara  naweḍ,  ad
Gma-s  wis  sin  :  dayen  isehhlen  ihi,  ɛecrin  duru-nni  d  tid  i  ak-id  yeqqimen  si
lexlas amezwaru i d-teṭṭfeḍ, teffreḍ-tent acku d ayen i d-tḥellad s tidi n iɣallen-
Arezqi : xaṭi
tura…
Arezqi : xaṭi.
tettwarḥem…
Arezqi : xaṭi.
ik.
Arezqi : xaṭi.
1-6-6- Iwudam
Iwudam i ɣef tebna tullist-a d wigi :
1-6-6-1- Iwudam igejdanen
Arezqi  :  D  awadem  agejdan  i  iselḥan  ineḍruyen  n  tullist,  d  win  idemɛen  ad  d-
yawi  tameṭṭut  ur  yeɣrin ara ad  thenni  iman-is deg  uxxam  ur tt-xedɛit ara, acku
netta  ɣer  ɣur-s  tillawin  yeɣran  d  tixadaɛin,  deg  taggara  d  tameṭṭut-nni  ur  neɣri
ara i t-ixedɛen.
Feṭṭa : d tin yextar Urezki seg teqcicin n taddart, yexdem deg lbal-is dakken t-id
yellan deg  Lezayyer anda  yezdeɣ, d  yir tiqcicin,  maca deg taggara  ur  yewwi-ḍ
ara ɣer yiswi-is, txadeɛ-it, terna tenɣa iman-is.
94
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
1-6-6-2- Iwudam inaddayen
Ilemẓi : yezdeɣ deg lbaṭima iqublen s axxam n urezqi, yal tikelt mi ara d-yeffeɣ
Urezqi s axedim, netta yettas-d ɣer feṭṭa zehhun akken.
Aɛessas  n  tewwurt  n  lbaṭima  :  d  win  d-yewwin  lexber  i  Urezqi  dakken  yella
yiwen yettas-d ɣer wexxam-is.
Imawlan n Feṭṭa : baba-s, yemma-s, gma-s ameqqran, gma-s wis sin, iɛarḍ-iten-
id Urezqi ɣer imekli.
1-6-7- Tigawin
Tigawin d ineḍruyen iɣef tettwabna tullist, tullist « Ɛecrin duru » tebna ɣef
kraḍ n tegnatin am yal tullist taqbaylit :
1-6-7-1- Tagnit n tazwara
Arezqi  izweǧ-d  seg  taddart  d  Feṭṭa  imi  ur  teɣri,  ur  tessin  aɣerbaz,  acku
akken yenwa netta tid ur neɣri xḍan-t i tcemmatin, yesɛa yir tamuɣli ɣer t-id kan
yeɣran.
1-6-7-2- Tagnit n tigawin
yekcim.
1-6-7-3- Tagnit n taggara
Tebda tagnit-a mi yenna uɛessas n lbaṭima i Urezqi dakken yettas-d yiwen
ilemẓi ɣer wexxam-is, yuɣal iɛuss tameṭṭut-is yeṭṭef-itt-id akked yilemẓi-nni deg
wexxam, yuɣal yerra-tt ḥala i ssekran deg ttberna, yeffeɣ seg wexxam aṭas ur d
Arezqi iɛreḍ-d imawlan n Feṭṭa yiwen wass ɣer imekli, qqimen ttqessiren
ma d Feṭṭa tegla s terwiḥt-is, tḍegger-d iman-is seg ubalku, temmut.
95
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
1-6-8-Tasiwelt
Deg tullist-agi daɣen amaru ur d-asen-yefki ara i yiwudam littaɛ akken ad
idiren akken bɣan, imi mačči d nutni i d-iḥekkun ɣef yiman-nsen, maca d amaru
i d-yeḥkan fell-asen, d netta i yesselḥan tigawin, rnu amaru maci d awadem deg
tullist-agi, yella-d d azɣaray. Amedya ɣef waya-agi :
- Arezqi ur innum ara ttbernat…
- Arezqi yettali yirekkabin yettxemmim…
- Tebbejneq d imeṭṭi, teɣli ɣer yiḍarren-is, teqqar-as …
- Azekka-nni mi d-usan imawlan n Feṭṭa, yefreḥ yis-sen mačči d kra…
1-7- Tulmisin n tullist « iminig »
1-7-1- tutlayt
Tutlayt yessexdem umaru d tutlayt tushilt ara yefhem yal yiwen, d tutlayt
n yal ass. Fessuset ɣef yal win ara yeɣran tullisin-a, amaru ad t-id naf yessemres
awalen ijenṭaḍen, inzan, tumnayt, d userwes, aya-a akk yerna lecbaḥa i weḍris,
-  Awalen  ijenṭaḍen  n  taɛrabt  :  lexrif,  tefreḥ,  lɛecra,  lḥaǧa,  lewḥuc,  ihuzz,
seg-sen ad d-naf :
  Assemres n wawalen ijenṭaḍen
leḥzen, lehna, tettḥarab, lɛasker.
-  Awalen ijenṭaḍen n tefransist : tamacint.
1-7-2-Adeg
Taddart : d adeg anda i d-dran ineḍruyen n tullist.
Fransa : d tamurt uɣur yunag Meqran.
96
Taxamt n usewi : d adeg uɣur tekcem Wenza akken ad tessew lqahwa i Meqran.
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
1-7-3- Akud
Yal  amaru  mi  ara  yaru  tullist  yessexdam  akud  akken  ad  d-yessebgen  melmi
ḍran-tt tigawin d yineḍruyen n tullist :
Deg  tullist  «  Iminig  »,  ddan-d  aṭas  n  imerna  n  wakkud,  mi  d-yettmeslay
umaru  ɣef  ineḍruyen  i  d-yeḍran  deg-s,  ayen  i  d-yettbegginen  aya-agi  d
imedyaten i d-nekkes seg uḍris :
-  Ahat d tamert tis snat neɣ tis kradet n wass, di taddart ters-d tsusmi…
Azekka tanezzayt ad affgeɣ.
Armi d leɛcra yemslam yid-sen, yeǧǧa-asen talwit.
Ilindi tettaɣ-it tawla ɣef teswiɛt ideg yella, ass-a d urrif i d-yuɣen ul-is.
Acḥal aya ur t-yessakked d ussan neɣ d agguren, ahat nnig.
-  … Gma yeffeɣ arma d iḍ ara d-yass…
1-7-4- Aglam
Amaru deg tullist-a yessemres aglam n yineḍruyen, tɣawsiwin d yiwudam :
1-7-4-1- Aglam n yineḍruyen
-  Di taddart ters-d tsusmi ur tufid zzhir iwumi ara tesleḍ…
-  Yessed ɣef txelalt yellan di lḥiḍ.
-  Teddem-d ula d nettat tejɣem tiqit n lqahwa…
-
Yuli ɣer tmesriffegt yeṭṭef amkan.
1-7-4-2- Aglam n tɣawsiwin
-  Tagnit tellexs seg ugeffur i d-ikkaten.
-  Aneznaz yekkat.
Leqfel a d-yettwalday, tawwurt temerzazeɣ.
Udem yecmumeḥed ɣer-s d taḍsa…
tazeddgant.

Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
-
Tḥuza afus n Meqran acku afus-is yettargagi.
1-7-4-3- Aglam n yiwudam
-  Wazna yuzwaɣ wudem-is…
-  Wazna teqqim ahat tettwehim kan d lxaṭer n wergz-agi…
-  Mqran … iwalaten kan yecmumeḥ d taḍsa… qqimen mmeslayen, ḍsan… Ur
yecliɛ ara ma d Wazna tebda imeṭṭi.
-  Meqran… Yal ass yeḥzen…
-  Meqran… Yettargu, yettargagi, yettlejlij… Taggara yeqqim a yettru, aqerru-
is ger tgecrar-is, ḥala asnecfet i wumi a tesleḍ.
1-7-5- Tadiwennit
1-7-5-1- Tadiwennit yellan gar Wazna d Meqran
Wenza : amek tettiliḍ ihi a Meqran, acḥal aya ur d-tusiḍ, yella kra i k-yuɣen ?
Meqran  :  aql-akem  la  tettwaliḍ  a  wazna,  am  zik  am  tura,  ur  tufiḍ  d  acu  i
ibeddlen…I kemm amek i telliḍ? Anda yella gma-m ?
Wenza : di telwit, gma yeffeɣ arma d iḍ ara d-yas, qqim ad terǧud…
Meqran : ilaq ad ruḥeɣ, ur zmireɣ…
Wenza : xaṭi, ad teqqimeḍ, acḥal aya tura, ur tqessreḍ ara yid-i … rǧu ad ak-id-
sseweɣ lqahwa!
asikel?
Wenza : yenna-yid gma tebɣiḍ ad truḥeḍ ɣer Fransa, d tidet? Melmi ara tinigeḍ?
Meqran  :  d  tidet  ad  ruḥeɣ,  azekka  tanezzayt  ad  affgeɣ,  terna  inig-iw  macci  d
Wenza : d acu ? Ad teffeɣeḍ ur d-tettezziḍ ara ?
Meqran : amek tebɣiḍ ? D acu ara xedmeɣ nniḍen ?
Wenza  :  dɣa  d  tidet  a  Meqran  ad  truḥed  ur  d-tezziḍ,  ad  teǧǧeḍ  akk  wid  i  k-
iḥemmelen, yemma-k d tamɣart?
Meqran : zemreɣ ad ruḥeɣ, ɣas ad tejreḥ tasa-iw, ad aḍneɣ maca yewwi-d fell-i
rrwaḥ…

tidireḍ am kečč am madden, ayen-nniḍen eǧǧ-it i Rebbi.

Meqran : ttwaliɣ tafsut mm ijeǧǧigen d tagrest idumen deg uraǧu n wezɣal.
ur sawḍeɣ ara…

1-7-6- iwudam
1-7-6-1- Iwudam igejdanen
Meqran : d awadem yeselḥan ineḍruyen n tullist, d win yebɣan ad yinnig ɣer
temurt n Fransa akken ad yettu temẓi-is, mi yelḥaq ɣer din ur tt-yefri d rray-is.
1-7-6-2- Iwudam inaddayen
Wazna  : d tin yebɣan ad yeqqim Meqran  ur yettinnig ara ad d-yeǧǧ  yemma-s
Yemma-s  n  Meqran  :  d  tin  d  irebban  Meqqran  almi  yimɣur,  ur  tebɣi  ara  ad
waḥdes.
d-yinnig ɣer Fransa

n tegnatin am yal tullist taqbaylit :
1-7-7-1- Tagnit n tazwara
Fransa.
1-7-7-2- Tagnit n tigawin
Yewwi-d umaru ɣef  Meqran asmi iruḥ s axxam n Wenza, ad t-iwali nettat
d gma-s, d tdiwennit i d-yellan gar-asen, yenna-as-d daɣen dakken ad yunag ɣer
Inig  n  Meqran  ɣer  tmurt  n  Fransa  s  yiswi  n  tatut  n  temẓi-is,  dɣa  mi
yewweḍ ɣer dinna yuɣal ixeddem akken ad yesɛu idrimen, yekka-d akk timdinin
Tigawin d ineḍruyen iɣef tettwabna tullist, tullist « Taninna » tebna ɣef kraḍ

1-7-7-3- Tagnit n taggara
1-7-8- Tasiwelt
bɣan nitni.
Deg waddad-agi aneggaru, amaru ur d-yemmeslay ara ɣef tifrat n wugur n
Meqran, ma yella yessaweḍ yettu temẓi-is, d tebrek i d-yuɣen ussan-is.
Amaru deg tullist-a, yella-d d azɣaray imi ur yetteki ara deg tullist, maca d
netta  i  d-yulsen  ineḍruyen  yerna  yeḥka-d  ɣef  iwudam  akken  yebɣa  netta,  dɣa
iwudam  lḥan  akken  s-yehwa  i  umaru  imi  ur  sen-yefki  ara  tilelli  ad  lḥun  akken
- Meqran iḥulfa i qejjar deg ifasse-is, yerra-tan ɣer ubalṭun-is…
- Mi yewweḍ ɣer tseɣlit n yiwen wexxam yessed ɣef txellalt yellan di lḥiḍ.
- Yessusem ciṭ la tt-yettmuqqul yuɣal ikemmel deg wawal-is…
- Meqran yettmeslay-d ɣef yiman-is s isefra…
1-8-Tulmisin n « Tizqaqin n taddart »
Ad  neɛred  ad  nekkes  tulmisin  i  ɣef  tebna  tullist-a,  ama  dayen  yeɛnan
tutlayt, adeg akud, iwudam, tadiwennit, aglam, tigawin d tsiwelt.
1-8-1- Tutlayt
Tutlayt yessexdem umaru deg tullist-agi d tusridt, d tutlayt n yal ass, yal
amdan yezmer ad tt-yefhem, acku d tutlayt taqbaylit i yessemres di tira-is.
Amaru ihi yessexdem tutlayt fessusen, d tin ssexdamen medden di tudert
n yal ass.
100
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
Tutlayt  di  tullist-agi  tesbeggin-d  dakken  ineḍruyen-is  llan-d  deg  tmetti
Taqbaylit,  imi  ad  d-naf  deg-s  amaru  yessemres  kra  n  wawalen  i  d-yemmalen
aya-agi : tizqaqin n taddart, tajmiɛt, adrum, abrid n tala.
Ihi awalen d wid n teqbaylit, d tutlayt taqbaylit, akken daɣen ad naf amaru
yessemres awalen ijenṭaḍen i d-yekkan ama seg tutlayt tafransist neɣ seg tutlayt
n taɛrabt.
  Asemres n wawalen ijenṭaḍen
-  Awalen d yekkan seg tefransist : tabaturt, lakul, akustim, aṭaksi, luzinat.
-  Awalen i d-yekkan seg taɛrabt : zzman, aɣebbar.
1-8-2- Adeg
Deg tullist-agi « Tizqaqin n taddart », ad d-naf amaru yessexdem awalen i d-
yemmalen adeg anda i ḍerrunt tigawin.
Tizqaqin  n  taddart  :  d  adeg  anda  yal  amdan  iɛedda-d  seg-sent,  yeswa  si  tala-
nsent, dinna i ttɣiman medden, tturaren ilmeẓyen.
Taddart : d adeg anida ttidiren yemdanen, tiwaculin d yedrumen.
Tineṭlin  :  deg-sent  i  llan  wid  yemmuten,  d  tiwwura  yettawin  ɣer  tmeddurt  n
dihen.
Tajmiɛt : d adeg anida ttnejmaɛen wat taddart, deg-s daɣen i yeɛreḍ Yidir tayri,
dinna i yessen tin i izedɣen tirga-s.
Tala  :  d  adeg  anida  d  ttasent  tullas  n  taddart  ad  agment  aman.  D  agi  daɣen  i
yattwali Yidir tin iḥemmel.
Abrid  n  taddart  :  d  adeg  ansi  i  iɛedda  usensi  ɣer  taddart,  akken  ad  awin  tislit.
Timizar : d adeg ansi i iɛedda Qasi n At Waɛban, akken ad yaweḍ zik s axxam,
axater abrid n taddart ɣezzif imi yenneḍ.
101
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
Nnig  webrid  :  ansi  iwala  Mennad  d  Qasi  asensi  mi  iɛedda  s  axxam  n  tin
iḥemmel Qasi.
1-8-3- Akud
ad naf :
taddart.
ara d-tɛeddi ɣer tala.
Amaru  deg  tullist-agi  yessexdem  awalen  d-yemmalen  melmi  ḍran-t  tigawin
Iṭij  qessiḥen  :  d  akud  i  d-yemmalen  melmi  tturaren  ilmeẓyen  deg  tezqaqin  n
Yal tameddit : yemmal-ɣ-d akud melmi yettɛassa Yidir ad iwali tin iḥemmel mi
Amenzu n Yulyu n leḥsab n tefransist : d akud i yemmalen melmi i s yenna Qasi
i yemma-s ad yerzu ɣer-s, ddurt i d-iteddun.
Ass-agi : yemmal-aɣ-d melmi ara teddu tin iḥemmel Qasi d tislit, imiren i iruḥ
ad tt-iwali qbel ad truḥ.
Amaru  deg  tullist-agi,  yessexdem  imerna  n  wakud  mi  d  yettmeslay  ɣef
yineḍruyen-is ad naf: asmi, iseggasen, tura, zik…
1-8-4- Aglam
Amaru yessemres deg tullist-a aglam n yiwudam, tigawin d tɣawsiwin :
1-8-4-1- Aglam n yiwudam
-  Tamɣart terza-tt ddunit.
-  Taqcict tecbeḥ mačči d kra.
-  Yemma tameqqrant.
-  Udem-is yewlelles.
-  Baba-s d amerkanti.

Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
1-8-4-2- Aglam n tigawin
-  D imeẓyanen i d imezwura mzazalen-d ɣer s agni n tezqaqin anda ara uraren
deg yijdi i yitij qessiḥen
-  asmi yella d acawrar ula d netta ixnunes deg uɣebbar i uzal
-
tiɣimit-is di tejmiɛt kan, mi yekfa cceɣl n lexla ad iqesser d yilmezyen.
1-8-4-3- Aglam n tɣawsiwin
-  Tizqaqin n taddart, cfant-d i tmeddurt n wid yellan ɣer-sent
-  Tabaturt tamezwarut ad tettemserɣa am leqdeɛ ujenwi.
-  Tabaturt tuɣwas.
-  Abrid n taddart ɣezzif.
1-8-5- Tadiwennit
Tadiwennit deg tullist-agi « tizqaqin n taddart » ur telli ara s waṭas, ad naf tin
kan yellan gar Qasi d Mennad :
Qasi : Amek telliḍ ?
Mennad : aqel-iyi di lxir d lehna.
Qasi : Ahh ! D acu akka i k-yuɣen ?
Mennad : ulac !
dyemlal yid-s deg webrid-is ɣer wexxam.
1-8-6- Iwudam
103
Ihi deg tullist-agi ulac aṭas n tdiwennit ḥala tin yellan gar Qasi d Mennad, mi
Yal tullist tesɛa iwudam ama d igejdanen neɣ d inaddayen, i ɣef ḍrant tigawin.
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
1-8-6-1- Iwudam igejdanen
Yidir : d awudem agejdan deg tullist-agi « tizqaqin n taddart », deg-s yewwi-d
umaru ɣef amek i d-yesɛadda temẓi-is di taddart. D win ur neɣri ara yak, dɣa ur
iḥemmel ara wid yeɣran, tiɣimit-is kan deg tejmiɛt anda i yeɛreḍ tayri.
Qasi  n  At  Waɛban  :  ula  d  netta  d  awudem  agejdan  deg  tullist-agi,  yella  d
ameddakel n Yidir, ayen i yas-yeḍran i netta ula d Yidir yesɛadda-t-id, imi i sin
yid-sen tid ḥemmlen jewǧent d wiyiḍ.
1-8-6-2- Iwudam inaddayen
Ilemẓi  yelsan  akustim  :  d  win  yuɣen  taqcict  i  iḥemmel  Qasi.  D  win  yellan  d
amerkanti imi baba-s yesɛa acḥal d luzin acḥal d lbilla…
Mennad  :  d  ameddakel  n  Qasi  n  At  Waɛban,  d  netta  id  as-d-yewwin  lexber  i
Yidir d akken tin iḥemmel, fkant imawlan-is ad tezweǧ d wayeḍ.
1-8-7- Tigawin
Tigawin  d  ineḍruyen  iɣef  tettwabna  tullist,  tullist  «  Tizqaqqin  n  taddart  »
tebna ɣef kraḍ n tegnatin am yal tullist taqbaylit :
1-8-7-1- Tagnit n tazwara
Deg tegnit  n tazwara, amaru  yewwi-d tamuɣli ɣef Yidir dakken  yettɣimi
deg  tejmiɛt  kan,  dinna  i  yeɛreḍ  tayri  i  tikelt  tamezwarut  anda  yettwali  tullas
tɛeddint ɣer tala, isɛedda ussan-is deg talwit deg tirga anda tt-yettani am akken
yerra yid-s axxam.
1-8-7-2- Tagnit n tigawin
Ameddakel  n  Yidir,  Qasi  n  At  Weɛban  mi  d-yuɣal  s  axxam  yemlal-d
Mennad anda is-d-yessaweḍ lexber dakken tin iḥemmel ass-nni ad teddu d tislit,
104
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
ula  d  yidir  akken  i  d-as-teḍra,  imi  tirga-is  ur  kemmlent  ara,  tin  iḥemmel  fkant
imawlan-is ad tezweǧ daɣen.
1-8-7-3- Tagnit n tagara
Imi tin iḥemmel Yidir fkant imawlan-is ad tezweǧ, ula d netta zewǧen-as
wexxam-nsen, yufa-d iman-is ḥala netta i d-yeqqimen deg tezqaqin n taddart yal
yiwen s anda yerra, yal yiwen anda yewweḍ.
1-8-8 Tasiwelt
Tasiwelt  deg  tullist-agi,  ur  txulef  ara  ɣef  tullisin  yezrin  imi  amaru  deg-s
yusa-d d azɣray, ur yelli ara seg yiwudam n tullist, ɣas akken d netta i d-yeḥkan
inedruyen  n  tullist-a,  d  netta  i  d-yettalsen  ɣef  yiwudam  d  wayen  isen-yeḍran,
- Yidir yessikid deg-sen yemmekti-d temẓi-s…
-  Tiɣimit-is  di  tejmiɛt  kan,  mi  d-yekfa  ccɣel  n  lexla  ad  d-yas  ad  iqesser  d
- Yidir ladɣa ue iḥemmel ara wid yeɣran.
1-9- Tulmisin n tullist « Ih ! Lukan ad teẓreḍ! »
Ad neɛred ad nefk tulmisin i ɣef tebna tullist « Ih ! Lukan ad teẓreḍ! », ama
dayen  yeɛnan  tutlayt,  adeg,  akkud,  iwudam,  tadiwennit,  aglam,  tigawin,  d
amedya :
yelmezyen.
tsiwelt.
1-9-1- Tutlayt
Tutlayt  yessexdem  umaru  deg  tullist-agi,  am  nettat  am  tid  yezrin  yakan,
imi d tutlayt tusridt, d tin isehlen.
Tutlayt  d tin  n teqbaylit  n  yal ass, yal amdan  yezmer ad tt-yefhem, acku
tella-d d tusridt ulac deg iɛewwiqen.
105
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt
Amaru,  deg  tullist-agi  am  tid  yezrin  yessexdem  daɣan  kra  n  wawalen
ijenṭaḍen, akken ad ttfehmen  medden  merra, imi awalen  ijenṭaḍen  uɣen amkan
deg tutlayt-nneɣ.
  Asemres n wawalen ijenṭaḍen
-  Awalen d yekkan seg Tefransist : lbak, abalku,  sbitar.
-  Awalen d yekkan seg Taɛrabt : ṭṭlam,  lbaṭel,    ṭtabla.
  Asemres n wawalen imaynuten
-  Tasdawit, Akayad, tamdint.
1-9-2- Adeg
Tasdawit n Bab Zwar : d adeg anida yemyussan unalas d Mennad, imi d yettas
ɣer tesdawit akken ad iɣer tamaziɣt.
Axxam  anda  yeqqar  Mennad,  akken  ad  iɛawed  i  lbak,  acku  ur  t-id-yewwi  ara
Taddart ddaw idurar n Ǧerǧer : d adeg anda i d-kkren imawlan n Mennad, akked
Lyssi : d adeg anda Mennad yessen Jeǧǧiga.
abrid amezwaru.
anda yenṭel jeddi-s.
1-9-3- Akud
n gma-s.
Tanekra n Tuber : asmi tekker gar izzayriyen, dɣa yal yiwen seg-sen iɣelli s ufus
21 iseggasen : asmi yessen Mennad tamurt i deg d-kkren imawlan-is, d lejdud-is.
Yuɣal yal ma ad yesɛu lweqt ad iruḥ ɣer dinna.
Ass n ssebt : d ass i deg yenɣa lɛesker Jeǧǧiga, mi teqqim deg ubalku dɣa nɣant.
Amaru  yessemres  daɣen  imerna  n  wakud,  seg-sen  ad  naf:  ass-nni,  tameddit,
asmi…

Aḥric wis sin                                                                                          Tasleḍt

-
Iteddu ad izer imesdurar.

1-9-6- Iwudam
1-9-6-1- Iwudam igejdanen

am yal tullist taqbaylit :
1-9-7-1- Tagnit n tazwar
Tigawin d ineḍruyen iɣef tettwabna tullist, tullist-a tebna ɣef kraḍ n tegnatin
Amaru  deg  tegnit  tamezwarut  n  tullist-agi,  yefka-d  tamuɣli  ɣef  tudert  n
Mennad akked tin iḥemmel. D wamek sɛeddan ussan-nsen deg talwit d leḥmala,
akked usirem-nsen ad ɣren deg tesdawit d lwaḥid.
1-9-7-2- Tagnit n tigawin
Yella-d  deg  lmut  n  Jeǧǧiga  d  wamek  itt-nɣan  lɛesker,  d  leḥzen  akked
tebrek i d-yuɣen ussan n Mennad d usirem-is i iruḥen, imi temmut tin iḥemmel
dayen ur d-tettuɣal.
