Ixef wis sin
tasleḍt n tullisin
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                         Tasleḍt
Deg yixef wis sin n tesleḍt, ad neɛreḍ ad nexdem tasleḍt tasentalant i yal
tullist  seg  tullisin  «  Ger  zik  d  tura  »,  ad  nekkes  asentel  agejdan  d  yisental
inaddayen n yal yiwet, d limarat n usentel.
2- Tasleḍt tasentalant n tullisin
« Ger zik d tura » d ammud n tullisin i yura Saɛid Cemmax, ad neɛred ad
nekkes isental igejdanen d yisental inaddayen n yal yiwet.
2-1- Tasleḍt n tullist « Taninna »
Ad neɛreḍ ad nekkes asental agejdan i ɣef tebna tullist Taninna, d yisental
inaddayen, syin akkin ad nefk limarat n usentel.
2-1-1  Asentel agejdan: Tudert n tlemẓit taqbaylit
Asentel i d-yufraren deg tullist-a « Taninna » d asentel n tudert n tlemẓit
taqbaylit.
Di tullist-a yemmeslay-d umaru ɣef tudert n Taninna, seg mi tekcem tasda
wit  armi  tezweǧ,  yemmeslay-d  akk  ɣef  wuguren  d-temlal  tlemẓit  taqbaylit.
Taninna,  ad  tt-naf  truḥ  ad  d-tɣer  deg  tesdawit  n  Bab  Zwar,  ugur  amenzu  i  d-
temlal din d ugur n tmetti, imi d-yusa yiwen ilemẓi yeṭṭeyiḥ-as. Ugur wis sin d
tayri-s  ur  yelḥiqen  ara  ɣer  wayen  yellan  s  tidet,  yemmeslay-d  umaru  akk  ɣef
wayen d-tɛac, ama d ayen yelhan, ama d ayen n diri (am wuguren d temlal). Win
tḥemmel tayri-is ur telli ara zeddiget am tayri-is nettat. Ma yella d ayen yelhan d
agerdas i d-tewwi seg tesdawit d tdukli i d-yellan gar-as d tmeddakelt-is Wrida
tin itt-iɛawnen, tessebgen-as-d belli Basel ur yeṣfi ara. Melba ma nettu zzwaǧ-is
d Ḥend yerna tesɛa aqcic.
Akken i nwala asentel-a agejdan « Tudert n tlemẓit » ijmeɛ-d akk isental
inaddayen i d-yeddan deg tullist ɣef waya yessefk fell-aneɣ ad nessegzi s telqay
yal  asentel  anaday  i  yiman-is  acku  d  wid  d-yefrurin  seg  usentel  agejdan,  ɣef
waya ur d nekkis ara limarat n usentel.
111
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                         Tasleḍt
2-1-2- Isental inaddayen d limarat n usentel (le motif )
Ad  neɛreḍ  ad  nefk  akk  isental  inaddayen  d  limarat-nsen  i  ɣef  d-tewwi
tullist Taninna :
2-1-2-1- Aɛewwiq n tmetti
Taninna  twala  dakken  timetti  anda  d-tekker  deg-s  laman,  nettat  deg
taddart i d-trebba, ulac arrac ileḥun zelmeḍ yefus, ttaken azal d leqder i teqcict
ara d-iɛeddin sdat-nsen.
Ayen i d-yeskanen Aɛewwiq n tmetti i d-temlal Tninna deg uḍris :
Imiren,  teḥbes-d  yiwet  n  tkerrust  ɣer  tama-nneɣ,  llan  deg-s  kraḍ  n  warrac,
alemmas deg-sen yessufeɣ-d aqerru-is si ṭṭaq inṭeq ɣer teqcict yenna-as: Yya-d
ad tedduḍ yid-i am sserwuɣ ayen tebɣiḍ… aha lḥu !
Aqcic yeṭeyyiḥ, imeddukal-is ttaḍsan, netta simi irennu…
2-1-2-2 Tayri
Tayri d assaɣ  i  ijemɛen  gar sin wulawen,  d aḥulfu  yezdin  gar  yemdanen
tezmer ad tili gar ubabat d mmi-s akken tezmer ad tili gar tyemmat d warraw-is
daɣen gar leḥbab d yimeddukal.
Ihi  aṭas  n  yimyura  i  d-yefkan  tamuɣli-nsen  ɣef  usentel  n  tayri  gar-asen:
Camille Lacoste-Dujardin, Yucef Nacib, Muhemed Djellaoui, Robert …
Ma  nemmaslay-d  ɣef  tayri  deg  tmetti  taqbaylit,  anda  zwaǧ  yettili-d  d
tamsalt n twacult, ulac akk amkan i yiḥulfan n umdan, tayri gar teqcict d weqcic
tettuneḥsab  d  lɛib  imi  tezmer  ad  d-tawi  ayen  n  diri  i  twacult  (d  lḥecuma)  ḥaca
tayri yellan gar lwaldin d watmaten.1 (Camille Lacoste-Dujardin, 2005 : 34)
Di tmetti taqbaylit nezmer daɣen ad d-naf tayri yezdin gar urgaz d tmeṭṭut
ur tessaweḍ ara ɣer yiswi, di tewsit-a n tayri, d temeṭṭut kan ad d-yemlalen kra n

Aḥric wis sin                                                                                         Tasleḍt
wugguren  di  tmetti,  ad  tuɣal  ad  tettwali  deg-s  s  yir  tamuɣli  ɣef  taluft-a  ad  naf
Yucef  Nacib (1994 : 80) yefka-d tamuɣli-s anda i d-yenna dakken aḥulfu n tayri
ur ilaq ara ad iban deg tmetti, ma yella tban-d ad teglu s waṭas n lmaḍerra ladɣa
tameṭṭut ama si tama n ubabat neɣ n twacult neɣ n taddart-is. 1
Deg tullist « Taninna » tayri iɣef d-yewwi umaru d tayri yellan gar tlemẓit
taqbaylit  d  umeddakel-is  Basel,  akken  nezra  Basel  d  aselmad  n  umezruy,  ɣef
annect-a  i  texdem  deg-s  Tninna  laman,  imi  d  aselmad  d  win  yesselmaden
imdanen  ɣef  ayen  yelhan,  ur  tettcukuḍ  ara  deg-s  lexdeɛ,  imi  Basel-a  macci
akken  i  t-tenwa  Tninna  i  yella,  d  win  itt-ixedɛen  d  yiwet  n  teqcict  isem-is
Litisya. Γef aya ad d-nini tayri n Basel d Tninna ur tessaweḍ ara ɣer yiswi-is.
Deg  usebtar  14  ad  naf  Taninna,  tules-aɣ-d  amek  d  tella  tayri-s  d  Basel,
anect-a iban-d deg tenfaliyin-a :
Asmi i myussaneɣ d Bassel, mmuteɣ si lferḥ.
ur cfiɣ ara amek iyi-yeɛǧeb Basel, neɣ amek i bdiɣ ḥemmleɣ-t armi yessaweḍ ad
yeqqel d netta kan s wayes ttidireɣ, d netta kan i wimi ttidireɣ.
2-1-2-3 Tadukli
Tadukli  ɣer  Robert  (2012 :  2656) : « d  assaɣ  yellan  gar  sin  neɣ  ugar  n
yemdanen neɣ n tɣawsiwin, yettwaḥsben am lebni n ugraw n yigemnawen».2
Ihi  tadukli  nezmer  ad  d-nini  d  ayen  yezdin  sin  neɣ  ugar  n  yemdanen,
tadukli  tezmer  ad  tili  gar  wergaz  d  tmeṭṭut  akken  tezmer  ad  tili  gar  tmeṭṭut  d
tmeṭṭut ad cerken gar-asen aṭas n temsal.
Deg tullist-a asentel-a n tdukli d win yezdin gar Wrida d Tninna, llan-t  d
timeddukal  seg  mi  bdan-t  leqraya  armi  iwḍent  ɣer  tesdawit  yal  yiwet  d  acu  n
tanga* itt-ceggɛen.
Wrida  d  tin  iɛawnen  tameddakelt-is  mi  d-tfaq  dakken  Basel  d  win  i  ixedɛen
Taninna truḥ tewwi-tt akken ad taɛu ayen ixeddem s wallen-is.

Aḥric wis sin                                                                                         Tasleḍt
Deg  usebtar  wis  15  ad  d-naf  amaru  yemmeslay-d  ɣef  Wrida  mi  d-tewwi
Taninna ɣer lqahwa qqimen-t ad ttqesirent, d ayen is-d-tenna Wrida i Tninna i d-
yesbeggenen tadukli yellan gar-asent :
D timeddukal i nella seg asmi nekcem s aɣerbaz, ass-a ur bɣiɣ ara ad am seččeɣ
terẓeg di tlemmast n tiẓet maca d tadukli-nni yekkan gar-aneɣ acḥal d aseggas i
d-yessawlen.
Ur zmireɣ ara ad ffreɣ fell-am acemma seg ayen zriɣ.
Cfiɣ asmi meẓẓiyit, neddukul akken sked tin ur nexdim …
2-1-2-4 Lexdeɛ
Lexdeɛ  yettili-d  mi  ara  d-yexdem  umdan  laman  deg  albeɛd,  dɣa  ad  t-
yeɣḍer,  as-yeffeɣ  i  ubrid.  Llan  kra  n  yimyura  i  d-yefkan  tamuɣli-nsen  ɣef
tɣawsa-agi,  seg-sen  Lacoste-Dujardin  (2005  :  343)  i  d-yessebgenen  dakken
lexdeɛ  yezmer  ad  d-yili  s  usekcem  n  uccengu*  ɣer  taddart,  lexdeɛ-agi  d
tiremgit*  iweɛren  akk  ɣer  yimezdaɣ  n  taddart,  d  leɣlad  iɣef  yettḥasab  usaḍuf*
bla asifses. Win ara ixedɛen sumata neqqen-t s tyita s ukrafaj. Ma win ixedɛen,
yerwel, yettwalɛen alama tenger ddunit, trika-ines ad as-tt-kksen, axxam-is ad t-
sserɣen, ma yella d lexdeɛ ameẓyan, bab-is ad as-anfen, maca tacemat n lexdeɛ
ad teɣmu ijufar-is: Ad as-seṭlen tamart d claɣem-is, ad ixeddem tafellaḥt melba
asgunfu* imezdaɣ n taddart ad ttwalin deg-s, yerna deg-s ad leɛnen. 1
Deg tullist-a d Basel i ixedɛen tameddakelt-is Taninna, ur yeẓri ara  belli
tayri n Tninna d tayri zedigen, ɣas akken timeddukal-is yal tikelt qqaren-as atan
flan tɛeǧǧebeḍ-as, iwalem-ikem, imi Taninna d tin yeṭṭfen di nnif-is, tesɛa yiwen
testeqneɛ yis-s ur teɛlim ara ad as-yeffeɣ i ubrid.

Aḥric wis sin                                                                                         Tasleḍt
Asentel-a  yemmeslay-d  fell-as  umaru  deg  tullist  «  Taninna  »  mi  tebda
Tulsa n wayen twala: zziɣ ɣer texxamt-nni yettilin deffir ukuntwar, walaɣ Basel
yerba Litisya, yenneḍ-as ifassen-is a tt-yessudun …
2-1-2-5 Ttar
Ttar  d  ayen  yellan  seg  zik,  ɣer  yegduden  merra,  yal  tikkelt  mi  ara  asen-
yexdem  walbaɛḍ  ayen  ur  nelhi  ara,  ttnadin  amek  ad  as-d-rren  ttar.  Kamal
Buɛmara  (2010  :  483)  d  yiwen  n  umaru  i  d-yesbadun  awal-a:  «  Ttar  d  azal
anmetti swayes d-yettarra umdan (adrum, taddart, lɛerc…) ayen i as-iruḥen, i as-
yettwakksen, am lḥerma, nnif».
Deg tullist-a ttar d win i d-terra Tninna i Basel, tella tḥemmel-it s nneya,
netta ixdeɛ-itt. Iceggeɛ imawlan-is s axxam ur teqbil-it ara.
Amaru yessebgen-d dakken Taninna d tin yeṭṭfen di lhedra-is tenna-as ala,
terra-d  ttar  akken  iwata  ayen  i  d-yesbegnen  annect-a  d  ayen  i  d-yusan  deg
tenfalit-a i d-yura umaru deg uḍris asebter wis 17:
Di leɛnaya-k a Basel, ttu-yi amek akken iyi-tettettuḍ ma tessuḍuneḍ Litisya.
Mi texdem tameɣra n la sutnence yusa-d ɣer din yella-d wawal gar-asen Tenna-
as  dayen  ur  ttuɣal  ara  ad  tezziḍ  ɣur-i.  Icaggeɛ  imawlan-is  s  axxam,  Taninna
Mlalen  irgazen  di  lḥedd  n  Buɣni,  yenna-asen  Lewnis  yelli-s  tugi  ad  tezweǧ  d
teṭṭef deg wawal-is :
Basel.
2-1-2-6 Nnif
Kamel  bouamara  (2010  :  336),  yefka-d  anamek  i  wawal-a  Nnif:  «  Azal
ideg tella lḥerma, iseɣ, tirrugza, tafeṭazit, lxir deg wul …».
Nnif d awal d-yekkan seg tutlayt taɛrabt, yekkad sef wawal inzer… awal
nnif sexdamen-t Leqbayel iwakken ad d-inin leḥaja yesɛan azal meqqren, d tayri
tezedyant n umdan, d netta i d-ssaḥ, s nnif i yettzuxu, iyi-s id sebganen lherma-
115
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                         Tasleḍt
nsen,  win  ara  yesɛun  nnif  d  win  yeṭṭfen  deg  lḥerma-is,  ad  yesɛu  leqder.  1  (
Camille lacouste-Dujardin, 2005 : 261)
Nnif deg tullist-a yusa-d s wudem arusrid nefhem-it-id seg kra n tigawin
yexdem Lewnis mi yesla dakken Basel yesqaṭeɛ i yelli-s deg ubrid yeqqar-as yir
lehdur.  Lewnis  d  anifi  yekker-d  ad  yesseɣli  lbaṭel  izaden  akken  ad  d-yesasi
lḥerma d tlelli i yebɣa Basel ad yesruḥ.
Deg usebtar wis 19 amaru yemmeslay-d ɣef nnif, aya-agi d ayen i d-yusan
u wudem arusrid  imi  nefhem-it-id s tɣuri-nneɣ  i weḍris:  Lewnis  yesla  i wayen
yeḍran d yelli-s, yewwi-t-id nnif iruḥ s axxam n Basel yenna-as i baba-s : Sufeɣ-
d  akka  izem-agi  i  tesɛiḍ  bla  ddin  n  Rebbi,  ara  d-ddmeɣ  leɛmer-is!  afuḥan!  ad
yettnekker ad ireggem yessi-s n yergazen.
2-1-2-7 Imrabḍen
Imrabḍen  d  wid  i  yesɛan  assaɣ  d  ddin,  usan-d  ɣer  tmurt  n  leqbayel  deg
tasut  tis  16  seg  ssaqiya  alḥemra  di  Lmaruk.  Tadra-nsen  d  aɛraben,  akken  d
qqaren  d  aɛraben  qqersen-d  seg  nnbi.  Sumata  xeddmen  d  lecyax  n  lǧameɛ,
bennun  timɛemrin  (d  tiwuriwin  isɛan  assaɣ  d  tesreḍt)2.  (  Camille  Lacoste-
Dujardin, 2005 : 227)
Imrabḍen  d  imdanen  yettidiren  iman-nsen,  tilawin-nsen  ḥeǧǧebent,  ur
xedment ara deg berra mgal tlawin n leqbayel. Ttwalin ima-nsen d nutni i yesɛan
azal  ɣef  wiyiḍ,  dɣa  ur  seɛɛun  ara  akk  assaɣ  ɣer  yemdanen-nniḍen,  adeg  anida
ttidiren  ttsemmin-as  imrabḍen,  d  nitni  i  d  imezwura  i  d-ixedmen  Zzawiya,
xeddmen-tt berra n taddart anida sselmaden ddin, qqaren-d dakken sɛan leɛnaya
imi sseḥluyen imuḍan.( Camille Lacoste-Dujardin, 2005 : 228)

Aḥric wis sin                                                                                         Tasleḍt
Imrabḍen uɣen amkan meqqren deg temnaḍt n Leqbayel, akken ad jebden
imdanen-nniḍen ɣer tama-nsen qqaren-asen nekkni d imawlan n tektabt n leqran,
yerna ad ddun yid-sen mgal acengu-nnsen, irgazen-nsen ssawalen-asen Sidi  ma
d  tilawin-nsen  Lalla,  mxalafen  ɣef  leqbayel  maca  qqaren-d  Leqbayel  d  ayla-
nneɣ, ttabaɛen « Ṭṭariqa Rreḥmaniya», aṭas deg-sen i yettekin deg tnekra-nni  n
1871, seld n tnekra-agi llan kra rewlen ɣer Surya llan wid tenfa Fransa ɣer « La
nouvelle Calédonie», yebda ineqqes urmud-nnsen ̽ seg-mi d tekcem Fransa, wid
yeqqimen  di  tmurt  yerra-ten  umnekcum  d  laminat  n  tuddar,  ma  d  win  i  d-
yeqqaren dakken d nitni i yesɛan azal i izewaren rran iman-nsen ɣer uselmed n
ddin. (Camille Lacoste-Dujardin, 2005 : 228)
Ihi deg tullist-a Taninna, amaru yemmeslay-d ɣef imrabḍen, yesbeggen-d
dakken  ur  ttemsefhamen  ara  d  Leqbayel,  deg  tullist-a  imawlan  n  Basel  d
imrabḍen, ma d imawlan n Tninna d Leqbayel, Taninna tegguma ad teqbel Basel
acku ixdeɛ-it, imi baba-s n Basel ur yeẓri ara s wannect-a, yebda yettɛayar deg
Leqbayel  dakken  d  tilawin  i  yettḍebbiren  fell-asen,  yerna  ameddakel  n  Basel,
yenna-asen-d belli nutni ur ttnasaben ara Leqbayel.
Limarat n usentel-a d tid d yeddan deg usebter wis 19-20- 21 :  awwah  !
Kenwi s  Leqbayel truḥem deg-sent, d tilawin a yettḍebbiren fell-awen…
Taqbaylit jami ad tekcem s ixxamen-nneɣ, d imrabḍen i nella…
2-1-2-8 Tira s tmaziɣt
Amaru  deg  taggara  n  tullist  yesseda-d  tabrat  id  as-d-tura  Tninna,  iswi-is
deg  waya  ad  d-yessebgen  dakken  mačči  ala  win  yeɣran  tamaziɣt  ara  tt-yarun,
Taninna  tella  d  taselmadt  n  tusnakt  tuɣal  ɣer  tmaziɣt  acku  d  tin  yebɣan  ad
texdem ɣef tutlayt-is.
Deg  usteqsi  i  nefka  i  umaru  deg  tririt-is  nufa-d  yettwali  ilaq  tira  deg
tmaziɣt  ad  tenarni1,  abeɛda  di  tallit  n  80,  seg  wayen  nefhem  seg  tebrat  is-tura
1  Uɣal ɣer usebter 220.
117
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                         Tasleḍt
Tninna  i  umaru  tenna-as  10  iseggasen-a  imi  nemyussan,  tabrat  tura-as-tt  deg
useggas n 1998 acku tenna-as aggur-nni iɛeddan i nɣan Meɛtub.
Ayen  d-yeskanen  aya-a  deg  tebrat  dakken  Taninna  tettaru  s  tutlayt
tamaziɣt: di lakul, beddleɣ acu i sɣarayeɣ : ǧǧiɣ tusnakt uɣaleɣ ɣer tmaziɣt.
2-2  Tasleḍt n tullist « laman d leɣder »
Ad neɛreḍ ad nekkes asentel agejdan i ɣef tebna tullist « laman d leɣder»
d yisental inaddayen, syin akkin ad nefk limarat n usentel.
2-2-1 Asentel agejdan d limarat n usentel : ttar
Ttar deg tullist-a « Laman d leɣder » d win i d-yerra Uwejhan deg Ujendi
i yesxedmen Wezna tenɣa argaz-is, aya-agi akk sseba-is d taferka n uzemmur i
yebɣa Ujendi ad d-yawi, maca mi t-yerbeḥ uwejhan deg ccreɛ, dɣa tella-d ceḥna
gar-as d Meqran (mmi-s Uwejhan).
Ihi  Awejhan  ula  d  netta  yufa-d  tifrat  amek  ara  yenɣ  Ajendi,  yessexdem
Ḥnini  n  Muḥ  u  Remḍan,  terra  iman-is  d  taderwict,  tettruḥu  s  axxam  n  Ujendi,
tettawi-d  isallen  i  Uwejhan,  yiwet  n  tikelt  tezra  dakken  Ajendi  ad  d-yinig
tasebḥit, tenna-as i Uwejhan, iruḥ tasebḥit iɛus-it deg ubrid, yenɣa-t. Yerra-d ttar
n mmi-s i iruḥen mebla tuɣalin.
Deg  usebter  37  amaru  yesbeggen-d  dakken  Awejhan  yerra-d  ttar  deg
Ujendi  i  yenɣan  mmi-s,  deg  tenfalit-a  :  yewweḍ-d  wass-nni  n  yinig  n  ujendi,
kkreɣ deg yiḍ ruḥeɣ zwareɣ s abrid n tniri… jebdeɣ di zznad snat n tikkal yeɣli…
2-2-2- Isental inaddayen d limarat n usentel
Ad  neɛreḍ  ad  nefk  akk  isental  inaddayen  d  limarat-nsen  i  ɣef  d-tewwi
tullist-a :
118
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                         Tasleḍt
2-2-2-1- Aḥewwes
Aḥewwes  d  awal  d-yekkan  seg  umeyag  ḥwes,  kamal  Buɛmara  (2010  :
204)  d  win  d-yefkan  anamek  n  ḥwes  :  «  Jelqem,  ddem,  aker,  kkes-as  kra  s
lemɣawla».
Yemmaslay-d  umaru  deg  tullist-a  srid  ɣef  Ujendi  i  yebɣan  ad  iḥawes
yiwet  n  tferka  n  uzemmur  n  Uwejhan.  Mi  yeẓra  belli  Awejhan  d  mmi-s  ruḥen
ɣer lgirra dɣa yebɣa ad yeḥqer mmi-s amaẓuẓ, ihi d Ajendi i yezwaren s axxam
n ccreɛ akken ad yerbeḥ netta taferka-nni.
Deg usebtar wis 24 amaru yemmeslay-d ɣef ttar mi d-yenna :
Tikelt-agi  Ajendi  yebɣa  deg  uzal  qayli  ad  yeḥwes  yiwet  n  tferka  n  uzemmur  n
Uwejhan. Ajendi iruḥ ɣer tribunal n Draɛ Lmizan, yessufeɣ-as-d lkarṭa i Yidir.
2-2-2-2- Tiririt n tferka
Akken nezra Ajendi macci d taferka-is, yerna yezwar ɣer wexxam n Ccreɛ
maca mi d-yuɣal Uwejhan seg lgirra, yufa-d mmi-s yeḥsel dɣa iruḥ srid s axxam
n Ccreɛ, yerra-d taferka-is i yebɣa ad yawi Ujendi.
Ayen d- yeskanen anect-a deg tullist:
Ladɣa d Awejhan i ibedden ɣer s axxam n Ccreɛ n Draɛ Lmizan, yewwi-
yas akk ttbut ɣef wakal…
2-2-2-3- Akellex
akken ad d-tenɣ argaz-is.
Wazna:
Deg tullist-a d Awejhan i iɣurren Wezna, tella-d gar-as d Meqran cceḥna
ɣef ccreɛ dɣa yebɣa ad d-yekkes aqerru-is, yufa-d Wezna d lḥila ara yessexdem
Deg  usebtar  wis  27  amaru  yuder-d  tikerkas  s  wacu  yettkellix  Ujendi  i
Si tikelt ɣer tayeḍ ad as-d-yawi ayelluc swayes ssedhuyen arrac, tikelt d tazrart,
tikkelt tayeḍ d taqerɛet n rriḥa, abrid-nniḍen d ameqyas.
ɣas  sferḥ  iman-im  si  tura,  tameddit-agi  ad  twaliḍ  Taseɛdit  teffeɣ  axxam-iw  i
lebda, d kem a t-izedɣen, d kem ukud a sɛuɣ arraw-iw…
119
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                         Tasleḍt
tameddit, taddart akk tnezzeh-d ɣer umennuɣ gar Ujendi d tmeṭṭut-is.
2-2-2-4- Leɣder
Deg tullist-a Wezna  texdeɛ argaz-is  yellan  yexdem  deg-s  laman,  tedda  d
uberrani,  tefka  afus  ɣef  urgaz-is,  tenɣa-t  mebla  ma  tfaq  i  yiman-is,  lehdur  n
Ujendi qqimen-t deg wallaɣ-is armi tegla s wergaz-is.
Deg usebtar wis 29 amaru yessebgen-d dakken Wezna teɣder argaz-is:
Tegga-yas acečči i Aɛmer, yiweḍ s azaɣer ad yekrez, yemmut ɣef lmaɛun…
2-2-2-5- Laman
Laman d tagnit i deg ulac lekdeb, lexdeɛ, tagdi…
Deg tullist-a laman d Meqran i t-ixedmen deg tmeṭṭut-is meɛna nettat ur s-tefki
ara azal i laman n wergaz-is, tumen aberrani i tt-yewwin ɣer yir abrid.
Ma nuɣal ɣer limarat n usentel, ad d-naf amaru yemmeslay-d ɣef laman s
wudem  arusrid,  Aɛmer  d  win  i  ixedmen  laman  di  tmeṭṭut-is,  yexter-itt  d  nettat
ukkud ad  yecrek ddunit-is, ama deg  lferḥ  neɣ di  lqerḥ. Yettaǧǧa-tt tettruḥu ɣer
tala weḥd-s, yenwa ur tt-xeddeɛi-t ara, deg uxxam mi tbeddel ṭbiɛa yid-s Aɛmer
meskin  d  nneya  yenwa  si  ɛeggu  n  ccɣel  n  wexxam  i  txeddem  akken  imi  tuɣ
tameṭṭut tezṛa d acu tebɣa.
3-2- Tasleḍt n tullist n « Tadyant n mmi-s uciban »
Ad neɛreḍ ad nekkes asentel agejdan i ɣef tebna tullist « Tadyant n mmi-s
uciban », d yisental inaddayen, syin akkin ad nefk limarat n usentel.
2-3-1 Asentel agejdan d limarat n usentel: Ttrebga n ddunit
Amaru  deg  tullist-a  tadyant  n  mmi-s  Uciban  yebɣa  ad  yessebgen  belli
ddunit tettrebbi, mačči d tayemmat neɣ d ababat kan i izemren ad irebbi mmi-s,
timsirin i d-yettemlili wemdan deg tudert-is n yal ass.
Ihi  deg  tullist-a  tadyant  n  mmi-s  Uciban,  Mezyan  iruḥ-d  ɣur-s  yiwen
akken ad as-yenɣ axsim-is. Mezyan yeḥka-as i baba-s imiren baba-s yessufeɣ-it
ɣer wezniq, akken ad iẓer timsirin i d-tettak ddunit i yemdanen.
120
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                         Tasleḍt
Aciban lamer yewwet mmi-s ahat ad as-yeffeɣ akk i webrid imi netta yemla-as d
acu n wazal yesɛa wemdan, ma yenɣa-t amek ad tuɣal tmuɣli n tmetti ama ɣur-s
neɣ ɣer imawlan-is.
Ttrebga n ddunit deg tullist-a yemmeslay-d umaru fell-as s wudem arusrid
nefhem-itt-id  seg  tigawin  yexdem  Mezyan,  d  anusu-nni  yettnusu  deg  yiḍ  deg
berra akken ad iẓer ma ur yenɣi walbeɛd s anda is-yehwa ad iruḥ, ur t-yettaɣ kra,
meɛna win ara yenɣen tamgerṭ, ad qqimen ad tnadin fell-as alamma nɣan-t neɣ
ahat ad rren ttar deg imawlan-is. Ayen i d-yeskanen annect-a deg tullist:
Azekka-nni, Mezyan yega akken is yenna baba-s, yensa di tejmaɛt.
Yenna-as baba-s:
A mmi yella kra ik-id-yeḍran iḍenizeryen neɣ xaṭi?
Yenna-as Mezyan:
Xaṭi a baba, acemma ur d-yeḍri.
Ihi deg tullist-a, Aciban yal tikkelt mi ara ad yass mmi-s ad yečč imensi,
yesteqsay-it almi d tikelt  taneggarut,  yenna-as dakken  lukan tenɣiḍ amdan-nni,
tili lhedra ur tettfaka ara, yerna ussan-is di lḥir ara ten-tesɛediḍ.
2-3-2- Isental inaddayen d limarat n usentel
Ad  neɛreḍ  ad  nefk  akk  isental  inaddayen  d  limarat-nsen  i  ɣef  d-tewwi
tullist-a :
2-3-2-1- Ttar
Argaz-nni  i  d-yusan  deg  yiḍ  ɣer  Meẓyan  yellan  daxel  n  lqahwa-is
yessuter-as ad as-yenɣ axessim-is acku yebɣa ad d-yerr ttar deg-s.
Deg tullist-a asentel n ttar yemmeslay-d fell-as umaru deg usebtar wis 41
s wudem arusrid, mi is-yenna wergaz-nni i Meẓyan :
Mebla ma ntezzi ntenneḍ ad ak-tt-iniɣ d acu-tt, d yiwen i yellan d axṣim-iw, bɣiɣ
Aciwer ɣer kamel bouamara (2010  :  07):  Steqsi ameqqran, win  yessnen,
ad t-kkseɣ si ddunit.
2-3-2-2- Aciwer
win ijerben, uqbel ad tgeḍ kra.
121
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                         Tasleḍt
Deg tullist-a tadyant n mmi-s Uciban d Meẓyan i iciwren baba-s d acu ara
yexdem  mi  d-yusa  ɣur-s  yiwen  n  wergaz,  yessuter-as-d  ad  as-yenɣ  axṣim-is.
Meẓyan iḥar amek ara ad yexdem.
Deg usebtar wis 42 amaru yemmeslay-d ɣef ucaweṛ n Meẓyan, ayen i d-
yeskanen annect-a d ayen is-yenna Meẓyan i baba-s :
A baba! Ass yusa-d yiwen yessewhem-iyi. Yessuter-iyi-d yiwen n cci aqli ḥareɣ
amek ara xedmeɣ…
2-3-2-3- Azal n umdan
Amdan d win yesɛan azal meqqren deg tmetti, yeswa yerna Rebbi ixleq-d
amdan,  yefka-as  azal  meqqren,  isjed-as  lmalakat  yerna  yefka-as  leɛqel  s  ways
ara  imeyyez  lxir  d  ccer,  iḥerrem-d  ayen  ara  iḍurren  amdan.  Ṛebbi  yeḥrem
timenɣiwt  n  wemdan  yerna  yuder-d  deg  tektabt-is  dakken  win  yenɣan  amdan
amzun yenɣa akk imdanen.
Ihi deg tullist-a iban-d wazal n wemdan deg wayen i d-as-yenna wergaz-
nni  i  Meẓyan  dakken  ad  as-yefk  azal  n  wayen  ad  d-iḥer  deg  10  neɣ  15  n
iseggasen, iban-d wazal yesɛa wemdan, lamer ur yesɛi ara wemdan-nni i yebɣa
ad d-ineɣ lqima tili ur yettnadi ara ad d-yefk akk idrimen-is akken ad d-yekkes
aqerru-is.
Deg usebtar 42 amaru  yemmeslay-d ɣef wazal n wemdan s wudem usrid
mi yella Meẓyan ihedder d yiman-is :
Di  leɛmer-is  ur  ixemmem  ɣer  ssuma  n  wemdan,  ass-nni  ixemmem:  ziɣ  d  tidet
imdanen ɣlayit, ma yella yezmer yiwen ad yefk annect-agi n yedrimen…
Iruḥ deg usmuzgem imiren ɣef wazal n wemdan…
2-4-Tasleḍt n tullist « Ad gen tameɣra »
Ad neɛreḍ ad nekkes asentel agejdan i ɣef tebna tullist « Ad gen tameɣra »,
d yisental inaddayen, syin akkin ad nefk limarat n usentel.
122
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                         Tasleḍt
2-4-1- Asentel agejdan d limarat n usentel : azal n tegmat
Kamel buɛmara (2010 : 164)  d yiwen n umaru i d-yefkan tamuɣli-is ɣef
wawal tagmat:« d idamen i icerken atmaten n yiwet n tɛebbuḍ, n yiwen wexxam,
n yiwen n wedrum…atg».
Tagmat deg tullist-a tella gar Akli U Muḥ d watmaten-is i d-irebba, d wid
i ɣef irebba tassa, meɛna azal n tegmat deg tullist-a d win i d-yeglan s wayen n
diri.  Akli  u  Muḥ  yewwi-t-id  nnif  ɣef  watmaten-is  i  yugin  warraw-is  ad  ten-
ɛerḍen  ɣer  tmeɣra-nsen, dɣa  Akli  yekker  yenɣa  iman-is,  isbeggen-aɣ-d dakken
tagmat d tin yesɛan azal meqqren.
Deg usebtar wis 46 d 48, amaru yemmeslay-d ɣef azal n tegmat s wudem
arusrid  deg  usebtar  46  yessebgen-d  dakken  atmaten  n  Wakli  ur  ḥdiren  ara
tameɣra, seg wannect-a i iruḥ Wakli yenɣa iman-is, aya yemmeslay-d fell-as deg
usebtar  wis  48.  Deg  usebter  wis  46  :  yewweḍ-d  wass  n  tmeɣra,  taddart  akk
tegguǧi-d  ɣer  wexxam  n  Wakli…  ḥala  atmaten  n  Wakli,  qqimen  kan
mmuɣebnen…  Deg  usebtar  wis  48  :  ffɣen  warraw-is  d  kra  inebgawen  ttnadin,
ufan-t  iɛelleq  iman-is  s  umrar  ɣer  yiwet  n  teslent  gar  tbucicin  yellan  deffir
wexxam.
2-4-2- Isental inaddayen d limarat n usentel
Ad  neɛreḍ  ad  nefk  akk  isental  inaddayen  d  limarat-nsen  i  ɣef  d-tewwi
tullist-a :
2-4-2-1- Tukksa n leqder
Lemqadra  d  tagnit  anda  amdan  yettak  azal  meqqren  i  wemdan-nniḍen,
maca tuksa-is d azal-nni ara yettwaksen i wemdan.
Arraw  n  Wakli  u  Muḥ  ur  uɣen  ara  rray  i  baba-tsen,  mi  sen-yenna  ad  ɛerḍeɣ
leɛmum-nwen ɣer tmeɣra, kksen fell-as leqder, d awal-nsen i iɛeddan amzun ur
Deg usebtar wis 46 amaru yemmeslay-d ɣef wannect-a s wudem arusrid,
aya ad t-id-naf deg tdiwennit yeḍran gar Wakli d warraw-is, ad naf arraw-is ur s-
sen-yenni kra.
uɣen ara rray.
123
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                         Tasleḍt
Akli: bɣiɣ ad d-necdeɣ atmaten-iw ɣer tmeɣra
Arraw-is: ḥala ta-agi ur d iḍerrun ara, u ma llan di tmeɣra a t-an nekni ḥsu si
tura tili-nneɣ tebṭel…
usebtar wis 46:
Ayen yerḥan Akli s waṭas imi arraw-is kksen fell-as leqder, at taddart akk
rzan-d ɣer tmeɣra ala atmaten-is aya  yusa-d deg tenfalit  yessexdem  umaru deg
Sked win ur d-nerzi ḥala atmaten n Wakli, qqimen kan mmuɣebnen…
2-4-2-2- Timenɣiwt n yiman
Tikwal  imdanen  yettefeɣ-iten  leɛqel,  teggen  tamrart  i  yiman-nnsen  ɣas
akken  zṛan  belli  Rebbi  iḥerrem  ɣef  wemdan  ad  yenɣ  iman-is,  d  Rebbi  i  t-id-
yefkan d netta ara t-yekksen.
Ihi  Akli  iruḥ  ɣer  wayen  yellan  deffir  n  tudert,  yenɣa  iman-is  s  ufus-is,  iɛelleq
iman-is ɣer teslent, sseba n wannect-a d tagmat d leqder ikksen warraw-is fell-a.
Amaru  deg  uḍris,  asebtar  wis  48  yemmeslay-d  ɣef  tmenɣiwt  n  yiman  s
wudem arusrid, ixeber-aɣ-d dakken Akli yemmut deg tenfalit :
Ufan-t  iɛelleq  iman-is  s  umrar  ɣer  yiwet  n  teslent  gar  tbucicin  yellan  deffir  n
wexxam.
2-5 Tasleḍt n tullist « Tuɣalin »
Ad  neɛreḍ  ad  nekkes  asentel  agejdan  i  ɣef  tebna  tullist  «  Tuɣalin  »,  d
yisental inaddayen, syin akkin ad nefk limarat n usentel.
2-5-1 Asentel agejdan d limarat n usentel
Deg junyu 1988 aṭas n imeḥbas i wumi d-serḥen seg lmaruk, llan wid d-
yesɛeddan leḥebs dinna  azal n 150, ṭṭfen-ten seg 1976 deg lmaruk deg Amgalla
lgira n Puli Zaryu, llan wid yesawḍen snen ula d tamaziɣt , tacelḥit deg leḥbas n
Maruk, tuɣalin tettcabi ɣer tina  n Unerri  de belezak,  meɛna  maci d tina,  ufiɣ-d
yiwen seg wid d-yuɣalen.1
1  Uɣal ɣer timerna, adiwenni i texdem Ghoul d saɛid Cemmax.

yiseggasen,  ayen  d-yeskanen  annect-a  dayen  d-yenna  Meqran  i  yimawlan-is  :
tɣilem  mmuteɣ,  imi  14  iseggasen  aya  ur  d-baneɣ  ara,  inaɣ  d  ameḥbus  i  d  iyi-

yisem-is, rẓan asenduq-nni ineḍlen, ufan yeččur d ijdi, d ssil n uneẓruf.
2-5-2- Isental inaddayen d limarat n usentel
Ad  neɛreḍ  ad  nefk  akk  isental  inaddayen  d  limarat-nsen  i  ɣef  d-tewwi

Deg  tmurt  n  leqbayel  zik  mi  ara  yemmet  wergaz,  tameṭṭut-is  ttaran-tt  i
ulews-is  akken  ur  tettuɣal  ara  ɣer  wexxam  n  imawlan-is,  yerna  tesgujul  ara
Deg tullist-a, Sekkura mi ɣillen yemmut wergaz-is dɣa imɣaren-is rran-tt i
ulews-is,  ur  tt-ǧǧin  ara  ad  tuɣal  ɣer  imawlan-is,  ḥetmen  fell-as  tuɣ  alews-is
Amaru deg usebtar wis 51, yemmeslay-d ɣef wannect-a mi d-yenna:
Lḥaǧ  Qasi  d  temɣart-is  juban-tt-id  sya  u  sya,  ḥettmen  ɣef  Sekkura  ad  tt-yerr
Agujil  d  win  ur  nesɛi  baba-s  neɣ  yemma-s  neɣ  ur  ten-iseɛu  ara  deg  sin

2-6- Tasleḍt n tullist « Ɛecrin duru »
Ad neɛreḍ ad nekkes asentel agejdan i ɣef tebna tullist « Ɛecrin duru », d
yisental inaddayen, syin akkin ad nefk limarat n usentel.
2-6-1- Asentel agejdan d limarat n usentel: Lexdeɛ
Feṭṭa d tin i ixedɛen argaz-is, tettaǧǧa-t armi iruḥ ɣer uxeddim, tessekcem-
d  yiwen  n  ilemzi  ɣer  wexxam-is  tzehhu  yid-s  macci  d  tikkelt  neɣ  snat,  armi
icukk  deg-s  uɛessas  n  tewwurt  yesselḥeq  lexber  ɣer  wergaz-is  belli  yettas-d
yiwen  ɣer  wexxam-is  ur  t-yessin  ara,  yessekcem-as  ccek  i  Urezqi,  iɛus-itt  dɣa
yeṭṭef-iten daxel n texxamt n tguni!.
Amaru  ur d-yudir ara awal  n  lexdeɛ s wudem  usrid,  maca  yella wacu d-
yesbegnen  dakken  Feṭṭa  texdeɛ  argaz-is,  texdem  ayen  ur  iqebbel  leɛqel  n
Tikkelt-nni iwala Feṭṭa teffeɣ-d s abalku, iwala-tt tesweɛday ɣer yiwen wexxam
Ciṭ akka iwala ilemẓi-nni yerra ɣer lbaṭima-nni anda yezdeɣ…
Yekcem, yeqqur s ibeddi mi iwala tameṭṭut-is ɛeryan gar ifassen n weqcic-nni …

Aḥric wis sin                                                                                         Tasleḍt
2-6-2-1- Laman
Arezqi  d  win  i  ixedmen  laman  deg  tmeṭṭut-is,  yettruḥu  ɣer  lxedma  seg
sbeḥ alamma d tameddit werǧin icukk deg-s ad t-texdeɛ.
Si  laman  yellan  gar-as  d  tin  yellan  d  tacrikt  n  ddunit-is,  Arezqi  iḥulfa  i
yiman-is seg wid uɣur d yerza lferḥ.
2-6-2-2- Yir tamuɣli n tmetti ɣer teqcict yeɣran
Arezqi  ayen  t-yeǧǧan  ad  yexḍeb  Feṭṭa,  d  yir  tamuɣli  yesɛa  ɣef  teqcict
yeɣran, yejɛel aserwet-a yellan di tallit-a yella kan ɣer teqcicin yeɣran.
Arezqi  deg  tullist-a  yenwa  amzun  leɛyub  yellan  di  tmetti  tazzayrit  d
leqraya  i  ten-id-yeslalen.  Ad  d-naf  amaru  deg  usebter  wis  55  yesbegen-d  yir
tamuɣli n Urezqi ɣer tin yeɣran :
Arezqi yenna-as deg wul-is :
yeɣran…
2-6-2-3- Ssmaḥ
Ad  aɣeɣ  tin  ur  neɣri  ara,  tin  ur  nessin  ara  ticemmatin-agi  i  ssnent  timserrḥin
Feṭṭa  mbeɛd  mi  texdeɛ  argaz-is,  tettḥellil  deg-s  akken  ad  as-yesmeḥ,
tenwa ayen texdem deg-s drus. Γas akken yenna-as semḥeɣ-am meɛna netta ul-is
yerɣa, amek tin deg wayeḍ yexdem laman teɣḍer-as ddunit-is.
Yettban-d usentel n ssmaḥ deg tenfalit-a :
Feṭṭa tebda teṭṭalab deg ad as-yesmeḥ : Tebbejneq d imeṭṭi, teɣli ɣer yiḍarren-is,
Arezqi ur s-yefki ara azal imi tettru, isemmeḥ-as kan nnig wul, ayen d-yeskanen
teqqar-as s usnexfet : Semmeḥ-iyi.
annect-a d ayen is-yenna :
Nekk  a  t-an  semḥeɣ-am,  maca  wissen  kan  allaɣ-im  d  wul-im  ma  ad  am-
semmḥen, kemm i ixedmen ta-agi acemma ur t-tectaqeḍ…

yekkes-d  ɛecrin  duṛu  id  as-d-yefka  weqcic-nni  i  d-yettasen  ɣer  tmeṭṭut-is,

Aḥric wis sin                                                                                         Tasleḍt
yesteqsa-ten  d  anwa  ara  ad  yafen  ansi  is-d-kkant  ɛecrin  duru-nni,  tameṭṭut-is
tenwa ad asen-d-yini dakken texdeɛ-iyi, dɣa Feṭṭa tenɣa iman-is.
Ayen i d-yeskanen dakken Feṭṭa tenɣa iman-is, yettban-d deg tenfalit-agi :

2-7- Tasleḍt n tullist « Iminig »
Ad  neɛreḍ  ad  nekkes  asentel  agejdan  i  ɣef  tebna  tullist  « Iminig »,  d
yisental inaddayen, syin akkin ad nefk limarat n usentel.
2-7-1 Asentel agejdan d limarat n usentel: tatut n temẓi
Asentel agejdan i d-yufraren deg tullist-agi « Iminig », d asentel n tatut n
temẓi.
Tatut n temẓi macci d ayen i isehlen ɣef wemdan ad t-yexdem, acku temẓi
d ayen tɛedda macci d ayen ara d yuɣalen ɣer deffir, ad t-nbeddel wa ad t-nettu,
rnu ɣer waya macci d yiwen wass neɣ sin ara nemḥu, d leɛmer s lekmal-is.
Deg  tullist-a  Iminig,  amaru  yemmeslay-d  ɣef  Meqran  i  yebɣan  ad  yettu
temẓi, dɣa yufa-d tifrat i wugur-agi s trewla ɣer tmurt n Fransa mebla tuɣalin, d
unadi  n  temdini-is  akken  kan  ad  yettu  temẓi-s  i  yeṭṭfen  deg-s.  ulac  ttawil  ur
yexdim akken ad yettu maca aya-agi d awezɣi.
Deg tullist-agi amaru yemmeslay-d ɣef tatut n temẓi i ɣer yebɣa Meqran
ad yaweḍ, aya-agi yettban-d s wudem usrid deg usebtar wis 62 :
Macci d ayen isehlen ɣef wemdan ad t-yexdem i tataut n temẓi…
Yekker i Fransa s iɣallen d wallen: ixeddem… Ar ass-a ur yewwiḍ ɣer lebɣi-s.
Ad yefru ayen id-as-tettalas temẓi akken ad yesɣers ayen i t-icudden ɣer-s…

n diri.

2-7-2- Isental inaddayen d limarat n usentel-nsen
Ad  neɛreḍ  ad  nefk  akk  isental  inaddayen  d  limarat-nsen  i  ɣef  d-tewwi
tullist-a :
2-7-2-1- Asmekti n temẓi
Amdan yella tikwal anida yettuɣal ɣer deffir akken ad yemmekti taɣawsa,
neɣ aneḍruy neɣ albeɛd, d aktay i iɛeddan yakan, ama d ayen yelhan neɣ d ayen
Ihi asmekti n temẓi d tuɣalin n wemdan ɣer wayen i iɛeddan deg tudert-is,
seg-s yettmeki amek yesɛedda ussan-nni mi yella d ameẓyan.
Amaru  deg  tullist-agi  yemmeslay-d  ɣef  usentel  n  usmekti  n  temẓi  s
wudem usrid, imi d yewwi ɣef Meqran i d-yemmektin temẓi-s akken ad iwali d
acu id-as-tettalas bac ad tt-yettu, aya-agi yettban-d deg imedyaten-a:
Ma yeqqim ad yettmekti taddart-is yettani gar wallen-is ixxamen-nni n wakal…
Yettwali diɣen lexyal n iberdan uɣur d ffɣent tzuliɣin…
Yettwali axxam-nsen d isulas i d-yecfan i tudert n yemdanen.
Temẓi-s yecfa-as-d tella deg-s yemma-s tbedd fell-as…
2-7-2-2- Inig
D rrwaḥ n wemdan ɣer tmura n medden, yezmer ad yili d rrwaḥ n tuɣalin
akken  yezmzer  ad  yili  daɣen  d  rrwaḥ  mebla  tuɣalin,  meḥsub  ad  yeqqim  deg
tmurt n  medden ad yeǧǧ tamurt-is, wa ad yuɣal d aɣrib di tmurt n iberraneyen,
inig.
Ihi iminig, yettuneḥsab amzun d tarewla ara ad yerwel wemdan seg tmurt-
is  ɣer  tmura  tiberraneyyin,  yal  yiwen  s  yiswi  n  trewla-agi  ama  d  anelmad  ɣef
tezrewt neɣ i uxeddim neɣ ɣef wayen-nniḍen.
129
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                         Tasleḍt
Deg  tullist-agi  yewwi-d  umaru  ɣef  lebɣi  n  Meqran  i  d-yellan  d  inig  ɣer
tmurt n Fransa, aya-agi yusa-d s udem usrid ad t-id-naf deg tdiwennit i d-yellan
gar Meqran d Wenza, asebtar wis 61:
Ciṭ akka tuɣal-d Wenza, tenna-as :
Yenna-iyi-d gma tebɣiḍ ad truḥeḍ ɣer Fransa, tidet ? Melmi ara tinigeḍ ?
D tidet ad ruḥeɣ, azekka tanezzayt ad afgeɣ, terna inig-iw macci d asikel.
D acu ? ad teffɣeḍ ur d-tettezziḍ ara ?
Yenna-as Meqran :
Amek tebɣiḍ ? d acu ara xedmeɣ nniḍen ?
2-8- Tasleḍ n tullist « Tizqaqin n taddart »
Ad neɛreḍ ad nekkes asental agejdan i ɣef tebna tullist « Tizqaqin n taddart
», d yisental inaddayen, syin akkin ad nefk limarat n usentel.
2-8-1- Asentel agejdan d limarat n usentel : lmektub
Deg tudert n wemdan, yal yiwen d acu yessaram yal yiwen d acu d iswi i
ɣer yebɣa ad yaweḍ, maca win i aɣ-d-ixelqen yal yiwen seg-neɣ yerra-as amur-
is deg tudert-is, imi ma yella yura deg twenza n wemdan ad yawi neɣ ad yaweḍ
neɣ ad yekseb taɣwsa, ɣas yerwel fell-as ad tt-tettbeɛ imi fell-as i tura.
Ihi lmektub yura ɣef yal yiwen deg twenza-s ama diri-t neɣ yelha yessefk
fell-aɣ ad t-neqbel, wa ad nidir yid-s.
Deg  tullist-agi,  «  Tizqaqin  n  taddart  »  yewwi-d  umaru  ɣef  lmektub  s
wudem  arusrid  nefhem-it-id  seg  tɣuri-nneɣ  i  tullist-a,  imi  yemmeslay-d  ɣef
wayen  i  yuran deg twenza  n  wemdan  ur  yezmir ad t-ibeddel, dɣa Yidir d Qasi
gar  wid  i  yebnan  tirga-nsen  akken  ssaramen  ad  ffɣent,  maca  lmektub  yedda
akken yebɣa uxellaq, imi sin yid-sen tid ḥemmlen zewǧent d wiyiḍ, dɣa ɣelḍen
130
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                         Tasleḍt
deg  leḥsab-nsen  macci  akken  ɣillen  ara  teffeɣ  taluft,  deg  yimedyaten-a  ad  naf
limarat n usentel n lmektub i d-yellan fell-asen i sin yid-sen, deg tdiwennit i d-
yellan gar Qasi d Mennad:
Qasi: Ihi, d acu yellan ma tettbaneḍ tḥezneḍ ?
Mennad: Tezriḍ ! ur bɣiɣ ara ak-sḥezneɣ… ihi tin akken i tḥemmleḍ ass-agi ad
Asmi d-yufa iman-is yeɣleḍ di leḥsab-is: tin iḥemmel fkan-tt imawlan-is tedda d
teddu d tislit.
tislit.
2-8-2- Isental inaddayen d limarat n usentel
Ad  neɛreḍ  ad  nefk  akk  isental  inaddayen  d  limarat-nsen  i  ɣef  d-tewwi
tullist-a
2-8-2-1- Abeddel n tudert
Zik  imdanen  d  wid  yeṭṭfen  deg  wansayen-nsen,  xas  ɛeddan  acḥal  d
aseggas  maca  qqimen  kan  akken-nni,  d  yiwen  n  lɛerc  d  yiwen  n  wedrum
tamɛict-nsen  seg  tmurt  i  xeddemn  yal  taɣawsa,  yella  leqder  gar  yemdanen  yal
wa yettɛawan wayeḍ amzun d yiwen ufus, mazal tella tejmiɛt deg taddart, tullas
mazal ttruḥunt ɣer tala, ilmeẓyen mazal ttɛassan tilmeẓyin deg webrid-nsent ɣer
tala.
Maca annect-a yak teddunn wussan uɣalen imdanen beddlen imi ǧǧan akk
leɛwayed d wansayen n zik, amɛic n tmurt dayen yekfa acku yella ansi ad aɣeɣ
yemdanen,  uɣalen  yal  yiwen  anda  i  yunag  ǧǧan  akk  taddar,  tullas  ulac  tid
yettruḥun  ɣer  tala…  acku  d  ayen  tbeddel  tmeddurt  kullec  yella  tura,yernu
ttruḥun medden ɣer temdinin.
Deg tullist-agi amaru  yemmeslay-d ɣef  tezqaqin  n taddart  yeqqimen  kan
akken llant, maca d imdane i ibeddlen, yal yiwen anda yerra.
131
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                         Tasleḍt
Ad naf limarat n usentel deg yimedyaten-a
Maca imezdaɣ s waṭas.
Ur ttɣiman ara yelmezyen deg tejmiɛt, sɛan akk ccɣel i ten-yeṭṭfen.
Ulac ifellaḥen ad ixedmen tibḥirin, si ssuq i d-ttaɣen medden ayen ḥlaǧen…
D taxeṭṭayt temɣart ara d-izedmen isɣaren, yella lgaz n teqreɛtin.
2-9- Tasleḍt n tullist « Ih ! Lukan ad tezreḍ! »
Ad neɛreḍ ad nekkes asental agejdan i ɣef tebna tullist Taninna, d yisental
inaddayen, syin akkin ad nefk limarat n usentel.
2-9-1- Asentel agejdan d limarat-is : tanekra n tuber 1988.
Asentel i d-yufraren deg tullist-agi Ih ! Lukan ad tezreḍ ! , d win n tnekra
n tuber 1988, yewwi-d fell-as umaru s wudem usrid.
Ayen yeḍran deg tnekra n 05 tuber 1988, macci d ayen ara yettu wemdan
imi  d  ayen  i  d-yeǧǧan  ccama  deg  yemdanen,  acku  acḥal  d  win  iruḥen  d  asfel
acḥal d win ijerḥen deg-s.
Deg tnekra n tuber 1988, d tin i d-yellan di Lezzayer sseba-ines d liḥala n
tudert  n  yemdanen  yettidiren  deg  lemḥayen,  acku  tamɛict  txuss,  axeddim  ulac,
tadamsa  i  d-yellan  deg  ubrid  n  uɣelluy,  tebda-d  d  tamesbanit ̽  deg  tlemmast  n
lezzayer tuɣal tuɣ amkan wessiɛen tedda akk ɣer temdinin-nniḍen.
Yeffeɣ-d  wegdud  azzayri  ɣer  berra  akken  ad  ssutren  azref-nnsen  seg
uwanak,  imi  tiweḍ  tudert-nnsen  ɣer  tilisa,  tebda-d  d  tamesbanit  tuɣal  meqqert
taluft  imi  seg  tmesbanit  tuɣal  d  amussu  asmi  d  yeffeɣ  yigen  ɣer  wegdud
yesserwet  deg-sen  akken  ilaq,  imi  acḥal  d  win  yemmuten  iruḥ  d  asfel  acḥal  d
win  i  ijerḥen,  tuɣal  taluft  n  usuter  n  uzref  d  tanekra  d  traḍ  gar  yezzayriyen,
uɣalen ttemwaten gar-asen, dɣa ḍelben abeddel asertan i lezzayer merra aya-agi
132
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                         Tasleḍt
yegla-d daɣen s ubeddel n tmendawt, maca deg tnekra-agi iruḥ d asfel azal n 500
d taɣtest ̽.
Llan daɣen wid  ur  neddi ara deg tnekra-agi  maca ruḥen d asfel,  mmuten
ur xdimen ula d acemma, nɣan-ten lɛesker maca macci s liɛmada, am texḍibt n
Mennad  i  yemmuten  deg  tnekra-agi,  mebla  ma  texdem  ula  d  acemma,  imi
teqqim deg uxxam maca wwten-tt temmut.
Deg  tullist-agi,  yemmeslay-d  umaru  ɣef  tnekra  n  tuber  1988  aya-agi
yettban-d deg yimedyaten-agi :
Ḥsiɣ aṭas ara s-yinin ciṭ yemmuten di tnekra-nni n tuber…
Tiweḍ s anda akken a naweḍ akk.
Ass n ssebt i tt-ḥuzan ɣer ubalku, lɛesker mara kkaten deg igenni, din i teɣli…
2-9-2- Isental inaddayen d limarat n usentel :
Ad  neɛreḍ  ad  nefk  akk  isental  inaddayen  d  limarat-nsen  i  ɣef  d-tewwi
tullist-a :
2-9-2-1- Tayri
Tayri d aḥulfu yellan deg wul i yettbuddu wemdan wemdan-nniḍen, tayri
temxalaf  imi  tella  tin  gar  tyemmat  d  warraw-is  akked  wergaz  d  tmeṭṭut,  tayri
tettili-d  s  lemwalfa  n  wemdan-nni  i  nḥemmel,  dɣa  ad  nuɣal  nettidir  kan  seg-s
aya-agi yattawi ɣer leḥmala, imi tayri tettas-d seg lemwalfa.
Deg  tullist-agi,  amaru  yemmeslay-d  ɣef  tayri  yellan  gar  Mennad  d
Jeǧǧiga,  d  wamek  myussanen  akked  wussan  sɛeddan  akken  kan  ddukulen  deg
yal  taswiɛt.  yemmeslay-d  dakken  tayri-nsen  d  tin  yellan  zeddiyet  acku  acḥal
nitni akken i llan werǧin msefraqen, ɣas akken yiweḍ-d wasmi d tewwi Jeǧǧiga
lbak  tuɣal  tebɛed  ɣef  Mennad  maca  deg  wadeg  kan  imi  ɣas  akka  maca  ufan-d
tifrat akken ad ttemwalin ɣas akken mbaɛaden.
133
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                         Tasleḍt
Nasserdin  d  yiwen  umaru  d-yefkan  tamuɣli-is  ɣef  tayri-a  n  Mennad  d
Jejiga dakken tesɛa assaɣ ɣer tsertit1    ( Nasserdin Ait Ouali, 2014 : 178)
Deg tullist-agi, yewwi-d umaru ɣef tayri s wudem usrid, imi ur yessexdem
ara lemɛani uffiren akken ad yemmeslay ɣef tayri n Mennad d Jeǧǧiga, aya-agi
yettban-d deg yimedyaten-a :
Asmi t-ssneɣ tella yiwet n teqcict yid-s…
Ur tebɣi ara ad teqqim yiwen wass di tudert-is ur yelli ara Mennad ɣer tama-s.
Ah ! awi yeẓran d acu d tayri kečč ad tfehmed.
Asirem n Mennad d wa : ad yekcem ɣer tesdawit ad iɣer d Jeǧǧiga, ad yili yid-s
simi ad rren axxam.
2-3-2-2- Lmut
Lmut tettili-d ma yella amdan yiweḍ-d wass-is, ad iruḥ seg tudert n da-agi
ɣer tudert n d ih-in, imi rruḥ-is ad yeǧǧ tafekka-d ad teqqim deg tmurt,
Yal amdan yessefk fell-as ad yaweḍ wass ad iruḥ ad yinig s anda ad nruḥ
akk  bla  tuɣali,  imi  aya-agi  ilaq  ad  yeḍru  maca  lmut-agi  yal  yiwen  amek  si-d-
tettas imi llan wid yuḍnen mmuten, llan wid yesɛan tazmert ula akk d acu uḍnen
maca  mmuten  kan  akka  bla  sseba,  llan  wid  yettemtaten  deg  teswiɛin  n  tnekra
neɣ ṭraḍ.
Lmut  ihi,  ma  yella  amda  d  ayen  iruḥ  seg  tudert-agi,  bla  ad  yuɣal  ɣer
tudert, deg tullist-agi amaru yemmeslay-d ɣef lmut Jeǧǧiga d leḥzern d wurfan i
Mennad akked d usirem id-as-iruḥen imi tella nettat i d kullec ɣef Mennad.

134
Aḥric wis sin                                                                                         Tasleḍt
Yemmeslay-d umaru ɣef lmut n Jeǧǧiga i d-yeǧǧan Mennad deg tebrek d
tudert-is  i  tezdeɣ  terzeg  seg-mi  t-teǧǧa,  yewwi-t-id  s  wudem  usrid,  aya-agi
yettban-d deg yimedyaten-agi :
Ass n ssebt it t-ḥuzan, ɣer ubalku…
Akken tt-walaɣ ɣliɣ fell-as ur zmireɣ ad ṭṭfeɣ imeṭṭi.
Walaɣ udem-is tikelt taneggarut dayen ḥala di lkaɣeḍ ara tt-zerreɣ
Ayen ruɣ fell-as limer tmaran idammen seg  wallen yali udem-is d  wemzur-is a
ten-rreɣ d izeggaɣen.

yebna-tt  ɣef  lxilaf  yellan  gar  tmetti  Taqbaylit  tamensayt  d  tmetti  Taqbaylit

Tagrayt tamatut
Tagrayt tamatut
Tagrayt tamatut
Tazrawt-nneɣ  tella-d  ɣef  tullisin  yura  Saɛid  Cemmax,  ma  sɛant  tulmisin  n
tullist Taqbaylit, d tuksa n yisental i d-yewwi deg yal yiwet deg-sent.
Iwakken  ad  nessiweḍ  ɣer  wayen  nebɣa,  nefren-d  ad  nexdem  tasleḍt
tasentalant i yal tullist, netbeɛ tizri n yemyura am : 
Ilmend n waya-agi, deg uḥric n tesleḍt banent-d tullisin n Saɛid Cemmax,
d  tid  yesɛan  tulmisin  n  tullist  Taqbaylit,  nerna  nessebgen-d  akk  isental  i  ɣef  d
yemmeslay umaru deg wammud-agi n tullisin.
Tutlayt yessemres umaru Saɛid Cemmax deg tullisin-is, d tutlayt tushilt d
tin yezmer ad yefhem yal amdan, d tin yellan d tusridt acku amaru ur yessexdem
ara awalen  uffiren d  lemɛani  i  iweɛren akken  ur  ifahem ara wemdan anamek  n
wayen  d-yenna,  maca  tikwal  nettaf-d  amaru  yessemras  kra  n  yinzan  iwakken
kan  ad  asent-yefk  udem  n  tmetti  taqbaylit.  Deg  tullisin-a  amaru  yewwi-d  ɣef
yisental yellan deg tilawt, nezmer ad d-nini d timsal yettidir umdan deg tudert-is.
Deg  tullisin-agi  daɣen,  nufa-d  amaru  yessexdem  akud,  iwakken  ad
yessebgen  melmi  d  ḍran  yineḍruyen  n  tullist,  akken  i  d-nufa  daɣen  adeg  i  d-
yessebganen imukan anda ḍran yineḍruyen n tullist.
Iwudam  deg  tullisin-agi,  bḍan  ɣef  snat  n  tewsatin;  iwudam  igejdanen  d
yiwudam inaddayen, imi d nitni i yesselḥayen ineḍruyen n tullist, yerna fell-asen
i ɣef tbedd tullist si tazwara almi d taggara.
Aglam  daɣen  d  win  i  d-yeddan  deg  tullisin-agi,  anda  i  d-nufa  yella-d
uglam n tigawin, iwudam d tɣawsiwin.
Akken tella daɣen tdiwennit i d-yellan gar yiwudam, aya-agi yettmuddu-
as  udem  n  tilawt  i  tullisin,  yerna  yettcuddu  ineḍruyen-is.  Tasiwelt  d  tin  yellan
daɣen  deg  wammud-agi,  deg-s  ad  naf  amaru  tikwal  d  netta  kan  i  d-yettalsen
138
Tagrayt tamatut
inedruyen,  meḥsub  ur  yefki  ara  i  yiwudam  tilelli  akken  ad  ssenfalin  nitni  ɣef
yiman-nsen d waken bɣan nitni, tikwal-nniḍen d iwudam i d-yettalsen ineḍruyen
d nitni i d-iḥekkun ɣef yiman-nsen.
Ma  d  isental  deg  wammud-agi  n  tullisin,  seld  uxeddim  n  tasleḍt
tasentalant,  nufa-d amaru Saɛid Cemmax yewwi-d ɣef  isental  yellan deg tmetti
Taqbaylit, yemmeslay-d ɣef lxilaf yellan gar tmetti Taqbaylit tamensayt d tmetti
Taqbaylit  tartart,  d  isental  yellan  deg  tilawt,  d  ayen  yezmer  yal  amdan  ad  ten-
yidir deg tudert-is am (tayri, lexdeɛ, ttar…).
Nufa-d yewwi-d ɣef usentel n tayri gar zik d tura, di tallit tamensayt ɣas
ma  tella  tayri  imi  ur  d-tt-ban  ara,  zik  tella  leḥya  d  lḥerma,  ma  deg  tallit-a
tamirant  tban-d  yerna  s  wudem  ufdiḥ,  akka  am  tullist  Taninna  tayri  tella  s
wudem  ufdiḥ  yerna  ur  tesaweḍ  ara  ɣer  yeswi  deg  taggara,  sseba  n  wanect-a  d
lexdeɛ-nni  n  Basel,  yexdeɛ  tamdakkelt-is  yerna  yeḍmeɛ  ad  tt-qebel  ad  tt-zweǧ
yid-s.
Yerna  ymesselay-d  ɣef  ttar  yellan  kan  zik,  acku  tura  llan  yissuḍaf  ara
yḥekmen  ɣef  win  iɣelḍen  di  kra.  Daɣen  yemmaslay-d  ɣef  temsalt  n  zwaǧ,  zik
yiwen ma temmut tmaṭṭut-is, ttaran-tt i ulews-is, ma yella deg tallit tartart ur d-
nettaf  ara  anect-a,  syen  akkin  yerna  ybeder-d  yir  tamuɣli  i  tesɛa  tmetti  ɣer
teqcict  yeɣran,  amaru  yebɣa  ad  d-yini  deg  tullist-nni  n  «  ɛecrin  duru  »  dakken
maci ala taqcict yeɣran i yesɛan laɛyub, ula d tin yeqqimen deg uxxam. Ma deg
tullist  «  Ad  gen  tameɣra  »  yebɣa  ad  d-yessebgen  dakken  deg  tallit-a  tamirant
imdanen d wid  yettaran  iman-nsen sɛan tamusni,  nutni  xḍan  i tmusni, akka am
warraw n Wakli, ur fkin ara leqder i baba-tsen, glan s terwiḥt-is.
Deg taggara n tezrawt-nneɣ ad d-nini tullisin yura Saɛid Cemmax d tid yesɛan
tulmisin n tullist taqbaylit, ma dayen yeɛnan isental, yewwi-d ɣef wid yella deg
tmetti Taqbaylit, llan s wudem n tilawit, akka am : tayri, lexdeɛ, laman, taddukli,
tikkelax,

Taninna,
Neɣ tudert n tlemẓit taqbaylit
A-tt-an  tiweḍ-d  lkaṛ-nni  yettawin  ɣer  tmezduɣt  n  inelmeden  n  tesdawit.
Yekker wemdegger anda amdan  yezmer ad d-yini “nekni d  lmal, d akraren”…
Tullas  neɣ  arrac,  ur  yelli  win  yenḥerwan  deg  wayen  ara  yeḍrun  imi  uɣen
tannumi,  wulfen.  D  taswiɛt  i  yebɣan  akka.  Yiwet  n  teqcict  sya  u  sya  nnḍen-as
warrac  ara  tettsuɣu,  amzun  ulac  wi  yeslan,  ad  tiniḍ  armi  d  imiren  i  sen-tenniḍ
“Demmret  !”…Taqcict  a  tesḥirẓil  s  ufud  i  s-tefka  tfekka-s  armi  tiweḍ  ɣer
tewwurt ad tali, attan yeddhem-itt-id yiwen, zemreɣ ad d-iniɣ ur ikcim ara akk s
aɣerbaz, seg wid nni i wumi qqaren aɣyul 3 yetran ! Temkerfaf, ciṭ i ixuṣṣen ad
tetti di trekkabin-nni n wuzzal. Tedda tikelt nniḍen deg udemmer, tuli.
“Uuk  !”  terra-d  nnehta,  xuṣṣent  ḥala  turin-is  ur  d-ddint  ara,  udem-is
yewlelles, werraɣ…  Tɛedda tama n ṭṭaq a tettmuqul deg ugeffur amek i d-iɣelli
ɣer wemdun n waman. Tezzi allen-is ɣer lɣaci, tessikid amek ttemyussaden ɣer
temzizzal, ttazzalen s anda ara ddarin… Iqder teɛya di tmuɣli, tebra i wallen-is.
Ticenfirin-is  ldint  amzun  tṛuḥ  ad  tergem  tuɣal  am  akken  ibedd-as  wawal  deg
Teqleɛ lkaṛ ad truḥ, leɛyaḍ yekker di beṛṛa imi iṣekker umenhar tawwurt.
Taqcict  ur  teṭṭif  ara  deg  iman-is,  temkerfaf,  teddhem  yiwen  n  weqcic  tama-yis
iles-is.
tenna-yas:
-  Suref-iyi…
Ur d-tfukk ara awal, yerra-yas-d :
-  Uh ! Ulac aɣilif…
Ara  tetteddu  lkar.  Mi  tiweḍ  ɣer  temlilit  n  iberdan,  teḥbes  ɣer  lǧiha
tayeffust imi d tikaryas d-yekkan deg ubrid igezmen i yettɛeddin. Imiren, teḥbes-

yessufeɣ-d aqerru-s si ṭṭaq inṭeq-d ɣer teqcict, yenna-yas…

Ammud n tullisin

leḥya-nni i d as-mlan imawlan-is tekka-d nnig wawal i tebɣa a t-id-tini; tessusem

Aqcic  yeṭeyyiḥ,  imeddukal-is  ttaḍsan,  netta  simi  irennu…  zzin  ɣer-s  kra
inelmaden  iban  zzeɛf  ɣef  wudmawen-nsen…  imuqel-iten-id  yessusem.  Yuɣal
daɣen imiren ad yessawal ad d-yeqqar ayen ur yezmir ara wemdan ad d-yini di
teẓgi weḥd-s. Zzin inelmaden-nni ɣer teqcict, tɣaḍ-iten. Aqcic-nni icuff leḥnak-
is yerra-d awal-is ẓid ad yettecmumuḥ.
-  Yya-d, aha ! ur ttaggad, nekk mačči am wiyyaḍ…
Takerrust-nni teqleɛ tewwi  yid-s winna…  Iberdan  fran  maca ula akken ad
d-yessewɛad  s  ufus.  Taqcict  terra-d  nnehta…  Nndama  tban  ɣef  udem-is…
Nndama  ɣef  taddart  teǧǧa  s  lḥif…  Ur  as-iserreḥ  ara  baba-s  ad  d-tṛuḥ  ɣer
Lezzayer  ad  tkemmel  les  études  supérieures  armi  tuɣal  tudert-is  d  qeḍran  …
Nndama n tlalit neɣ n yir teswiɛt i deg i tella. Tusa-d si taddart-nnsen yellan deg
wedrar n Ǧerǧer anda arrac d-tettemlili tturebban, ur sɛin anecta n ddɣel d tismin
ɣer  teqcicin.  Tecfa  mi  ten-id-temlal  a  sen-tini  “azul  !  ”,  ad  as-d-tini  “azul  !  ”.
Nitni, ad ddun d webrid nnsen, nettat allen-is ad asen-tebru ad tkemmel abrid-is.
Tusa-d ad tɣer akken ur tt-yettḥaz uzaglu n tmetti i yettaran tilawin d taklatin i

ttaɣen  imdanen  akken  ad  lehhint  kan  d  leqdic  n  wexxam  deg  wass,  d  tguni  d

Ass-n ladɣa i teqseḍ a d-teṭṭixer si tesdawit n Bab Zwar, ad tuɣal ad tɣer
di tin n Tizi-Wezzu anda i teqqar Cabḥa tameddakkelt-is…
Ccix n taddart yeɣra leqran armi ijemmel settin ḥizeb, iceggex yerna icax !
ur  yezmir  ara  ad  d-yebder  awal  melba  ma  yedda-d  kra  n  leqran  neɣ  kra
imeslayen n taɛrabt. Iḥetteb taɛrabt d tameslayt yextaṛ Sidi Rebbi i tarwa-s acku

tameslayt-nni; ma d aɛṛab akken yebɣu yili d amakar neɣ d yir amdan, ad yezger
yerna s uɛennen ! Ruḥ kečč ad tfehmeḍ !
Ccix-agi  yella  zik  yettaru  tiḥreztin,  ttẓurunt  medden.  Yettzuxxu-yasen,

yemrabḍen n tallit-nni.

yessɣar Descartes d tarbaɛt-is, uɣalen kksen-as awal i ccix-nni. Maca ula d netta

ɣer  Iṛumyen  uqbel  lgirra  !  Dacu  kan,  di  temnaṭ-nni,  imdanen  ur  ḥemmlen  ara
taɛṛabt imi tt-terra ddewla d takna i tmaziɣt.
Ccix  yufa-d  iman-is  ḥala  netta  i  yettarrran neɣ “yettdafaɛen” ɣef taɛrabt.
Yettzuxxu  i  medden  acku  itekka  ɣer  s  ameddakel-is  akud  yeɣra  di  Zituna  i
yeqqlen  d  lewzir  mbaɛd  mi  yɛedda  d  prifi.  Yettaḍsa  m  ad  yemmekti  mi  yas-

Ammud n tullisin
“ A Muḥ Crif ! Kečč d lwali nekk d lewli ! Ihi, efk-iyi-d ad ak-n-fkeɣ !”…
Ihi, aṭas i d-nenna ɣef ccix-agi aḥecraruf maca ur d-nenna ara yesɛa mmi-s
d  ameẓyan  isem-is  Basel.  Isem-agi  d  baba-s  i  d-as-t-yextaṛen  acku  d  isem  n
mmi-s n Ḥafeḍ El-Asad, izem n Ibaɛtiyen; yernu lulen deg yiwen n wass ! limer
yeẓra  ccix  tella  yiwet  n  temdint  di  tmurt  n  Sswis  isem-is  Basel  (Bɛles),  ahat
mačči akka ad as-isemmi !
Basel-agi,  imi  d  netta  i  ɣef  a  naru  tura,  d  aẓerbuḍ ;  yeɣra  ciṭ  mbaɛd
yeṭaxer-d  si  lakul.  Yessekcem-it  baba-s  ɣer  l’ITE  s  tmusni  yesɛa  di  lakadimi.
Yeffeɣ-d zun d ccix  n ttarix acku  mačči seg wid  izemren ad  yesɣer amezruy  !
Maca  Basel  yerra-tt  ḥala  i  tecmatin  d  ṣṣekṛan  yal  ass  yerna  ula  d  tissit  n  lkif  i
yeḥfeḍ  mi  yeddukul  d  leḥbab  ɣer  tala  Gilef  anda  i  ttedṛagin  les  algéroises,  les
oranaises d les européennes acku qqaren-d i medden “ur nḥemmel ara la racaille
agi nnwen, neǧǧa-yawen-tt”…
Asmi i myssaneɣ d Basel, mmuteɣ si lfeṛḥ acku iban-iyi-d yecbeḥ, d aqcic
n  taddart-nneɣ,  yeɣra  yerna  d  ccix  n  lakul.  Ferḥeɣ  acku  ur  ggiɣ  ara  am  kra
tmeddukal-iw i yettbeddilen  ameddakel yal dduṛt neɣ yal aggur ma ɛeṭṭlent aṭas
!  Ddeqs  deg-sent  iyi-ḥawten  akken  ad  iyi-semlilent  aked  kra  n  warrac  i  wumi
ɛeǧbeɣ maca nekk ttagiɣ. Ur cfiɣ ara amek iyi-d-yeɛǧeb Basel, neɣ amek i bdiɣ
ḥemmleɣ-t armi yessaweḍ ad yeqqel d netta kan i swayes ttidireɣ, d netta kan i
wumi ttidireɣ. Ttṛaǧuɣ kan melmi a yestufu ad yas ɣur-i ɣer tesdawit. Tameddit,
ttṛaǧuɣ kan di texxamt-iw, di Mduḥa, melmi ara yi-tini walbeɛḍ n tullas “atan a
kem-yettnadi uḥday-nni yerɣan fell-am !”
Akka  i  ddreɣ  di  lfeṛḥ,  smeckukuleɣ  tirga  anda  ttwaliɣ  kan  mḥemmaleɣ
nekk d Basel.
Yiwen  wass,  tɛerḍ-iyi  Wrida  as  sweɣ  yid-s  lqehwa  deg  yiwen  n  salon  de
thé  i  wumi  qqaren  la  délicieuses.  Akken  neqqim,  tebda  Wṛida  ameslay  am  yal

tikelt ma ara tt-id-mlileɣ, tesɛa dayem kra n tedyant ara d-tini, yerna axeclaw ur

Mi yas-slan kra n warrac i Basel a yesfuǧǧuɣ kkren-d nnuɣen yid-s. Llan kra
bɣan  ad  as-fken  taḍriḥt,  maca  ggren-d  iman-nnsen  kra  n  wid  i  ten-iferrun,
ḍerqen-t-id  si  tejmiɛt,  nnan  i  yilmeẓyen-nni  “susmat,  rennun  ara  zzit  i  tmes,  d
nekni a iberrin si baba-s, yerna a t-nxeṭṭi…
Awal ur yeqqim ara ger ilmeẓyen, ɣas nitni ssusmen, Taninna diɣen terra
s  ul-is  ur  tenni  acemma  i  imawlan-is…  Maca  llant  tmeddukal-is,  nnant  i
imawlan-nnsent  kra  i  d-yenna  Basel.  Lewnis  yesla.  Ur  yumin  ara  ɣas  mačči  d
yiwen i yas-d-yennan… Lɣaci ur bɣin ara ccwal, qqaren-as d ṣṣekṛan i d-yeṣkeṛ,
neɣ mačči d nettat i d-yelha… Iruḥ-d s axxam yennuɣ yelli-s imi ur d as-d-tenni
ara,  yeddem-d  ifuci-s  yeffeɣ.  Yerra  ɣer  Tgersift,  tama  n  taddart  anda  zedɣen
imṛabḍen…  Tameṭṭut-is  akken  twala  tefka-t  tewwurt  tceggeɛ  ɣer  ṭṭemman  n
wedrum  d  kra  n  warrac  n  twacult  nnsen,  tenna-yasen  ad  t-ḍefren  mulac  ad
timɣur taluft.

akka  tamurt  nneɣ  ass-a  yewwi-tt  yeɣzer,  ur  d-yewwi  ara  a  nettu  temẓi  acku  d
amur  n  tmeddurt  nneɣ  ur  d-yettuɣalen  ara  i  yebɣu  nadir-it.  Mačči  deg  yezri  i

Laman d leɣder
-Amur amezwaru-
1.
“Aman d laman” akka i qqaren imezwura nneɣ, akka i d-ufan awal: tsuta
tettaǧǧa-t-id  i  tayeḍ  armi  i  d-yessaweḍ.  Nesteqsay  ɣef  ssebba  i  ten-yewwin  ad
ggen aman d laman. Гas akken ncukket cwiṭ imezwura nneɣ ḥemmlen ad walin
imeslayen n lemtul d-qqaren ɛedlen, amedya d awal agi aman i icuban ɣer laman
lmer  mačči  d  asekkil  “I”  i  yernan  ɣer  wawal  agi  wis  sin.  Daɣen  ma  nmuqel  s
Imuhaɣ,  a  naf  sɛan  yiwen  n  wanzi  i  deg  qqaren  “aman  iman.”  Nadi  tura  ad
tfehmeḍ ! Maca tella lmeɛna deffir n umeslay “aman d laman”, d acu-tt ? akken
iyi-d-sfehmen widak yessnen di taddart, at zik, ḥala tafellaḥt i d cceɣl nnsen, di
ḥertadem d ameggel d wekraz n wurtan, d azraɛ n yirden d temẓin, deg unebdu d
aserwet… d uɣellet. Ma yili  ur wwiten ara igerfan  ger  yennayer d  yebrir, ayen
izerɛen  ur  yettfekti,  ma  ur  telli  saba,  laẓ  a  d-iɛass  lerfuf;  arebrab  ad  yezdeɣ
ulawen. Dimi qqaren aman d laman. Гer wat zik, d aman n ugeffur i d ddunit ma
xḍan d tamettant i yettraǧun deg-sen. Ayen akk a yekk urebbit anẓar ur asen-d-
yebri ara d nnger i yeggunin. Akka i d tamuɣli nnsen ɣer tudert. Yal wa d anda i
t-tessaweḍ tmussni-s. Yal wa d takti yesɛa, yal wa tallit deg i yeddar, i ɣer icudd.
Mbaɛd  mi  beddlen  lewqat,  ttmettaten  wid  yesɛan  tikta  nni,  ttlalen-d
yemdanen  yesɛan tikta  nniḍen ddren taswiɛt  nniḍen  ur  ncuba ara  ɣer tin  n zik.
Llan  wid  yufan  aman  mačči  d  laman  acku  zemren  a  d-glun  s  tmettant  n  win
ɛzizen ɣef wexxam, nnan ihi laman yemxalaf ɣef aman imi wigi zemren ad ilin d
“wer laman” !
Tadyant d tin yeḍran d yiwen n wergaz deg yiwet n taddart ur iban yisem-
is. Aṭas n tudrin yellan di tmurt n Leqbayel, yal ta d tidyanin d-tessaweḍ. Argaz
isem-is  Awejhan.  Гas  isem-agi  iɣab  aṭas  aya  di  tmazɣa,  ḥala  di  tezmamin  i  d-
yeqqim,  nnan  tsemmint  deg  wedrar  ineffusiyen  di  tama  n  Libya  maca  ula  di
162
Ammud n tullisin
ddewla  n  Fransa  llan  wid  yesɛan  isem-agi  di  tama  n  At  Yeḥya  di  temnaḍt  n
Micli.
Ihi,  Awejhan  agi  yesɛa  sin  warrac  d  snat  teqcicin,  d  afellaḥ  seg  wasmi  i
yas-d-cfan  lǧiran-is  neɣ  imezdaɣ  n  taddart.  Ddeqs  n  wurtan  i  yesɛa  ama  d
azemmur di tniri neɣ d tazart deg uzaɣar. Yedder netta d twacult-is s rrezq i d-
ḥellant  tidiwin-is.  Werǧin  i  yas-d-yessukes  yiwen  ayen  n  diri.  Ihenna  medden,
nitni hennan-t. yedder lxir yugar fell-as, yewwi-d tislit i mmi-s mi yewweḍ ɣer
tizi  n  zzwaǧ.  Yelli-s  tameqqrant  hattan  tewweḍ  d  tilemẓit  qrib  ula  d  nettat  ad
teǧǧ  imawlan-is  akken  ad  terzu  ɣef  wid  i  tt-yebɣan.  Akka  i  tella  tmeddurt  n
twacult  asmi  i  d-tewweḍ  “lgirra  n  Lalman”.  Awejhan  tessels-as  Fṛansa  d
aɛsekriw,  iruḥ  ad  yennaɣ  ɣer  tmurt-nni,  am  netta  am  izzayriyen,  ameggaru  ur
yezgil  yiwen.  Ɣas  akken  qrib  ad  yessiweḍ  40  iseggasen  di  leɛmer-is,  tewwi-t
Fṛansa neɣ akken qqaren di tallit-nni: temmubilizi-t !
Am netta am medden. Di taddart, ala kra n yemɣaren iwessuren, tilawin d
warrac i d-yeqqimen.
Awejhan  iṛuḥ, ad  yennaɣ  mgel  Lalman tanazit  i d-yezzi,  mmi-s ameqran:
Aɛmer daɣen akken ciṭ mbaɛd baba-s i t-wwin, armi yexsi ṭṭrad i d-yuɣal. Deg
wexxam n Uwejhan ladɣa i d-yeqqimen di lgirra-nni ḥala tilawin ggunint aqcic-
nni  wis  sin:  Yidir  imi  yas-semmḥen  si  sserbis-nni  acku  di  tallit-nni  tuɣ  yuḍen
yiweḍ  ɣer  tizi  n  lmut.  At  wexxam  ttraǧun  kan  melmi  asen-d-yaweḍ  ujeɛbub  n
lkaɣeḍ  akken  d-yewweḍ  i  kra  n  yemɣaren  n  taddart:  d  nnican  ɣef  mmi-tsen
yemmuten  di  Ṭelyan,  di  Biljik  neɣ  di  Lalman  neɣ  ahat  di  Fṛansa  s  yiman-is.
Yeɣli  Hitler:  tefra  lgirra  yezzi-d  baba-s  d  mmi-s  ɣer  taddart.  Feṛḥen  imawlan-
nnsen imi d-uɣalen d imuddiren, imi ur mmuten ara kan ccwi !...
Maca lḥif ur ifukk ara ɣas tefra lgirra. Asmi d-iwḍen irgazen s axxam ufan-

maca yettnadi kan amek a yesnerni ssɛaya-yis, yuggi ad yissin leqniɛa yas akken

nnsen  i  yeɛddan  d  ṭṭamen.  Tikelt-agi,  Ajendi  yebɣa  deg  uzal  qayli  ad  yeḥweṣ

temubilizi-yaɣ Fṛansa, ur neẓri ma nemmet neɣ a nidir, argaz yeqqim di taddart i
tḥeggaṣ”…
Yefra  ccreɛ;  yerbeḥ-it-id  Uwejhan  maca  teqqim-d  terẓeg  d  umɣanzu  ger

neɣ d sin i ttwaxeṭṭan ɣer tejmiɛt acku nnuɣen, maca ugin ad rren aḍar i sin.
Ad iṛuḥ a d-yuɣal ɣer ccreɛ-nni yeɛddan, ad yekker ubagaṛ ! Yiwen wass,
Ajendi a d-yettqeẓqiẓ ɣer Aɛmer, dɣa yenna-yas wagi, zdat medden meṛṛa:

k-yenɣen !...
Teɣli-d  tsusmi  di  tejmiɛt,  akken  d  teɣli  tugdi  acku  imeqqranen  n  taddart
ḥṣan  akka  i  d-beddunt  tlufa  ur  nferru.  Nitni  ladɣa  tnadin  amek  ur  d-ttilint  ara
tlufa ger medden akken ḥṣan daɣen Aɛmer mmi-s n Uwejhan, ɣas akken werǧin
i yas-d-ssuksen di taddart, maca yewɛer aṭas mi yeggul a d-yekkes kra a d-yeddu
neɣ a d-yeqqurmeḍ ! dɣa ugaden aṭas ad ineɣ Ajendi imir a d-tuɣal tinna n ttar
nni  zik :  ad  msengarent  twaculin  di  taddart,  ad  nfun  imdanen,  ad  hudden
yexxamen.
164
Ammud n tullisin
Ajendi si tama-s yeẓra acu i t-yerǧan: d lmut. Yeqqim yettḥebbir amek i d
tifrat-is, yufa-tt-id : ‘ma yeggul yiwen ak-ineɣ, zwir deg-s, enɣ-it !’’.
Yefra-tt deg uqerru-yis akka: ad ineɣ Aɛmer. Yuɣal yettxemim amek a t-
ineɣ ? Limer as-d-yesɣim albeɛḍ, izmer ad yeffeɣ wawal ad slen medden, ad isel
Uwejhan. Ad yuɣal ttar maca limer a t-ineɣ s tḥila, s tkellax, di laman yiwen ur
iẓer, yezmer ad yetthenni.
Aṭas  i  yeqqimen  akken  ad  d-yaf  tafukelt  i  swayes  ad  yekkes  Aɛmer  si
ddunit. Maca yufa-tt-id: ad yessexdem Wezna, tameṭṭut n Aɛmer acku d nettat i
d amdan i yettamen aṭas am baba-s, yemma-s neɣ gma-s. Acuɛer d Wezna i ɣer
ixemmem ? Acku yessen-itt d tahwawit kan: efk-as zzhu teǧǧa-yak yalci ! Maca
amek a yaweḍ ad as-imeslay ? sked akken ur yeḥṛaret ara ad as-yehder i Wezna
ur yufi ara. Yettɛassa-tt si tifawt ɣer tmeddit, ulac. Maca yegger-as tamawt acu
txeddem di yalass ssmana, yessen akk ansi i tettek ? akud ? melmi ? ayɣer ?...
Yiwen  wass,  yeẓra-tt  tɛedda  ɣer  tala  weḥd-s  yezwar-as  s  abrid  ihdeṛ-as,
nettat  mačči  tenna-yas  zzant  wala  rɣant.  Mi  tuɣal  s  axxam,  ur  asen-tenna  ara  i
wat  wexxam  ‘yenṭeq-d  ɣur-i  Ujendi’.  Wagi  tuɣal-as  d  tannumi,  yettqayas  kan
Wezna  melmi  a  tili  weḥd-s  akken  ad  as-yini  awal  neɣ  sin,  ad  yeḍs  ɣer-s…
yeqqar-as diɣen:
-  Ma tecfiḍ ɣef zik, mi netturar akken, ḥemmleɣ-kem, d kemm i bɣiɣ ad aɣeɣ
maca zwaren-iyi ɣer-m maca mazal d kemm i ḥemmleɣ !...
Si  tikelt  ar  tayeḍ  ad  as-d-yawi  ayelluc  swayes  ssedhuyen  arrac,  tikelt  d
tazrart,  tikelt  d  taqraɛt  n  rriḥa,  abrid  nniḍen  d  ameqyas…  Wezna  tuɣal  tefṛeḥ,
teqqar-as deg wul-is d argaz am Ujendi iyi-ilaqen mačči d Aɛmer i yexḍan akk i
zzhu n ddunit. Netta di tidet, Aɛmer ur yeẓri ara ilaq-as ad yelhi d tmeṭṭut-is: ad
as-d-yaɣ  kra  swayes  a  tettcebbiḥ,  ilaq-as  ad  tezzhu  !  …  Aɛmer  am  aṭas  n
yergazen n taddart ɣur-s tameṭṭut telha i tterbga n warrac, leqdicat n beṛṛa d wid
n wexxam … Akken qqaren kra imaṣuten: telha i sekksu d wusu…
165
Ammud n tullisin
Tebda  Wezna  a  tettɣanzu  argaz-is  ciṭ  ciṭ.  Mačči  di  yeẓra  walbeɛḍ  ma
tḥemmel Aɛmer neɣ xaṭi imi asmi i tt-fkan imawlan-is tedda d tislit. Acku zik, di
tmurt  n  Leqbayel,  d  lɛib  ad  yeffeɣ  wawal  ama  ɣef  tmeṭṭut  am  ɣef  wergaz,
tḥemmel  yiwen  neɣ  iḥemmel  yiwet  !  Ttṣeḍḥin  medden s tayri  ! Mačči am  tura
anda tayri teqqel d lsas n zwaǧ… (Rǧut: mazal tuddar anda yir leɛwayed nni  n
zik  ggumant  ad  ɣlint,  tidak  nni  ur  ten-id-llhiɣ  ara  !).  Ihi,  Aɛmer-agi  werǧin
tessin qbel zzwaǧ-nnsen: am nettat am tizyiwin-is, tullas n taddart qrib akka akk
i  ttezwaǧent,  di  tallit-nni.  Ladɣa  ma  yella  ur  iḥemmel  ara  wergaz  tameṭṭut-is,
ulac  uɣilif,  ad  kkren  imawlan  ad  as-nadin  tameṭṭut  nniḍen,  tikwal  melba  ma
tebra tmezwarut ! I yeḍran d lbaṭṭel…
Ihi amek akken i teḍra n Wezna ? Limer tettaf ur tettwali ara argaz-is, tebɣa
ad  as-yebru  akken  a  d  tt-yaɣ  Ujendi.  Sked  tin  ur  texdim,  Aɛmer  ur  yecliɛ  ara:
ɣur-s ɣas tessexṣer Wezna kra, terẓa kra neɣ tennuɣ d wat wexxam. D awezɣi,
yennuɣ-itt, yewwet-itt  neɣ  iḍerq-itt…  Aɛmer, ɣur-s  medden zemren ad sxesren
kra, ur yelli fell-as wawal. Wezna meskint tḥar anta ad d-tjab, ulac. Tameɣbunt,
ur teẓra ara mi dak-d-yeḍsa yiwen s wuglan, yefka-yak-d iles dɣa kečč ad tɣileḍ
ɛzizeḍ  fell-as;  netta  yuɣ  lḥal  a  yettnadi  kan  amek  a  yaweḍ  ɣer  lebɣi-s.  Mi  t-
yewweḍ  ur  k-id-yettissin  ara  ula  s  tmuɣli.  Aḥesrah  acḥal  n  wid  d  tid
yettwakellxen akka !
Wezna teḥṣa ur tezmir ara ad temfaraq kan akka d Aɛmer, ma yella twureb
ilaq  ad  tili  ssebba:  yella-d  umennuɣ,  tettwaḥqar…  Ur  tezmir  ara  tmeṭṭut  a  d-
tekker  ad  asen-tini  i  wat  wexxam  ‘ad  uɣaleɣ  s  axxam  n  baba  !’  Ilaq  ad  tili
ssebba.  Tettnadi  amek  a  tennaɣ  akd  Aɛmer  ur  tufi  ara,  yal  ass  yettawi-yas.
Yeqqar-as  deg  wul-is  iqder  d  ɛeggu  i  teɛya  di  leqdic  ɣef  baba  d  yemma  d  imi
treffu fell-i.
Mi iwala Ujendi Wezna tewwa u tessenṭi-d, yenna-yas:
166
Ammud n tullisin
-
Ihi ilaq-am ad tenɣeḍ Aɛmer acku skud ur am-yebra ara ur zmireɣ ara a kem-
aɣeɣ.  Netta  atan  ur  yellhi  ara  ad  am-yebru.  Teqqim-d  ala  yiwet  n  tifrat  a  t-
tenɣeḍ, mi yemmut a nemzawaǧ, a nerr axxam di sin, ad teṛwuḍ kra texsiḍ !.
Di tazwara tuggad imi di leɛmer-is ur tezli ula d tayaziṭ ma tuɣal takti-agi n
tmenɣiwt  tezdeɣ  allaɣ-is,  teqqaz  deg-s  am  twekka  deg  iniɣman.  D  acu  kan
yiwen  wass  tendekwal-d  tenna  deg  wul-is:  maca  di  tmenɣiwt  n  wergaz-iw,  ur
tufiḍ acu a rebḥeɣ acku  Ajendi  yezweǧ, s tmeṭṭut-is, yezmer ad  ikellex  fell-i.  I
wumi  a  nɣeɣ  Aɛmer,  netta  ur  iyi-yettaɣ  ara  !...  tebda  tmeṭṭut  a  tettfaq  s  anda  i
yebɣa ad yaweḍ Ujendi. Awi-d kan imi mazal d allaɣ n wemdan i tesɛa mačči d
win n tẓiwci !
Ayen deg a tciweṛ albaɛḍ ɣef ayen i yas-d-yenna Ujendi, nettat hha ! Tṛuḥ
ɣeu-s tenna-yas ayen tettxemmim. Ajendi yenna-yas:
-  D  aya  i  kem-yerḥan  !  Ɣas  sfeṛḥ  iman-im  si  tura.  Tameddit-agi  ad  twaliḍ
Taseɛdit  teffeɣ  axxam-iw  i  lebda,  d  kem  a  t-izedɣen,  d  kemm  akud  a  sɛuɣ
arraw-iw…
Ur tumin ara ayen akk i yas-d-yenna, maca tameddit, taddart akk tnezzeh-d
ɣer  umennuɣ  ger  Ujendi  d  tmeṭṭut-is.  Walan  akk  medden  mi  tt-yeḍreq  seg
wexxam-is : walan mi tedda Tasaɛdit d gma-s tbubb tawemmust iceṭṭiḍen, tuɣal
s axxam n baba-s. Dɣa Wezna tumen d tidet Ajendi yebra i tmeṭṭut-is akken a tt-
yaɣ  nettat  akken  i  das-iṛeggem.  Tefṛeḥ  mačči  d  kra.  Tura,  dayen  teffre-tt  deg
uqerruy-is: Aɛmer i d-yeqqimen d aɛkker ad tenɣ-it !
Temsefham d Ujendi, yewwi-yas-d yiwen ssem d ḥelljɣer neɣ lamuṛuṛa neɣ
acu nniḍen, wi yeẓran ? Yenna-yas ad as-tegg i Aɛmer deg wayen a isew tifawt
ma d akeffay, d lqehwa neɣ d latay.
Tegga-yas  acečči  nni  i  Aɛmer,  yiweḍ  s  azaɣer  ad  yekrez,  yemmut  ɣef
lmaɛun:  d  kra  ifellaḥen  i  t-yufan  yeqqur  ɣef  umekraz.  Teɣli-d  rriba  ɣef  at
167
Ammud n tullisin
wexxam,  rnu,  ḥeznen  mačči  d  kra.  Ladɣa,  Wezna,  ulac  win  i  tt-yuggaren  ayen
tru,  tɣaḍ  akk  medden.  Ulac  win  ixemmemen  ula  d  tadqiqt  d  nettat  i  yenɣan
Aɛmer: la at wexxam, la imdanen n beṛṛa. Maca medden akk cukken yella kra i
d-yekkan si tama n Ujendi acku Aɛmer ur yuḍin ara, llan wid yettekka di twizi
iḍelli-nni, ččan akken, xedmen akken, ur tufiḍ i ten-yuɣen. Di tallit-nni yiwen ur
yeẓri d acu yeḍran mačči am tura llan ṭṭebba ad ggen lututtsi, ad ak-d-inin argaz-
a ma d l’arsenic, d thalium neɣ d ssem nniḍen i swayes yemmut.
Awejhan yeɛdda fell-as uzaylal. Yuɣal ula d lmenteq yettgami a t-id-yali.
Icukket  ansi  i  yas-d-tekka  tyita:  yeččat  kan  ɣer  daxel  issusem.  Qqaren  at  zik
yiwen  n  lemtel  ttfakkan  i  yis  tamacahut  nni  winna  yewwten  wayeḍ  s  teylet
yenɣa-t:  ḥala win  yewwten d win  yettewwten  i  yeẓran  d acu  yellan  di teylewt,
ma d iferr n weslen neɣ d aqḍib n waldun. Awejhan yeḥseb iman-is ula d netta d
win yettewten, iḥulfa-yas i weqḍib n waldun mi yers deg wexxam-is. Ɣas akken
tiyita  s  mmi-s  i  tegla  maca  iḥulfa-yas  tura.  Anager  yiwen  weqcic  kan  i  yas-d-
yeqqimen,  Yidir  aɛzizen  ḥala  netta  a  d-yegrin  d  awṛit.  Ur  ilaq  ara  ad  yemmet,
ilaq ad yidir, ad yeqqim d axalaf n Uwejhan. Awejhan yella deg wawal izem  n
tizza, ur ilaq ara ad yenger uẓar-is.
Awejhan  yerna-t  leḥzen  d  lḥir.  Yeḥzen  imi  aqcic  i  ɣef  iɛetteb  acḥal  d
aseggas  akken  a  t-id-yessker,  iṛuḥ  am  tqeṭiṭ  lɛid.  Lḥir  imi  win  d-yeqqimen
mazal-it  d  ilemẓi  ḥala  ɛecrin  di  leɛmer-is,  ur-ɛad  yewwiḍ  d  argaz  izemren  ad
ibedd ɣef wexxam.
Kra  n  wussan  akken  yenṭel  Aɛmer,  Awejhan  yeqqim  deg  useqqif
yesseḥmuy, mi d-yekcem Yidir yessawel-as. Mi d-yusa Yidir yenna-yas i baba-
s:
-  Anɛam a baba ! d acu tebɣiḍ ?
Yenna-yas wemɣar nni s taɣect-is tarqaqt :
-Qim a mmi ad tesseḥmuḍ, ahat yenɣa-k qajjar, qim !
168
Ammud n tullisin
Yeɛdda Yidir iddem-d takarsit, yuẓa-d ɣer lkanun. Issawel wemɣar i tmeṭṭut-
is, yenna-yas:
-  Wa Lǧuher ! yya efk-as-d i mmi-m lqehwa ad isew…
Ciṭ akka tkecmed tmeṭṭut-is s ubeqraj n lqahwa d snat teɣrifin deg uḍebsi d
yiwet  n  tcabcaqt  teččur  d  akeffay  yettkuffut  akken  kan  i  t-id-teẓẓeg  si  taɣat.
Tessers-d  kulci  zdat  mmi-s  terra  akken  ad  teffeɣ  dɣa  inṭeq  ɣer-s  wergaz-is
yenna-yas:
-   Ah !... Aniwer ?
-   Ad ṛuḥeɣ ad ɛiwneɣ Wezna di leqdic…
Dɣa yerra-yas wergaz-is :
-  Anef-as, inaɣ tessen ad tegg imensi, anef-as; teqqimeḍ ad tesweḍ tajeɣɣimt n
lqehwa yid-neɣ…
Dɣa  teqqim  tmeṭṭut  nni  ɣaf  tkersit  tellha  a  d-tessurug  lqehwa  s  ifenǧalen
yellan di ssniwa. Terna teddem-d yiwen i yiman-is si tṛeffit. Yenna-yas Awejhan
i mmi-s :
-  A  mmi,  tura  gma-k  yemmut,  ad  yettwarḥem,  yessetma-k  atentan  akk  s
yexxamen nnsent, ḥala kečč i d-yeqqimen d ilemẓi, nek aql-ih ɣef tizi n lmut
ma  mačči ass-a, azekka a yi-tejlaq. Ihi qbel ad  mmteɣ bɣiɣ a k-waliɣ terriḍ
axxam, ad ak-feṛḥeɣ akken feṛḥeɣ i gma-k. acu i tenniḍ a tamɣart ?...
Tamɣart uɣent-d wallen-is, acḥal aya tura mi tebɣa ad twali mmi-s amaẓuẓ
d isli: ahat seg wasmi yesɛa xemseṭṭac neɣ seṭṭac iseggasen. Tenna-yas :
-  D tidet ! D tidet ay amɣar ! Ih ! d ayen iwulmen…
Yenna-yas Uwejhan i mmi-s :
-
Ihi  a  mmi  ṛṛay  attan  ɣer-k,  muqel  ma  tebɣiḍ  ad  tzewǧeḍ  aseggas-a  neɣ  ad
terǧuḍ ar qabel… Muqel tin i k-yehwan di teqcicin n taddart-a neɣ di tuddar
nniḍen tessneḍ neɣ ma tella yiwet si tyessetmatin n imeddukal-ik i k-iɛeǧben
ini-yaneɣ-d, a neddu ɣer imawlan-is…
169
Ammud n tullisin
Dɣa tamɣart nni tegzem-as-d awal :
-  Annaɣ ay amɣar, acuɣer a  nessexser  idrimen di  tmeɣra  nniḍen, ad  yerr kan
-  Ahat d ssuq nni nkent s tlawin i yefran, ssuq nneɣ nekni ur-ɛad, anef-aɣ a t-
nefru ihi akken iwulem lḥal. Nniɣ-as i Yidir ad yextiṛ tin iri d tin yexsa a yaɣ,
yanegma-s, yefra ssuq…
Awejhan yerfa, isuɣ :
mačči d tin tebɣiḍ kemmini…
Tamɣart terra-yas-d:
-  Annaɣ ay argaz, acu i txuss yanegma-s ?
Awejhan igzem-as awal:
a yaɣ…
Tamɣart terra-yas :
-  Nniɣ-as ad yefren netta tin iri netta, mačči d kemm i wumi nniɣ fren-as-d tin
-  Ay amɣar ula d nek d mmi, ilaq ad ḍebbreɣ fell-as, nekk d yanegma-s i bɣiɣ
a tt-yaɣ, ur tufiḍ acu n lɛib yellan ma yerra yanegma-s…
Awejhan yenna-yas :
-  Ula  d  nekk  d  mmi,  meɛna  ur  cerreḍeɣ  ara  fell-as  ad  yaɣ  ta  neɣtin,  bɣiɣ  d
netta  a  izewǧen  i  iman-is  mačči  d  kemm  ad  as-yesbibben  tameṭṭut  ahat
werǧin tt-iḥemmel…
Tameṭṭut nni terra-yas-d :
-  Hhee ! xaṭi ! nekk bɣiɣ ad yerr yanegma-s !
Awejhan yenna-yas :
-  Ur t-testeqsaḍ ara ula akken ad am-d-yini ma yebɣa-tt neɣ xaṭi…
Tameṭṭut-is terra-yas:
-  Ḥala beqqu a tt-yebɣu, ur tufiḍ acu i txuṣṣ yanegma-s ama di lqedd, di ḍḍrafa
neɣ di ccbaḥa, yerna yessen-itt, ḥala aɛǧab ara as-d-teɛǧeb !
Awejhan yerfa, isuɣ :
170
Ammud n tullisin
-  Aa wi ! isaṛ akka ! D aya kan i twalaḍ, ur twalaḍ ara yanegma-s-agi tugar-it
di leɛmer…
Tegzem-as-d awal tmeṭṭut-is :
-  Acexlaf ! Ula d kečč tuggareḍ-iyi s xemsa iseggasen maca tuɣeḍ-iyi…
Awejhan inṭew s igenni, yerra-yas :
-  A ddin ṛṛeb ! D argaz i ilaq ad yagger tameṭṭut mačči d tameṭṭut a yaggaren
-  Bla Rebbi ma yuɣ-itt i lukan a tekk ddunit yiwwas ! Ad iruḥ netta ad yextiṛ
argaz…
Dɣa tenna-yas tmeṭṭut-is :
-  Xaṭi !... Ihi, nekk ed yerr yanegma-s…
Awejhan isuɣ tikelt nniḍen, yebda sseb:
tin i yas-yehwan, d tin a yaɣ !...
Tameṭṭut-is tenna-yas:
-  Aha n nẓer ! ma mačči d yanegma-s a yaɣ !...
Awejhan yenna-yas :
-  A tamcumt henna-yaɣ, inaɣ kemm mačči bessif iyi-tuɣeḍ, d kemm iyi-bɣan.
Nekk  daɣen  ur  iyi-kem-id-qqinen  ara  imawlan-iw  ɣur-I  s  ẓẓur.  Ihi  anef  i
mmi-m  ad  yerr  ddunit-is  ɣef  yiman-is.  Amezwaru,  tḥettmeḍ-as-d  yelli-s  n
weltma-m  ma  d  wagi  dayen  berka  !  Yidir  ad  yezweǧ  iman-is,  ad  yaɣ  tin  i
yas-yehwan, tebɣiḍ neɣ tuggiḍ. Taggar n wawal mačči d kemm a izewǧen, d
netta…
Tamɣart  teffeɣ  s  zzeɛf,  ur  iban  acu  n  wawal  i  d-tesxewter  d  aneggaru.
Terra  ɣer  wexxam,  tufan  wezna  teǧǧa  aṛdam  n  seksu,  tuẓa-d  ɣer  tnebḍant  n
tewwurt a d-tesmeḥsis, dɣa tsuɣ fell-as :
-  Aḥlil  ! kem tura newwi-kemm id i leqdic neɣ i wesmeḥses ɣer tewwura ! –
Aha llhi-d d ccɣel-im…
Wezna tuɣal d tazeggaɣt, teḥṣa yesla-d wemɣar-is.
Deg useqqif Awejhan yezzi ɣer mmi-s, iwala-t am win yeffeɣ ṛṛuḥ, yenna-yas :
171
Ammud n tullisin
-  Aha  !  sew  lqehwa-yik  ahat  tuɣal  d  tasemmaṭ  !  ur  smeḥsis  ara  i  yemma-k.
lecɣal  n  yergazen  ḥala  irgazen  i  ten-iferrun,  ma    d  ssuq  nnsent  yexḍa-yaɣ.
Muqqel  kan  tin  tebɣiḍ  akken  i  yak-nniɣ,  ayen  nniḍen  yexḍa-k  ṛṛay…
Yemma-k a tt-iɛeddi zzeɛf ad teddem tamḥellest ad tezwir zdat-i…
Zrin wussan…
Awejhan ifaq-as i tmeṭṭut n mmi-s, tetteḥṛiṛit ur iban ayen, dɣa yessufeɣ-as
taɛessast : kra a yekk wass nett a d-yezg ger tselnin anda ur t-id-yettwali yiwen.
Ilaq ad iẓer acu yuɣen Wezna acku yesla  ɣer medden, mačči d abrid neɣ d sin,
tettaḍsa-yas  i  Ujendi  neɣ  tettanṭaq  ɣer-s…  Yessusem  ur  d-yenna  acemma  ɣas
akken ula d netta iwala-tt yiwen webrid tḍegger-as awal neɣ sin…
Si  tɛessast  nni  ines  anda  iqeggel  i  tt-iwala  di  tlemmast  uzal  a  tetteddu
xmat-xmat,  tezger  i  ẓẓerb,  tekka  ɣer  tmazirt  Ujendi  truḥ  qbala  s  axxam-is.
Awejhan yerra ɣer tzeqqa-s, yessawel i tmeṭṭut-is d mmi-s yenna-yasen ddan-d
yid-s ɣer ger tselnin. Yenna-yasen :

anekcum i tkeččem s axxam Ujendi…

tebɣiḍ, tura ur d-heddeṛ ara ɣef ayen ur twalaḍ neɣ ur teẓriḍ…

di  teswiɛt:  Wezna,  d  nettat  i  yenɣan  Aɛmer  (neɣ  tettekka  di  tmenɣiwt-is  ?)…

Yiwen  wass  Meqran  yekcem  ɣer  lqehwa  n  Yidir  am  ikerri  nni  yewwet
ṭaglal.  Ula  d  ibeddi  ur  izmir  ara  ad  ibedd,  iban  d  acu  n  texnact  i  deg  i  tt-
yesdenden  netta  d  imeddukal-is  armi  ad  as-qqaren  i  taɣaṭ  ‘ecc  akin  !’  ɣilen  d

amkan, yeqqim.

ayen i dak-iṛuḥen. Kker, nadi, ddu, steqsi,ekk-d timura ahat yiwen wass ad tafeḍ
win  i  ɣef  a  tettnadiḍ…  Maca  teqqimeḍ  kan  dagi  amek  tebɣiḍ  a  t-id-temlileḍ  ?

awezɣi. Ur ttḥiri ara, kra n win yeddan s ttawil yessaweḍ tikli-s. A k-iniɣ acu i
ɣ-yenna baba yiwen wass, dayen ur tesliḍ maca ma ad fakkeɣ awal ad tfehmeḍ

i d tifrat-is. Ḥsiɣ d Wezna i das-iggan asečči, maca mačči n nettat i t-inɣan d win
i  yas-d-yefkan  asečči,  i  yas-ikellxen  i  t-yenɣan.  D  tidet,  Wezna  teḍlem  attan  a
tettxelliṣ:  argaz-is  tečča  aqerru-yis,  inexḍaben  gguman  ad  qerrben  ɣer-s,  win
yeslan tin tegga i Aɛmer-iw, ad yerwel acku yuggad ma yuɣ-itt i mmi-s ad as-t-
tneɣ… Ajendi semmeḍ wul-is imi yekkes axṣim-is melba ma uzwaɣen ifassen-

is.  Yedder  di  lfeṛḥ  d  zzhu,  nekk  ddreɣ  di  leḥzen  d  wurfan.  Gulleɣ  s  limin  ur

wid i t-yecban.
Tecfam-as-d  i  Ḥnini  n  Muḥend  u  Remḍan.  Ihi  d  Ḥnini  nni  ḥeqqren  akk
medden  iyi-yefkan  ttawil  rriɣ-d  ttaṛ  i  mmi.  ẓriɣ  tekṛeh  Ajendi  acku  yeḥwes-as

yettaweḍ-itt-id waḍu  nni  ines, tesxewtir, tettnaɣ d  medden, teggan di  lǧameɛ…

taleqqimt n weɣrum… Taseɛdit tettceggiɛ-it ad as-tawi isɣren neɣ ayen nniḍen,

kra  yeḍran,  yemmeččen… deg wexxam Ujendi  ẓriɣ-t… D agguren akka. Asmi
iyi-tenna Ḥnini: Ajendi ad yinig ɣer Lezzayer ass n leflani. Nniɣ-as deg wul-iw
ihi d tidet ad yinig maca s anda ur d-yettuɣal. Ṛǧiɣ, simmal d yettaqrab wass-nni
simmal lferḥ yettnerni deg wul-iw.
Yiweḍ-d wass-nni n yinig n Ujendi, kkreɣ deg yiḍ ṛuḥeɣ zwareɣ s abrid n
tniri acku ẓriɣ seg-s ad iɛeddi akken ad yerkeb di lkaṛ. Qqimeɣ a ttraǧuɣ melmi

Ammud n tullisin
Tadyant n mmi-s uciban
Tadyant-agi  i  d-iteddun  cfiɣ  qqaren-tt-id  asmi  lliɣ  meẓzẓiyeɣ  di  taddart-
nneɣ, qqaren-tt  imawlan  i warraw-nsen  mi ara ten-ttrebbin,  mi ara ten-ttweṣṣin
ad  xedmen  ayen  yelhan.  Qqaren-tt  acku  d  yiwen  wemɣar  n  wedrum  n  taddart
iwumi  teḍra,  maca  ciṭ  n  yemdanen  i  yeẓran  d  anwa.  Tadyant  ur  tt-qqaren  ara
medden mi ara d-ttmeslayen ɣef ttar akked tiririt-is, maca qqaren-tt-id ɣef wayen
yelhan, ɣef webrid igerrzen.
Cfiɣ-as am wass-a i tallit deg iyi-tenna yemma tadyant n mmis Uciban, ur
cfiɣ ara acu i d ssebba n wawal, bdan at wexxam tmeslayen-d ɣef win ixeddmen
ayen  yelhan  d  win  ixeddmen  ayen  n  diri.  Yal  wa  d  anta  i  d-yettawi,  yal  wa
lemtel i ɣer ixemmem, yal wa tamacahut i yessen: wa, tin n tiḥerci d nneyya, wa
tin  inisi,  wa  tin  n  teqcict  d  yizem…  beddren-d  imdanen  ifazen,  lefḥul,  wid
yecban Ḥmed Umerri.
tbaṭel ɣef imeɣban…
Ladɣa ɣef Ḥmed Umerri, tenna nanna, ɣas ineqq lqeggad werǧin yesɛedda
Yuzzel  yiḍ,  beṛṛa  tillas  selɣent  yalci,  tiṭ  ur  tezmir  ad  tẓer  ayen  yellan  ɣef
azal n lmitra. Adfel yessa s leɛqel. Asemmiḍ igezzem ikesman, lukan albeɣḍ ad
yewqeɛ  ad  yequjjer  d  lmut  ara  t-yeddmen.  Deg  wexxam  azɣal  yeseftutes  kra
yellan  d  aḥunǧer,  iqjemyaṛ  ukerruc  reqqen  di  tkuzunt  neɣ  di  lkanun.  Abbu
yettali  ad  yeffeɣ  si  kra  n  uqadus  yulin  d  asawen  ɣef  ssqef,  maca  imi  yiwet  n
tama ur tezmiḍ ara aṭas, iteffeɣ-d ciṭ n wabbu tama n ssqef, ɣas akken iteffeɣ si
teḍwiqt nni yellan di lḥiḍ, kra din yeḍla-yas iselwan.
Aciban d yiwen wergaz ur d-yettwabdaren ara di taddart ḥala deg wayen
yelhan. Ur t-id-ttaddren ara medden deg waṭas n tmucuha maca ḥala deg yiwet.

Ammud n tullisin
Yiwet kan s ways yettwassen. Tinna beṛka. Ulac ababat yekkren ad iweṣṣi mmi-
s ur as-id-yenni ara imeslayen yenna Uciban.
Aciban  yesɛa  yiwen  n  mmi-s. Iṛebba-t-id am warrac  n taddart:  yemmal-as
leqder,  yessken-as  iseɣ,  iwehha-yas-d anwa i d abrid  n  lḥerma. Meẓyan  mmi-s
Uciban  yeḍfer  kra  i  d-as-yenna  baba-s,  yesɛedda  ussan-is  di  lehna.  Yenwa
yessen kra yellan di ddunit, neɣ xerṣum yessen kra ilaqen ad t-yissin yilemẓi am
netta  ur  yeffiɣen  ara  di  lebda  ɣer  temdint  n  Lezzayer  neɣ  ɣer  tmurt  n  Fṛansa.
Yedder  di  lehna,  ur  yesɛi  aɣilif,  ur  yessin  urrif.  Seg  wasmi  meẓẓiy  yettɛawan
baba-s  di  lqehwa:  yettɛawan-it  deg  uheggi,  di  tarda  n  leḥwal,  deg  wefraḍ  n
tḥanut… Werǧin i d-tella kra n temsalt ger-as d baba-s.
Maca ma yella ur d-tella ara kra temsalt dɣa dayen akken kan ara teddu ddunit.
Lhemm ur teẓriḍ ansi ara d-iṣuḍ, urrif ur teẓriḍ ansi ara d-yekk. ɣef aya ladɣa i
ilaq ɣef wemdan ad d-yezg d aɛessas yal ass. Ilaq ad yessikkid anda ara yessrus
iḍarren-is:  yezmer  ad  yili  d  agris  i  yukel,  ad  yewwet  iɣisi  ad  t-ččen  waman,
yezmer  ad  yili  d-tixmirt  i  deg  yedda  ad  yecceḍ,  ad  awḍen  iguma-is  ɣer  tegnit.
Dimi  yelha win  iteddun s  leɛqel, diri aɣiwel  yettawin bab-is ɣer  uɣelluy.  Awal
aneggaru d win n Ccix Muḥend u Lḥusin: “win ur nuzzil, leɛmer yendim, meɛna
leɛmer yeddim”.
Yeɣli-d ṭṭlam berra mi d-yekcem yiwen wergaz ɣer lqehwa. Meẓyan yenwa
d yiwen i d-yewwi webrid yenɣa-t usemmiḍ dɣa yekcem-d axaṭer di tegrest ciṭ n
yemdanen  i  yettɛeṭṭilen  ɣer  wurar  n  ddiminu  neɣ  lkarṭa,  aṭas  ikelyanen
(imsaɣen) d win ara d-ikecmen ad swen lqehwa neɣ llatay, ad qessṛen ciṭ mbeɛd
ad  ruḥen.  Asemmiḍ  d  yiḍ  i  d  iɣellin  zik  iḥettem  lɣaci  ad  tnejmaɛen  zik  s
ixxamen nnsen. Maca akelyan-agi n tmeddit-a ur yettwassen ara di taddart yusa-
d si tama akkin i tiɣilt, yeqqim ɣer ṭṭabla, yekmanda lqehwa, issusem.
Yessaɣ agarru yeqqim a yessikid aqehwaǧi seddaw ttiṭ.

Ammud n tullisin
Yeɣli-d  yiḍ,  ffɣen  akk  wid  yettɣiman  di  lqehwa  ḥala  argaz-nni  i  d-yeggran.
Iɛedda ɣer-s Meẓyan, yesteqsa-t ma yella win i yettraǧu neɣ i wumi yefka ttiɛad.

Meẓyan yewhem, argaz-agi mačči n taddart-nsen, d tikelt tamezwarut ara t-iẓer.

-Acu i k-id-yecqan ihi ?
Yenna-yas winna:

-D lxir kan, inaɣ ?

-D lxir kan a mmi !
yas :

t-kkseɣ si ddinit…

Meẓyan yettmuqul-it kan, winna ikemmel awal.
-Ihi  tamsalt-agi  tewɛer  aṭas  maca  ma  tɛawneḍ-iyi  ad  ak-muddeɣ  azal  n  wayen
ara d-tḥerreḍ di 10 neɣ 15 iseggasen n lxedma di lqehwa inek.

-Tamsalt-inu teshel ma tɛawneḍ-iyi aṭas n yedrimen ara d-trebḥeḍ deg-s. Mebla
ma ntezzi ntenneḍ ad ak-tt-id-iniɣ d acu-tt: d yiwen i yellan d axṣim-iw, bɣiɣ ad

Yenna-yas Meẓyan:
Yenna-yas winna:
-“A laṭif !, ad aɣ-yemneɣ Ṛebbi si temgaṛt !
- Mca, ad trebḥeḍ ayen swayes ara tesɛeddiḍ ddunit-ik meṛṛa !

- Xaṭi, xḍiɣ, ḥala aya ur xeddmeɣ ara !
Winna yemmeɣ ɣer lǧib ubalṭun-is iddem-d ameqqun n yedrimen yenna-yas:
-  Ax  tura  wigi  ṭṭef-iten,  a  tt-ih  tqerɛet-agi  deg-s  bala  ma  nniɣ-ak…  xemmem,
meyyez, ma isuɛed-ik ihayen, mulac err-iyi-ten-id.”
Yeffeɣ winna, yessegra-yas-d awal:
-  Ma  yella  tqebleḍ,  ad  ak-d-rnuɣ  ɛecra  neɣ  ɛecrin  imuren  am  win.  Ma  yella
tqebleḍ…
Meẓyan amzun di targit i yella yettezzi deg wallaɣ-is wawal-agi “ma yella
tqebleḍ…”. Yettezzi, yettenneḍ, yugi ad as-yebru. Yessakked deg yedrimen nni.
Yuggad, ma yefka-yas-d walbaɛḍ anecta n wedrim, azal n wayen d yettḥelli deg
useggas, iqder armi yewɛer aṭas ccɣel-agi. Di leɛmeṛ-is ur ixemmem ɣer ssuma
n wemdan, ass-nni ixemmem: ziɣ d tidet imdanen ɣlayit ma yella yezmer yiwen
ad yefk anect-agi n yedrimen akken ad ineɣ albeɛḍ waqila ihi wagi yeswa.
Iṛuḥ  deg  usmuzgem  imiren  ɣef  wazal  n  wemdan  amzun  yekcem  timura  i  ɣef
rezzun yemdanen deg tirga.
axxam.
Yemmekta-d  di  lqehwa  i  yella,  yeɣli-d  yiḍ  ilaq  ad  isekkeṛ  tawwurt  ad  iruḥ  s

axxam. Mi yiweḍ yufa ttraǧun-t at wexxam akken ad ččen imensi akken.

Meẓyan i baba-s:
ḥareɣ amek ara xedmeɣ…

-Ihi, uɣal ula d tameddit-a, ens daɣ din…
Meẓyan  yerfed  iman-is,  yerna  yerfed  ussu-nni  n  tmara,  yeffeɣ.  Yensa  di
tqernit n ṛṛef n lǧameɛ n taddart. Ttɛeddin yemdanen, ttuɣalen, yiwen ur yecliɛ
deg-s,  yiwen  ur  t-yesteqsa  acimi  yensa  beṛṛa.  Mi  d-tewweḍ  tewlellest  n  tifawt,
yekker yerra ɣer lqehwa ad yessarbi ikelyanen  imezwura ara iṛuḥen ad xedmen
deg icantiyen n lebni di Buɣni neɣ di Tizi-Wezzu.
Llan kra n leɛmum-is d xwal-is yerzan ɣer baba-s deg wass nnan-as acuɣer i
tḍerqeḍ  mmi-k  seg  wexxam,  ɣilen  d  aḍraq  i  t-yeḍraq.  Aciban  ur  tufiḍ  acu  i
yasen-yenna, uɣalen ur fhimen tigert acku mi steqsan Meẓyan ayen yeggan ɣer
wefrag  n  lǧameɛ  yenna-yasen  d  baba-s  i  yas-id-yennan  ur  tegganeḍ  ara  deg
wexxam. Maca Meẓyan ur asen-d-yebdir ara awal ɣef ssebba n waya.
Tameddit  n  wass  yerra  Meẓyan  s  axxam,  tessers-as-d  yemma-s  imensi,
yečča. Mi ifukk, yenna-yas baba-s :

yewwet, neɣ ad k-yeḥqer di tejmiɛt ?

- Ula yiwen ur d-yerri. Acuɣer a baba ?
Aciban yenna-yas :
- Ihi, ula d tameddit-a ṛuḥ ens daɣen din ad teẓreḍ…
Meẓyan  yega  akken  yennum,  yensa  ddaw  tdarit  n  lǧameɛ  n  taddart.  At
taddart  akk  slan,  wehmen  mi  ara  t-yesteqsi  welbeɛḍ  yeqqar-as  kan  d  baba  i  d-
yennan ens da, nsiɣ da.

neɣ ma ulac a-tan-leɛmum-is akked xwal-is ad t-awin ad yeggan ɣer-sen. Aciban
yenn-yasen-d yiwen wawal:
-Anfet-as, akka ad yissin d acu d ddunit…

Ammud n tullisin
