ur asen-texḍimeḍ ara ayen n diri… anda tebɣuḍ tedduḍ, anda i k-yehwa tenseḍ,
d laman, yiwen ur k-id-yettaweḍ, ur tettaggadeḍ ara anda tensiḍ ad yali wass…
Maca limer tenɣiḍ amdan, ad yeffeɣ wawal deg useggas, di sin, dim raw… yella
win  yeẓran  melmi ara  yeffeɣ wawal. Imawlan d tarwa  n wid tenɣiḍ ɣef tejɛelt,
ad nadin ad d-rren ttaṛ acku anza ur yettsusum arma yuɣ-it walbaɛḍ, ladɣa anda
teddiḍ ur tetthenniḍ, ur tegganeḍ, ur tettafeḍ talwit. Terẓeg ad d-taɣ ussa-ik, anef
ɛad tura layas… Ad k-yeḍfer lḥal arma ad teqqimeḍ ɣer nnig lkanun am tura ad
tettargagiḍ, ad as-tiniḍ tura ad d-asen ad iyi-nɣen…

Ad gen tameɣra
Di  kra  n  teswiɛin,  yessawaḍ  umdan  s  ufelleq  arama  yeṭṭerdeq  dɣa  ad  d-
yeglu  s  txessart  i  kra  n  wid  i  t-id-iqerben  neɣ  ahat  i  yiman-is.  Ger  wiggad  i
yettnekkaren ttḥuddun ayen bnan d wayen bnan wiyiḍ, aḥeddad n Lqalus nni ɣef
yura  Mulud  At  Maɛmer  deg  isefra  n  zik  n  Leqbayel,  neɣ  iɣef  yecna  Mennad,
neɣ i d-yesedda Muḥya di tsuqilt n tmezgunt-nni n Luksun: ‘Le ressucite’, tinna
i wumi isemma netta Muḥend u Ceɛban, ladɣa d amedya yettwessnen aṭas.
Amdan-agi  ladɣa,  yerra  ɣer  daxel  armi  ur  yezmir  ara,  yenfel-d  yessedrem
taddart, Lqalus trab ḥala isem-is i d-yeqqimen d awal.
Llan kra  mi d-ṭṭreḍqen ad faḍen am  uḥemmal  nni  ur  nesɛi aḥkim, ad ččen
tiɣezza, izuɣar d lewḍayat, ad zedren ɣer yill ur nesɛi lqaɛ…
Acu yessawḍen imdanen ad rekkmen neɣ ad ttayzagen am qeḍran n yingel
i  deg  yeṭṭef  ujajiḥ  ?  Di  tmurt  nneɣ  aṭas  i  ixussen  tamussni,  aṭas  i  d-yekkren
meẓẓyit,  kkren  ad  sselḥun  iderma  d  tuddar  nitni  tamussni  ur  d-yewwi  wara.
Mačči d lebɣi i nebɣa ad nini ilmeẓyen ur ssinen ara akken llan maca aṭas deg-
sen  xḍan  i  tmussni  n  ddunit.  “Mačči  d  allen  kan,  tamuɣli  n  wid  i  tt-yesɛan”,
akken  yeqqar  umedyaz.  Aṭas  n  teswiɛin  a  teqqareḍ  i  wid  iḥaren:  kra  n  win
yettazzalen s leḥmeq ad tt-id-yečč ɣef uxenfuc, nitni ulac ula d timesliwt ! win
ur  nezmir  yeqqar  zemreɣ,  win  ur  nessin  yeqqar  ssneɣ,  win  ur  neẓri  ad  ak-yini
ẓriɣ…  Dɣa  d  aya  i  aɣ-id-yewwin  ɣer  tegnit  am  ta:  nuɣal  nettemberraz  am
yilfan…
Akli  u  Muḥ  d  argaz  i  tewwi  lmizirya  nni  n  iseggasen  n  30-40  ad  yezger

yessas  kra  swayes  yesfeḍ  llaẓ  i  wat  wexxam,  yerra-d  tiferkiwin  yenzan,  yerna
Deg  wezɣal  kan  i  d-yettas.  Imir  ladɣa  i  yejweǧ;  yerna  ciṭ  rnan  ɣer-s  sin
Fṛansa  yegguma  ad  tt-yeffeɣ,  d  nettat  i  yas-id-yettakken  taleqqimt-nni  n

Atmaten-is rran axxam mbeɣd mi mmuten yimɣaren. Arraw n Wakli u Muḥ ur
d-myezgen  ara  nitni  d  leɛmum  nsen.  Teɣli-d  teɛdawt  ger-asen,  qqlen  amzun  d
idurar. Ma d  Akli  yigi ad  yebḍu d watmaten-is segmi  yal anebdu  mi ara d-yas
irezzu fell-asen ad ten-id-iẓer.
Yiwen  useggas,  heggan  warra-is  tameɣra  ad  d-awin  tislatin  deg  yiwen

lferḥ  nsen  ara  yilin  daɣ  d  lferḥ-is  imi  ara  iwali  arraw-is  gan  ixxamen  skud
yedder.
Mi qrib ad d-yeweḍ wass n tmeɣra, qqimen wat wexxam a temcawaren ɣef
wid  ara  d-necden.  Yenna-yasen  Wakli:  “bɣiɣ  ad  d-necdeɣ  atmaten-iw  ɣer
tmeɣra”. Arraw-is rfan, nnan-as: ‘ḥala tagi ur d-iḍerrunara, u ma llan di tmeɣra
atan nekkni ḥsu si tura tilin nneɣ tebṭel’…

i  yas-ffɣen afus. Yettkel ɣef tmeṭṭut-is ad t-id-tɛiwenad asen-tbeddel ṛṛay  maca
nutni  gguman  ad  aɣun  i  imawlan-nsen:  ṭṭfendeg  wawal-nsen  am  wemcic-nni
iḥewṣen  turret,  ɣas  ad  t-tezluḍ  mačči  ad  as-yebru.  Yeṭṭef-asen  lexwal-nsen,
tajmiɛt n twacult-nsen… Ulac, uggin ad d-rren ‘ṣahu’.
Yewweḍ-d  wass  n  tmeɣra,  taddart  akk  teggujid-d  ɣer  waxxam  n  Wakli,
usan-d  imeddukal  i  izedɣen di tudrin  nniḍen d wid  n temdinin.  Sked win  ur d-
nerzi, ḥala atmaten n Wakli, qqimen kan mmuɣebnen, terna iɣaḍ-iten gma-tsen i
rnan warraw-is. Tebda tmeɣra: d urar n tlawin seg iḍinizeryen, tid akk yessnen
ccna  ttwanecdent-d.  ta  tekkat  amendayer,  ta  tceṭṭeḥ…  ccnawi  ttifriren-d.  ma  d

Ammud n tullisin
Netta aya diri-t acku ur ilaq ara ad tḍurreḍ win yettamnen s tneslemt skud i

lḥal ɣef ccnawi.

Muḥ  u  Mḥend.  Yiwen  seg  yisefra-agi  yeɛǧeb-as  aṭas  i  Wakli,  d  winna  anda
akken i yas-yeqqar :
Ay ul-iw ṣber i usemmiḍ
Mi d-teɣlin ger-asen
Maca  Akli  ulamek  yeṣber,  yebda  yettmekti-d  temẓi-s,  yemmekta-d  lḥif  d
lmizirya i yesɛeddad imawlan-is, d watmaten-is…
“…  Ttruḥun  kessen  akken,  beṭṭun  ciṭ  nni  n  teḥbult  n  weɣrum  i  yasen-tegga
yemma-tsen,  ma  ulac  ttɣeẓẓen  bibṛas,  gemmren-d  felgu  d  lḥeswa,  ssekfalen-d

nsen imɣaren. ɛawnen Akli di lebni n wexxam, ɛawnen-t di zzwaǧ. Yecfa-d akk

iqebbel wul wala allaɣ…”
Akli yezder di ttexmam, yettezzi rewwint deg wallaɣ-is.

acku d netta i d-yewwi ad yeqqen lḥenni i warraw-is, ur iban anda yedda: ulac-it
di  lḥara,  ur  yeffiɣ  ara  ɣer  lqehwa,  ulac  win  yeẓran  ma  yella  waniwer  yerra.
Ffɣen  warraw-is  d  kra  inebgawen  ttnadin.  Ufan-t,  iɛelleq  iman-is  s  umrar  ɣef
yiwet n teslent ger tbucicin yellan deffif wexxam.
Akka i teḍra d wid ikkren ad d-gen tameɣra, taggara… gan tameɣra !
Akka i ttgen wid ur nessin…

Ammud n tullisin
Tuɣalin
1.
Akken  kan  i  d-tekker  seg  wussu,  Sekkura  terra  biha-biha  ɣer  s  aɣalad.
Teddem-d  acabcaq  n  waman  ad  tessired  udem-is  d  ifassen-is.  Mi  tfukk  tarda,
terfed-d  tameqqunt  n  yesɣaren  tesfaccet-iten  ɣer  lkanun.  Tessaɣ-asen  times  s
tecwawt i wumi tessaɣ s tkebrit mbaɛd mi tt-tebbeẓ di zzit. Deg yiwet n tikkelt
yuli  ujajiḥ  deg  igenni,  tfeǧǧeǧ  akk  texxamt-nni  usewwi  ad  as-tiniḍ  d  iṭij  i  d-
yewwten ɣer-s ɣas akken di berra mazal ṭṭlam, tafat n wass urɛad d-tban. Yebda
wabbu yettaččar taxxamt-nni, allen n Sekkura serrḥent s imeṭṭi. temmeɣ teddem-
d amegruc a t-tesrus-it ɣef yiran n lkanun, syin d akkin terra inyen fell-as.
Terra  ɣer  s  addaynin,  takasrunt  deg  ufus.  Tefka  i  taɣaṭ  tummeẓt  n  weslen
akken ad tezhu deg-s, tekkes-as imir taculliṭ-nni i yas-tetteg yal ass akken ur tt-
teṭṭḍen  ara  sin  nni  yiɣiden  imecṭaḥ.  Teṭṭanez,  yiwen  ufus  yeṭṭef  takasṛunt,
wayeḍnin iteẓẓeg, teqqar-as deg wul-is: “ṣṣbeḥ-agi aṭas uyefk i tejmeɛ taɣaṭ-iw,
timaẓẓagin-is  bɣant  ad  ṭṭreḍqent.  Ass-agi  arraw-iw  ad  ṛwun  akeffay,  ad  asen-
fkeɣ ad swen ayen bɣan !”. Teččur takasṛunt-nni, tɛedda tserreḥ-d i yiɣiden-nni
akken ad ṭṭden ayen i d-yeqqimen.
Teseww-d ayefk-nni s ufella n lkanun. Mbaɛd tɣumm-it, tekkes-it s ufella n
weḥnay. Truḥ tessaki-d argaz-is u tenna-yas:
-Kker ! atan waggur n yiṭṭij yuli deg igenni !. ilaq ass-agi ad nekfu ajṛaḍ usaɣur
deg Inyen n Weɣzen.
Yekker-d urgaz-is, mbeɛd mi yessared udem-is, tefka-yas-id akeffay simi ad
teww  lqehwa  i  terra  ɣef  tmes.  Terna,  tessenker-d  sin  warraw-is,  Weɛmer  d
Saɛid. Tefka-yasen ayefk ad swen. Saɛid yuza ɣer baba-s yettqessir yid-s. ma d
Weɛmer yerfed takersit akked ufenǧal-is yeqqim mbɛid ɣef lkanun.
Weɛmer  tura  ad  yili  yesɛa  14  iseggasen.  Si  zik  d  asusam  kan,  d  yemma-s
Sekkura kan i ɣer ineṭṭeq, d nettat i wumi yettaḍsa, ɣer-s kan i yettɣima… ula d
jeddi-s Lḥaǧ Qasi akked jidda-s Weṛdeyya, ur sen-ihedder ara: yekreh-iten.

Ammud n tullisin
Weɛmer  mačči  d  mmi-s  n  Lmulud,  argaz  n  Sekkura.  Aɛmer  d  mmi-s  n
Taqsiṭ  n  Weɛmer  mačči  am  tid  n  tezyiwin-is,  d  tamacahut  n  umeɣbun,
tessendaf ulawen n wid i as-yeslan. Amek i teḍra ?
Meqran.
2.
Di  kra  n  useggas  akken,  yemzawaǧ  Meqran  mmi-s  amenzu  n  Qasi  akked
Sekkura. Meqbel ad d-teddu ɣer-s, tuɣ-it yettxemmim yal ass amek i tga teqcict-
agi i yas-id-texḍeb yemma-s d xalti-s Jeǧǧiga. Yeḥsa kan isem-is Sekkura maca
di leɛmer-is ur tt-iwala. Yecfa tenna-yas xalti-s:
“Ammi, tecbeḥ, tezyen, terna d tasusamt. Ccɣel, ɛebbi fell-as ayen i ak-yehwan
ur  d-teqqar  ‘Aḥḥ!’.  yemma-s  temmut  asmi  i  tt-id-tesɛa,  d  jidda-s  i  tt-iṛebban
acku baba-s iɛawed zzwaǧ. Mi temmut jidda-s tegra-d ɣer yanababa-s…”.
Akken  kan  i  d-tedda  ɣer,  tekcem-as  ul-is,  yefreḥ  aṭas  yis-s,  nettat  daɣen,
tella leɛmer tefriḥ neɣ teḍsa; tura tuɣal tennecraḥ.
Tafsut i d-yezzin mbeɛd zzwaǧ-nnsen, ilul-d Weɛmer yerna-d lferḥ d lehna i
Sekkura d wergaz-is, akken feṛḥen yemɣaren ula d nitni. Maca lferḥ-agi ur idum
ara:  sin  wagguren  akken  ilul  Weɛmer,  Meqran  yeṭṭef-d  lkaɣeḍ  ad  d-yesɛeddi
lɛesker neɣ tiwizi n tmara, akken qqaren. Cegɛent ɣer tlisa. Aseggas amezwaru
sya ɣer da ad d-ṭṭfen tabrat-is wat wexxam, mbeɛd uɣalent tebratin nneqḍaɛent:
la tabrat, la lexbeṛ…
Yiwen  wass  deg  wussan  n  tegrest,  ddunit  akk  tettban-d  d  tacebḥant  seg
wedfel  ur tettwaliḍ ara  ula d  yiwen di beṛṛa, yaw a  yennejmaɛ. Sekkura tuɣ-itt
tettqeddir  isɣaren  deg  wefrag.  Tesla  i  lheffa  di  beṛṛa.  Akken  twulef  tɣil  d
Ḥemmama,  yiwet  n tjiratin-is  i d-yettsen tettɣima  yid-s  i  d-yusan tenṭeq ad as-
tini “Mreḥba yis-m ! Kcem !”.  Teṭṭerḍeq tewwurt, tessers taqabact, tṛuḥ teldi-tt-
id. Din din tsuɣ: “A yemma ɛzizen…”. Sekkura teɣli ɣef wemnaṛ n tewwurt…
Yers  usenduq  di  tesga,  ḥala  lewṣayef  n  Meqran  i  d-yettbanen  deffir  jjeǧ  n
yiwet  n  tama  usenduq.  Rnu  medden  ɣef  wergaz  i  ssnen.  Iru  Lḥaǧ  Qasi  d
XWedeya ɣef mmi-tsen. Iru Lmulud ɣef gma-s. Tru Sekkura ɣef wergaz-is i tt-

tessusem: ula d Lmulud ur as-teqqar ara txaq di kra n teswiɛt neɣ tettɣebben si
kra i d-yeḍran. Qbel zzwaǧ i tessen lmeḥna, temlal-d yid-s asmi tella meẓẓiyet.
Temxalaḍ yid-s uqbel ad tt-tefk tizi n tlatin.

sekra  yekka  wass  tettxemmim  ɣef  wayen  i  tesɛedda,  ɣef  wussan  iẓidanen  i
tedder akked Meqran. Ussan-nni ur d ttuɣalen. Ussan-nni yellan d tigzirt deg yill
n wussan ṛzagen.

tewwurt yesmeḥsis dɣa yesla i teḍsa tekka-d si daxel n wexxam-is. Yemmeɣ ɣer
lǧib  n  lbista  yeddem-d  tasarut  tis  snat  n  tewwurt,  tin  akken  i  d-ihegga  iḍin-
izeryen. Yeldi tawwurt yekcem, yesla  i teḍsa tekka-d si texxamt n tguni, yerra
ɣer  din.  Yekcem,  yeqqur  s  ibeddi  mi  iwala  tameṭṭut-is  ɛeryan  ger  ifassen  n
weqcic-nni  i  d-yeḍfer…  Aqcic  akken  i  d-iwala  Aṛeẓqi  iserreḥ  i  Feṭṭa  ɣef
umeṭreḥ, yebda a yettergigi. Ttmesmuqalen, amzun mraw iseggasen i iɛeddan di
ddunit-nsen…  Allen  n  Uṛeẓqi  urwent-d  aldun  yerɣan  mi  d-mlalent  d  tmuɣli  n
Feṭṭa, dɣa akken  i t-twala  latt-yettxezziṛ tserreḥ d  imeṭṭi acku tɣil ad tt-ineɣ ad
yernu aqcic-nni. Aṛeẓqi yezzi s ilemẓi-nni yenna-yas:
-Els iceṭṭiḍen-ik !
Aqcic am win a d-tekkseḍ seg imi n lmut, iḥuṛef yelsa aserwal, yerna atrikku
mbaɛd yekkes-it-id acku yeti-t, ad as-iɛawed timelsiwt… Aṛeẓqi yenna-yas:
Yemmeɣ  weqcic  ɣer  lǧib-is  yeddem-d  ɛecrin  duṛu,  yefka-yas-ten-id.  Aṛeẓqi
- Awi-d ɛecrin duṛu…
yenna-yas :
- Tura, nnejli, acu tettṛaǧuḍ ? Geffel !
Yeffeɣ weqcic-nni si texxamt; ddeqs zzalla, teṭṭerḍeq tewwurt n beṛṛa ḥala
tiɣri n warkasen ɣef trekkabin i wumi ara tesleḍ tama n usmicrew n Feṭṭa. Ahat
teḍra  yid-s  am  win  ara  d-tessukseḍ  si  tizi  n  lmut,  ahat  ad  ibeddel  tamezduɣt
werǧin d-ittezzi ara akaṛtyi-yagi.
Aṛeẓqi yettmuqul di tmeṭṭut-is, yesteqsay ma d nettat i d-nettat neɣ mačči
d nettat i d nettat. Ma d Feṭṭa tettru tugi ad tessusem. Inna-yas:
- Aha ! tura dayen ! Susem ! yya-d ɣur-i !...

tessetḥaḍ-iyi ?

ɣer tmurt. Yal ass ɣur-m i gganeɣ, ur ṭṭafareɣ ara sut iberdan, ur am-d-sekkreɣ
ara s axxam, ur kem-ttaǧǧaɣ ara weḥd-m  ad txiqeḍ: anda i rriɣ ad kem-awiɣ…
Ayen iyi txeḍɛeḍ ?...

yenneḍ-it i ɛecrin duṛu-nni, yenna-yas:

Iminig
1.
Ahat d tamert tis snat neɣ tis kradet n wass, di taddart ters-d tsusmi ur tufiḍ
zzhir iwumi ara tesleḍ, di beṛṛa d asemmiḍ, arrac ur qqimen ara deg izenqan ad
uraren am zik. Tura d taggara  n  lexṛif, d tagrest  i d-iteddun.  Tagnit tellexs seg
ugeffur i d-ikkaten. ɣer yel tiɣmert, aḍu yewwi iferrawen i d-iɣlin si ttjuṛ mi d-
iṣuḍ.  Aneznaz  yekkat,  tikwal  yettṣuḍu-d  ucelyaḍ.  Meqran  iḥulfa  i  qejjaṛ  deg
ifassen-is,  yerra-ten  ɣer  ubalṭun-is,  iteddu  allen-is  rsent  di  tegnit,  maca  ur  tt-
yettwali  ara…  yerna  ur  iceṭṭen  ara  ma  yeẓra-tt  neɣ  xaṭi.  Iteddu  deg  yiwen
wemḍiq,  yenneḍ di tqernit  n webrid  i  deg  i d-yelḥa.  yemmeɣ  yeddem-d agaṛṛu
yessaɣ-it,  iwexxeṛ  ɣef  yiwen  umdun  yellan  di  lewhi  n  tikli-s,  yejbed  yiwet  n
tikkelt, yerra-d nnehta mi d-isuḍ abbu n ugaṛṛu-nni amzun taɣect-is akka tedda-d
deg-s…
Mi yewweḍ ɣer zdat tseɣlit n  yiwen wexxam,  yessed  ɣef txelxalt yellan di
lḥiḍ. Ciṭ akka, yesla i wawal ad as-yeqqar : “Rǧu !”. Taɣect-agi issen-itt, iwalef-
itt  :  innum  isell-as,  ur  yecfi  ara  ɣef  tikkelt  tamezwarut  mi  d  as-yesla  iḍegger
agaṛṛu  ɣer  tegnit,  yukel-it,  yensa.  Ur  iɛeṭṭel  ara  yesla  i  leqfel  ad  yettwalday,
tawwurt temeṛzazeɣ. Yezzi, yunna udem, yuzwaɣ wudem-is si lferḥ… acḥal aya
ur  t-yessaked  d  ussan  neɣ  d  agguren,  ahat  nnig.  Udem  yecmumeḥ-d  ɣer-s  d
taḍsa, yesla tenna-yas: “azul fell-ak, kcem…”. Yerra fell-as azul, tiseɣlit tefka-t.
tefka-yas-d afus-is yufa-t yeḥma. Tenna-yas:
- Amek tettiliḍ ihi a Meqran, acḥal aya ur d-tusiḍ, yella kra i k-yuɣen ?
La t-testeqsay ma yella kra i t-yuɣen: ilindi tettaɣ-it tawla ɣef teswiɛt i deg
yella; ass-a, d urrif i d-yuɣen ul-is.
Yerra yekcem s axxam… yettmuqul deg udem-is yeḍsa-yas u yenna-yas:
-  Aql-akem  la  tettwaliḍ  a  Wenza,  am  zik  am  tura,  ur  tufiḍ  d  acu  i  ibeddlen.
Qqaren,  mačči  d  yiwet  neɣ  d  snat  tikwal  i  d-as-nniɣ  ad  awḍeɣ  ad  ten-id-ẓreɣ,

amkan yenna-yas deg wul-is: “Akken i yas-teqqar teqbaylit, ur texḍa ara, asirem

2.
Mačči  d  ayen  isehlen  ɣef  wemdan  a  t-yexdem  i  tetut  n  temẓi  maca  ula
akken  llan  wid  yebɣan  ad  ggen  tilas  i  wayen  i  d-iḍerrun,  ad  ḥebsen  lbaṭel  ur
yesserwat ara beṛṛa n wannar, ad slalen iseɣ d leḥerma akked lḥeqq; akka i teḍra
d Meqran  ma akken yewweḍ ɣer Fṛansa. Targit-agi tezga tezdeɣ aḍan-is akken
tedder  deg  ul-is,  tedder  deg  idammen  yuzzlen  di  tfekka-yis.  Targit-agi  nnes
tettfekti, tettefruruy armi d-tuɣ akk ussan-is. Meqran yettmeyyiz yufa akken ad
yeffeɣ i teswiɛt-a ilaq ad yerr azal i wayen akk is d-teǧǧa temẓi-s, yal lḥaǧǧa ad
d-yelhi  yid-s as-d-yaf  tifrat,  yettnedi,  yettxemmim…  yufa  kra d  ixef  uɣur ṭṭfen
takurin  n  lxiḍ.  Yufa-d  iẓewran  i  seg  ssegmen  yemɣan,  yufa-d  ssebbat  n  teṛzeg
ikecmen tudert-is. Yufa timsal yak cuddent ɣer yiwet yellan d tikerrist i ilaq ad
yefsi acku sekra ara tekk tkerrist tuggi ad tefsi ad yettḥulfu am akken d tiyersi-
yis i yurzen amzun d tamuxniqt. Ma yuggi ad yamen s twenza d wayen yeṭṭfen
ɣer-s,  yettamen  s  wayen  i  yexdem,  ayen  i  d-itddun  yettban-as-d  tikwal  d  lḥif  i
seg ad iḥemmel yal ass kra, yettban-as-d daɣen d aman imerẓuga yuggi ad adren
di tgerjumt qqimen din ttkuffuten. Ayen i t-id-yewwin ɣer Fṛansa mačči d ayen i
d-yewwin  akk  iɣriben  izzayriyen  i  d-yettasen  ad  xedmen  ɣef  lleẓ  n  warraw-
nnsen neɣ d ayen d-yettawin kra inelmaden ɣef unadi n tmussni di tesdaweyyin.
Meqran i t-id-yewwin d rregmat ur n-tekkes arma ḍsan widen yettrun !
Yella  deg  wawal  ula  d  izem  agellid  n  lewḥuc  yenna-t  i  teqcict:  leǧruḥ  qqazen
ḥellun,  ma  d  yir  lehduṛ  qqazen  rennun.  Meqran  iḥulfa  s  rregmat  qqazent  deg
iman-is amzun d burekku: ma yesteqsi walbeɛd amek yella, Meqran yeqqar:
“Aql-ih am ucagg yeqquren
S ufella n tenqelt
Aḍu i d-iṣuḍen ay-ihuzz
Ur ttuqeddreɣ d isɣaren
Ad rɣeɣ s tidet

Ammud n tullisin
Wamma akka udem-iw iduz…”
Meqran yettmeslay-d ɣef yiman-is s isefra, yettmuddu-d udem umeɣbun; ussan-
is d leḥzen; tameddurt-is d teṛzeg… tin yeḍran yid-s ḥala amedyaz i tt-id-yufan :
S wayen iẓiḍen i ɛaceɣ
Ma d ul-iw ɣer daxel icaḍ…
Tisemmiṭ  n  wul-is,  neɣ  lehna  n  wallaɣ-is,  yettwali-tt  d  tatut  n  temẓi-s
yesɛedda  di  lferḥ  deg  i  d-yemɣi  wurruz  n  wurrif :  ilaq  ad  yaweḍ  a  ten-yefru
akken ad yelhi d wayen nniḍen. D aya ladɣa i t-id-yewwin ɣer Lttari. ɣur-s ula d
ccwam i d-igellun s lehna yelha.
Ma yeqqim ad d-yettmekti taddart-is  yettanni  ger wallen-is,  ixxamen-nni
n wakal neɣ uqermud i ibubben zzman: kra n leḥyuḍ hudden, ttbanen-d kan iẓra
d  wakal  d  aya  i  d-yeqqimen  seg-mi  teffeɣ  Fṛansa.  Yettwali  diɣen  lexyal  n
iberdan  uɣur  d  ffɣent  tzulixin,  azniq  n  taddart  anda  a  tturaren  warrac  deg
uɣebbar, tajmiɛt anda d mlalen yemɣaren d kra n yelmeẓyen, tala anda ttemlilint
tullas  s  tecmuxin  n  talaxt  i  deg  i  d-ttawint  aman…  yettwali  afrag  n  wexxam-
nnsen, tamazirt i deg i tetteẓẓu yemma-s kra n lxeḍra… yettwali axxam-nnsen d
isulas-is  i  d-yecfan  i  tudert  n  yemdanen.  Yettani  jidda-s  i  yas-d-yeqqaren
timucuha n tteryel, tameddit di ccetwa ma qqimen ɣer lkanun. Yettwali yemma-
s i n-yeǧǧa q tettru asmi d-yusa. Yemmekta-d ayen i yas-tenna: “Asmi ad uɣaleḍ
a mmi ad iyi-d-tafeḍ iwḍeɣ ɣer ddaw wakal, axiṛ qqim ad tidireḍ…”. Ameslay-
agi aneggaru ur as-yesli ara, neɣ ur as-yuɣa ara: yeẓra-t akken ad yekkes aṭṭan i
yebdan  a  t-ikeččem…  Tikwal,  Meqran  yettara-tt  ɣer  tissit  deg  ubisṭru  arma
wwin-t-id  wid  it-yessnen  ɣer  texxamt  neɣ  tikwal  yettnusu  di  beṛṛa  neɣ  s  ddaw
tqenṭyar,  ddaw  kra  n  ṭṭjur,  anda  yufa…  Waah  !  meḥsub  yeksan  !  mi  yeswa  ad
yettanni iman-is d agellid n “Ṛṛuman dɣa ad yeṭṭes di tlemmast n wemdun deg
iriran d waman !
205
Ammud n tullisin
Tikelt nniḍen iɣelli-d fell-as rrebrab ur d-iteffeɣ ara si texxamt, ḥala ccṛab
i ittes akked ugaṛṛu… akken kra yekka wass, allen-is ttazzalent d imeṭṭawen.
Yekker i Fṛansa s iɣallen d wallen: ixeddem akken ad yesɛu kra a iṣerref
deg unadi n temdinin, Lyun, Maṛsay, Buṛdu… qrib ad yekk akk Fṛansa ar ass-a
ur yewwiḍ ɣer  lebɣi-s. Ar  melmi  ? Yenɣa-t naddam  yessers aqerru-s ɣef ṭṭabla
yellan  zdat-is  ur  yuki  armi  yeṭṭes,  yettargu,  yettargagi,  yettlejlij…  tikkelt-nni,
iruḥ am win ihajen yekker-d a yettsuɣu ad tɣileḍ d aderwic. “Ilaq a tt-fruɣ yid-
s”…  yettani  udem  n  lɛesker,  d  lexyal-nnsen  i  d-yekkan  zdat  wallen-is:  iqder
yecfa  maca  ur  yeẓri  d  acu  i  wumi  yecfa  ?  Ireggem,  ur  yeẓri  anda  ibedd  wala
anda  yella…  weḥd-s  daxel  n  texxamt;  akka  i  tḍerru  yid-s.  Taggara  yeqqim  a
yettru, aqerru-s ger tgecrar-is, ḥala asnecfet i wumi a tesleḍ.
Tatut n temẓi mačči d ayen i ɣer yezmer wemdan ad yessiweḍ acku mačči
deg  yiwen  wass  a  temḥuḍ  ayen  tesɛeddaḍ  ama  ẓid  neɣ  rẓag.  Netta  yekker  i
wedrar s ugelzim: ad  yefru ayen i  yas-tettalas temẓi akken ad yesɣers ayen  i t-
icudden ɣer-s, ad yerr ad yidir ddunit-is am netta am wiyyaḍ. Temẓi-s yecfa-yas-
d tella deg yemma-s tbedd fell-as, tettḥarab fell-as. Limer mačči d tayemmat atih
ass-a  yemmut:  nɣan-t  lɛesker  neɣ  yenɣa-t  usemmiḍ.  Maca  yemma-s  yal  ass
tezga  ɣer  tama-s,  tekkes  fell-as  tugdin  d  laẓ.  Akken  ad  as-yerr  lxiṛ  ilaq  a  tt-
yessefreḥ, ad as-yekkes iɣeblan d yerzan fell-as, d wurrif izedɣen adif n yeɣsan-
nni  d  yeqqimen  deg-s…  ayen  akk  yessefraḥ  yemma-s  zik  ur  idum  ara,  iwala
tisemmiṭ  n  wul-is:  ad  yerr  ttar  d  lḥerma  yettwakksen  ɣef  yemma-s.  Imiren
yezmer ad yebru i temẓi-s akken ad yidir ayen i yas-d-yeqqimen.
206
Ammud n tullisin
Tizqaqin n taddart
1.
Ahat cfant-d  i zzman  n  yiɣil, asmi  yal adrum  yerra d  uqerru-s, yella akken
bɣant  twaculin  yettekkan  deg-s.  Tizqaqin  n  taddart,  cfant-d  i  tmeddurt  n  wid
yellan  ɣer-sent.  Anwa  i  d  amessedrar  wer  nekki  ara  seg  webrid-nnsent,  ur
nessared  ara  si  tala-nnsent  neɣ  ur  neqqim  ara  ɣef  teḥnayin  n  tejmiɛt  i  tent-
iqerben.  Tizqaqin  d  nitenti,  i  yessemlalen  wid  yemmuten  d  wid  yeddren.  At
taddart  akk  ẓran:  tineṭlin  yellan  di  tezqaqin  d  tiwwura  ɣer  tmeddurt  n  dihen
akkin  i  tudert,  d  aya  i  sen-d-qqaren  imɣaren  di  tejmiɛt,  nutni  ttamnen:  “win
yeɛyen di tikli ɣef akal ad yinig ɣer ddaw-as ad yesteɛfu”.
D imeẓyanen i d imezwura mzazalen-d ɣer s agni n tezqaqin anda ara uraren
deg  yijdi  i  yiṭij  qessḥen.  Zzewren—isuɣan  d  taḍsa…  Yidir  yessikid  deg-sen
yemmekti-d  temẓi-s,  asmi  yella  d  acawrar  ula  d  netta  ixnunnes  deg  uɣebbar  i
uzal. Yidir ḥala netta i d-yegran di tɣalaṭ n tejmiɛt, si tifawt i yeqqim din, ad d-
yettmektay  temẓi-s  yettru.  Lgirra  tufa-t-id  d  ameẓyan.  Yedder  ger  lɛesker  n
Fṛansa d yemjuhad, akken armi tefra lgirra, yessaweḍ 20 iseggasen di leɛmer-is.
Tiɣimit-is  di  tejmiɛt  kan,  mi  d-yekfa  cceɣl  n  lexla  ad  yas  ad  iqesseṛ  d
yelmeẓyen.  Dinna  i  yeɛreḍ  tayri  mi  yettwali  tullas  ttɛeddint  ɣer  tala.  Tullas  n
taddart  ur  ttfakkant  ara  mi  dayen  fukkent  tid  yessawḍen  tizi  n  zzwaǧ,  ad
imɣurent tiyyaḍ. Din  i  yessen  Yidir tin a  izedɣen tirga-yis. Yuɣal  yal tameddit
yettɛassa-tt mara d-tɛeddi ɣer tala, iḥeggeṣ-d tamuɣli neɣ azmumeg seg wudem-
is. Yedder di talwit, di tirga i deg yettani am akken yerra yid-s axxam. Yidir ur
issin ara lakul, tikelt ukk tamezwarut mi yesla i yis yenna-yas:
“Ziɣ  arrac-nni  drewcen,  ad  ruḥen  si  tifawt  ɣer  temddit  ad  ɣren  ɣer  lecyax  n
Fṛansa, mbaɛd ad uɣlen…”.
2.

Ammud n tullisin
Yidir ladɣa ur iḥemmel ara wid yeɣran. Aṭas deg-sen ssimɣuren iman-nnsen
amzun  mačči  ɣef  yiwet  n  tegnit  i  teddun  yid-s.  Maca  yeɛdel  netta  d  yiwen
unelmad Qasi n At Waɛban segmi yas-d-yenna tadyant i yeḍran yid-s. D acu-tt ?
yiwen  ur  yeẓri  maca  Yidir  yecfa  mačči  seg  wid  itettun.  Attih  acu  i  yas-d-
-  Sliɣ  i  tbaturt  tuɣwas,  tiɣri-s  tuɣ-d  igenni,  dɣa  mi  d-rnant  tiyyaḍ  ad  tɣileḍ
yemmeslay Qasi :
imeẓẓaɣ-ik qqersen si zzhir-nni.
Zziɣ ɣer deffir d acu a twaliḍ ? D acu a ssikdent wallen-ik ? Ad tɣileḍ d
tamdint i d-yeggan asalu. Tabaturt tamezwarut ad tettemserɣa am leqdaɛ ujenwi
ddaw  tafat  n  yiṭij,  zewwqen-tt  s  ijeǧǧigen  ad  as-tiniḍ  d  tibḥirt  n  lwerd.  Mi
ssakdeɣ ɣer daxel-is,  iban-iyi-d  yiwen  yeṭṭef agaṛṛu  ger  iḍewdan-is tama  n win
yeṭṭfen  lqews  n  tenheṛt  ger  ifassen-is,  yettaḍsa,  ttbanent-d  tuɣmas  n  wureɣ  ger
wuglan-is ! Ɣer deffir yedda-d yiwen ilemẓi d tizya n ccix u ɣer ɣriɣ di tesdawit.
Cfiɣ  fell-as  cfaya  n  win  meẓẓiyen,  ccix  nni  ladɣa  yeqqar-iyi:  “Ma  tzewreḍ  di
tɣuri-yik  a  Qasi,  ad  tizmireḍ  ad  teffɣeḍ  si  tmurt-a  acku  kečč  ur  tezmireḍ  ad
tiḍireḍ deg-s…”.
Mi walaɣ ilemẓi-nni mmektaɣ-d ccix-nni. Mi d-mmektaɣ ayen iyi-yeqqar,
mmektaɣ ayen  iyi-tenna  yemma: “Ma tzewreḍ a  mmi di tɣuri-k ad tizmireḍ ad
teqqimeḍ di tmurt-a ɣer ɣur-I ur tezmireḍ ara ad tṛuḥeḍ ad iyi-teǧǧeḍ…”! ɛeddi
kečč fru-tt ! Ṛuḥeɣ deg wesmekti !
Win yettcabin ɣer ccix-nni yelsa-d akustim, yettecmumuḥ d taḍsa tama-s
tella  yiwet  n temɣart terẓa-tt ddunit ahat ɣef  uɛekkaz kan  i tleḥḥu, ɣer s idis-is
teqqim-d  yiwet  n  teqcict  tecbeḥ  mačči  d  kra,  tamuɣli-s  tcerreg  tirga.  Deg
uɣebbar  i  d-teǧǧa  tbaturt-nni  ur  walaɣ  kra,  ḥala  tid  d-yernan  deffir-s,  llant
teḥdayin, tilawin d yergazen-nnsent, ad tesleḍ kan i teḍsa, lkeff, tiɣratin, ccna…
mačči  d  yiwen  a  t-id-iniɣ…  Mi  yers  uɣebbar  akken  iɛedda  usensi,  ddiɣ  d
webrid-iw  ɣer  taddrat:  Abrid  i  yewwi  usensi.  Abbrid  n  taddart  ɣezzif  acku
yenneḍ, nniɣ-as limer ad zegreɣ kan syagi si tmizar ad awḍeɣ zik s axxam, a wer
i  yaɣ-yeṭṭef  yiṭij-nni  n  Yulyu  beṛṛa.  Mmektaɣ-d  ass-a  i  d  amenzu  n  Yulyu  s

Ammud n tullisin
leḥsab n tefransist. Ladɣa imir i d-mmektaɣ yemma tameqqrant i wumi nniɣ ad
rzuɣ ɣur-m dduṛt ad iteddun. Ladɣa acuɣer ur ttawḍeɣ ara ɣer-s ass-a… Mi qrib
ad awḍeɣ ɣer lḥara, mlaleɣ-d Mennad, nemsalam.
- Amek i telliḍ ?
- Aql-iyi di lxiṛ d lehna !
Walaɣ udem-is yewlelles, d acu i yellan ?. Steqsaɣ-t:
- Ahh ! D acu akka i k-yuɣen ?
Yenna-yi-d:
- Ulac !
Nniɣ-as:
- Ihi, d acu i yellan ma tettbaneḍ tḥezneḍ ?
Amzun yeggugem. Walaɣ texsaṛ nneyya-s tikelt-nni yerra-d nnehta, yenna-yi :
- Teẓriḍ ! ur bɣiɣ ara ak-sḥezneɣ di teswiɛt-agi i deg telliḍ maca yettif ad teẓreḍ
si tura wala arma d tameddit, ihi tin akken tḥemmleḍ ass-agi ad teddu d tislit.
- Aha ! daɣen tebḍid-d tikad-ik !
- Hhe ! d tidet, yya-d ɣer nnig webrid ad twaliḍ ma mačči s axxam-nnsen i yerra
usensi, tura iyi-d-yenna Wakli n Sekkura.
Din  ibeddeɣ,  qqimeɣ  allen-iw  ur  d-kkisent  ara  seg  wexxam  n  ….  ,  rsent  ɣef
lḥaṛa, rsent fell-as armi ḥulfaɣ ayen akk ttwaliɣ zik d azgen ass-a d wayeḍ.
- Tezriḍ ! Ad ṣubbeɣ, ad tt-waliɣ tikelt taneggarut.
Yezzi-d ɣur-i Mennad yenna-k:
- Ula d nekk ad dduɣ a tt-waliɣ.
Kkiɣ  seg  ayla  n  Mḥend  At  Lewnis  armi  d  abrid  n  tala,  ladɣa  mlaleɣ-t-id  din,
yelsa-d  akustim  i  d-yuɣ  ddurt-nni  iɛeddan  ɣer  “Cardin”  di  Lttari  !  Yewwi-d
tanegḥelt-nni  i  d-yuɣ  si  Legliz  !  nniɣ-awen  yesɛa-ten,  baba-s  d  ameṛkanti
ameqqran yesɛa snat n luzinat di Lḥerrac akked Birxadem, mebla lbillat di Ḥidra
neɣ nnutilat d leqhawi di Fṛansa ! yenna-yi :

Ammud n tullisin
- Amek yettili Qasi At Weɛban ! tusiḍ-d ɣer tmeɣra, mṛeḥba yis-k, dɣa  ussan-
agi i steqsaɣ fell-ak, nniɣ-as ad nṣeggeḍ ilfan di teẓgi. Maca nnan-iyi truḥeḍ ɣer
Wehṛan, ihi teɛǧeb-ik Wehṛan; aah ! nekk ḥemmleɣ-tt temdint-nni !...
Ikemmel  deg  wawal,  nek  ma  cfiɣ  ɣef  wayen  i  d-yerna,  ɣas    d-iceṭṭeb  isɣaren
zdat-I ur tẓerreɣ, ur tettwaliɣ.
Newweḍ,  nufa  tislit  teffeɣ-d  ɣer  s  afrag  n  waxxam.  Tura,  a  tt-awin,  uẓiɣ  ɣer
wegraw n yergazen qqimeɣ. Mennad tama-w i yella mi tuli s aṭaksi ad tṛuḥ. Rriɣ
ad ffɣeɣ, Mennad yella daɣen s idis-iw. Yeqleɛ usensi, acemma ue d iyi-yuɣ ur d
iyi-yerzi, si zik i walfeɣ…
3.
D  timucuha  i  iḥemmel  Yidir  n  At  Wakli  acku  ttcabin  ɣer  tin  i  yas-
yeḍran… asmi ɛeddan  iseggasen, asmi  d-yufa  iman-is  yeɣleḍ di  leḥsab-is: tin  i
iḥemmel  fkan-tt  imawlan-is  tedda  d  tislit,  seg  asmi  teffeɣ  taddart  ur  tt-yeẓri  i
lukan d yiwet n tikkelt. Yerna ciṭ, zewǧen-as wat wexxam nnsen, yufa-d iman-is
imiren  yettwarez:  ilaq  ad  iḥeṛṛ  idrimen  aṭas  akken  ad  iɛeggec  imawlan-is,
iɛeggalen-is…
Sked  lḥif  ur  yessin.  Acḥal  i  iɛeddan  tura  si  mi  tefra  lgirra,  d  iseggasen
mačči d kra. Yidir yesteɛfa si tezqaqin : yettwali akken llant i tent-mazal ɣer ass-
a, maca imezdaɣ beddlen s waṭas. Ur tɣiman ara yelmeẓyen di tejmiɛt, sɛan akk
ccɣel i ten-yeṭṭfen. Ulac ifelleḥen a ixeddmen tibḥirin, si ssuq i d-ttaɣen medden
ayen ḥlaǧen ma d ffɣen tameddit si lluzinat neɣ si lbiruwat. D taxeṭṭayt temɣart
ad izedmen isɣaren, yella lgaz n teqreɛtin. Ulac tullas ad iɛeddin ɣer tala acku a
tent akka akk di  lakul,  yerna  llan waman  deg  usariǧ  ula d ameksa  n taddart  ur
yufi ara win ara d as-d-yefken tiqḍiɛin, iruḥ a ixeddem d aqehwaǧi di Lezzayer.
Ur  d-grin  ara  at  taddart  ḥala  wid  wer  nezmir  ad  ffɣen.  Ulac  i  d-yeqqimen  si
tudert-nni n zik di tezqaqin ḥala nutenti. Tbeddel tmeddurt amzun di ddeqs zalla,
beddlen imdanen yid-s…

Ih ! Lukan ad teẓreḍ !
“Ḥṣiɣ aṭas ara s-yinin ciṭ  yemmuten di tnekra  nni  n tuber acku  i  yebɣun
yemmet ur d-yessawaḍ ayen iǧǧan tudert di tegrawla tis snatn wemdal. Maca a
wi k-iḥkan amek tejreḥ tasa-w mi walaɣ izzayriyen ɣellin ddaw ṛsas n izzayriyen
D  wigi  i  d  imeslayen  i  sliɣ  ɣer  Mennad  mi  s-nniɣ  wali  acu  i  d-nnan  di
lkaɣeḍ-agi. Mennad sneɣ-t asmi i lliɣ d anelmad di tesdawit n Bab Zwar  mi d-
yettas  ɣer  din  ad  iɣer  Tamaziɣt,  tuɣ-it  yeqqar  deg  wexxam  akken  ad  iɛiwed  i
ukayaḍ  n  lbak  acku  ur  t-id-iwwi  ara  abrid-nni  iɛeddan.  D  aqcic  alemmas,  acu
kan  ur  tṛebbuḍ  ara  iɣimi  yid-s,  terna  yexḍa  i  temɛyin-agi  n  zelmeḍ  yeffus.
Yekker-d di teqsabt, ur yessin tamurt i deg i d-kkren ibabaten-is armi yesɛa 21
iseggasen,  yewhem  asmi  yewweḍ  ɣer  taddart-nni  nnsen  ddaw  idurar  n  Ǧerǧer.
Seg imiren, melmi yesɛa kra n wussan n tɣimit, iteddu ad iẓer imesdurar, arraw
n taddart anda yenṭel jeddi-s. Asmi t-ssneɣ tella yiwet n teqcict yid-s, ula d nettat
ssneɣ-tt, isem-is Jeǧǧiga. Segmi yella yeqqar di Lycée Ttasteur yeddukul yid-s,
ixḍeb-itt. Imawlan n teqcict ugin di tazwara maca walan mačči d ara arzen yelli-
tsen deg wexxam, uɣalen deg wawal nnsen, qeblen-t, awi-d kan imi ula d nitni n
At Waɛban, wamag ɣas ad yili d mmi-s n win d win. Cfiɣ yeḥkayi-d Mennad ɣef
asmi  d-tewwi  lbak,  tullas  ferḥent  nettat  tettru  acku  mačči  yid-s  ara  yili  di
tesdawit  imi  netta  ur  t-id-yewwi  ara  yettru  ger  ifassen-is.  Limer  qqazen
imeṭṭawen  tiregwa deg weksum  yili  leḥnak  n Jeǧǧiga ass-nni ad keflen  yeɣsan
nnsen. Ue tebɣi ara ad teqqim  yiwen wass di tudert-is  ur  yelli ara Mennad ɣer
tama-s. ah ! a wi yeẓran d acu s tayri kečč ad tfehmeḍ. Ufan-d tifrat ger-asen: ad
iɛiwed asɛeddi u ukayad tikelt tis snat d acu kan tikelt-a ad yeqqar deg wexxam
akken ad yesɛu akud ad yexdem di beṛṛa, akken ad yettruḥu ɣer tesdawit ɣer tin
iri !
211
Ammud n tullisin
Asirem n Mennad d wa: ad yekcem ɣer tesdawit ad iɣer d Jeǧǧiga, ad yili yid-s
simi ad rren axxam. Yeḥṣa tamezduɣt di Lezzayer txuṣ maca yettxemmim ad d-
yawi amkan n lxedma di 10 iseggasen ad as-fken axxam, mazal tura 20 ayen nni
yezrin  ! lxaṭer-is yewseɛ mačči d kra. Yeqqar am wass-a ad tbeddel n neffeɣ si
yir taswiɛt ɣer tmeddurt taswiɛt awi-d kan a nelhu d leqdic. Ih a Mennad ! amer
kečč  i  txemmimen  akk  wigi  yellan  s  nnig-nneɣ  atih  izzayriyen  akk  ad  tessen
ayefk  tifawt,  ur  ttlaẓen  ara,  ad  slen,  ad  rren  ixxamen.  Yeqqar-iyi  Mennad  a
nexdem ɣas ma yehwa-yas lqern awi-d kan iswi-nneɣ ad t-naweḍ: a neffeɣ seg
umirej  n  lmizirya  i  deg  a  nettemxebbaḍ,  d  waluḍ  n  lḥif  i  yugin  ad  yesfeḍ  ɣef
ikesman. Yeqqar-iyi Mennad: “Twalaḍ ‘Ṛṛuman, Iwendalen, Ibiẓantiyen nebḍen
di  tmurt,  xedmen  lbaṭel  deg  wegdud.  Teffeɣ-d  teɣri  seg  wegdud  nni  yettewten
ideqqer  azaglu,  yekker  isuffeɣ-iten,  d  aḍummu  i  iḍum  Kusayla  Ibiẓantiyen  si
tmurt qbel ad tt-isdukkel. Tirga  mlalent d tifawt seg tifawt i d-tekka tafat, tirga
qqlent  d  asirem,  asirem  yeslal-d  lebɣi.  lebɣi  yiwen  ur  t-yettṛuẓu.  zdat  n  lebɣi
yefsi weẓru akken i yefsi wagu.
-  ḥedreɣ  zdat-I  mi  yeɣli  yiwen  weqcic  ur  yessaweeḍ  ara  mraw  iseggasen  di
leɛmer-is,  mmɣeɣ refdeɣ-t-id idim seg-s yettfeggiḍ. Iceṭṭiḍen-iw akk  umsen, ur
issaweḍ ara ɣer sbiṭar yemmut… teḥsiḍ nekk d Jeǧǧiga nemfaraq…”.
- Aww ! Tebɣiḍ ad tqessreḍ neɣ acu ?...
Walaɣ allen-is rsent ɣer lqehwa nni yellan ɣef ṭṭabla, mačči yejɣem-itt ula
d  tikkelt,  lqehwa  berriket  akken  berrikwudem  n  Mennad,  iwlelles  ad  tɣileḍ  d
temettant i d-yewwḍen ad tawi-t, awal  ur t-id-issuli nniɣ-as :
- Aah ! aɛni yella kra i d-yellan ger-awen, xuḍi…
Awal-agi aneggaru yedda-d n nnehta yesenquqlen idmaren-is.
- ur tt-ǧǧiɣ ur d iyi-teǧǧi.
- Amek ?
- Tiweḍ s anda a naweḍ akk.
- Temmut ?
- Nɣan-tt.
212
Ammud n tullisin
Iwala ameslay ur zmireɣ ad t-id-rnuɣ nnig waya maca yedda imiren deg wawal,
yenna :
- Ass n ssebt i tt-ḥuzan, ɣer ubalku, lɛesker mara kkaten deg igenni, din i teɣli,
aksum-is yefka-twaldun- ue as-icuḥḥ ara. Ur ḥsiɣ amek iwḍeɣ s axxam nnsen mi
iyi-id-yenna gma-s amejṭuḥ, akken tt-walaɣ ɣliɣ fell-as ur zmireɣ ad ṭṭfen imeṭṭi.
Ṭṭfeɣ-tt-id  ger  ifassen-iw,  ayen  ruɣ  fell-as  limer  tmaranidammen  seg  wallen
yalli udem-is d wemzur-is a ten-rreɣd izeggaɣen. Ay ruɣ i tt-ṭṭfeɣ ger ifasen-iw
bɣiɣ ad dduɣ ad iyi-tawi tmettant, ur ttɣimeɣ ara deffir-s, ttruɣ acku ɣas ṭṭfeɣ-tt
ger  ifassen-iw,  lferḥ  yennejla  seg  wul-iw.  Ttruɣ  ur  ḥṣiɣ  acḥal,  zziɣ  ɣer  baba
allen-is nexxrent mačči d ayen ara teẓreḍ yenna-k: “Ammi…”. Ur ḥsiɣ d acu i d-
yerna, cfiɣ kan ɣef ufus ines ayeffus yenneḍ-d i tuyat-iw. Ddiɣ ɣer s aẓkka, ay
din  a  lqum:  wa  yettɣizi,  win  a  yettru.  Walaɣ  udem-is  tikelt  taneggarut  d  ayen
ḥala di  lkaɣeḍ ara tt-ẓerren.  Hulfeɣ s s tebrek ad tettaɣ  ussan-iw seg wass-n ar
ass-a…  Tezdeɣ  uḍan  am  zik  am  wass-a.  ur  ḥṣiɣ  sani  ara  kkeɣ,  ihudd  usirem,
tudert a tt-tezdeɣ teṛzeq. Ur sɛiɣ iswi di tudert yecban ta-agi.
Iṭij a iɣelli beṛṛa, ad d-iɣelli ṭṭlam, maca walaɣ di tezwiweɣ(leḥḥmuregga)
n temdint cbaḥa d liser. Mektaɣ-d tahuski n Dasin i ɣef yecna Musa ag amastan.
Di tezwiweɣ nni n tmeddit walaɣ Mennad yettaḍṣa d Jeǧǧiga. Amzun si targit i
d-ukiɣ, walaɣ Mennad  iɣumm tama  nni seg d-tekka  leḥmuregga,  ma d Jeǧǧiga
yeqder  di  leḥmuregga  nni  kan  i  tella  acku  ulac-itt  dagi  (a  wi  yufan  ad  tili  !)
mektaɣ-d  belli  ma  ra  d-tegg  leḥmuregga  tameddit  n  wass  azekka  nni  ad  teṣḥu
tegnawt, ur d-yekkat ara ugeffur, ad yili yiṭij amzun d tafsut. D imi qqaren wat
zik :
Leḥmuregga n ṣṣbeh
Heggit isɣaren i useqdeḥ.
Leḥmuregga n tmeddit
A tteǧǧar aɛebbit
Nniɣ-as:
-“Teẓṛiḍ a Mennad, azekka ad yili yiṭij.
213
Ammud n tullisin
Dɣa yenna-k :
- Ih ! ad nemmager tafsut…

Tudert n umaru Saɛid Cemmax
Saɛid  Cemmax,  ilul  deg  useggas  n  1968  deg  At  Buɣerdan  (Buɣni)  deg
tmurt  n  leqbayel.  D  aneɣmas  n  tmaziɣt  ama  deg  tsertit  ama  deg  yidles,  aṭas  i
yeqdec i wesmil n yidles Amaziɣ d tutlayt tamaziɣt ladɣa deg Umussu Adelsan
Amaziɣ   ( M.C.B).
Saɛid Cemmax, mi yekcem ɣer tesdawit yefren ad d-iɣer tussna n ugama
(biologie),  maca  tettunefk-as  tegnit  deg  1989  ad  iɣer  tamaziɣt  deg  Inalco,  iruḥ
meɛna  ur  yesɛi ara tawil ad d-yeqqim deg Pari,  yuɣal-d ɣer  Tizi-Wezzu ,yeɣra
Tafransist  almi  d-yewwi  taragt,  deg  useggas  n  1994  yuɣal  ɣer  Inalco,  yexdem
agerdas  n  tɣuri  lqayen  (DEA)  ɣef  umawal  n  Teqbaylit.  Syin  yerna  yekfa
dductura  deg  useggas  n  2003,  ddaw  tmehla  n  Salem  Chaker,  yefka-as  azwel  «
Lexicologie berbère- l’élaboration du vocabulaire fundamental du Kabyle ».
Гef udlis « Gar zik d tura », yewwi-d arraz Mulud Mɛemri deg useggas n
1963. Tullisin d-yura deg udlis-agi, yella yessufeɣ-d kra seg-sent deg tesɣunin,
- Tullist « Tuɣalin » yessufeɣ-itt-id deg yebrir 1993, deg tesɣunt Tiɣri unelmad
(nº  4, Tasdawit n Tizi-Wezzu).
- Tullist « Tadyant n mmi-s uciban », yessufeɣ-itt-id deg tesɣunt Izuran, asebtar
37 deg useggas n 2002.
-  Tullist  «  Ad  gen  tameɣra  »,  yessufeɣ-itt-id  deg  tesɣunt  Izuran,  asebtar  08,
- Tullist «Tizqaqin n taddart », Tafukt nº 1, 1994, deg Asi Yusef.
- Tullist « Ih ! Lukan ad tezreḍ ! », Tamaziɣt tura, Utun wis sin, 1989.
-  Aḍris « Neǧma n medden merra », deg tasɣunt Tafsut, nº 14 deg yebrir 1990.
Amaru-a yura aṭas n yimagraden d yeḍrisen ama deg yeɣmisen ama deg tesɣuni
neɣ deg linternet, ad nebder kra n yimagraden, isaragen d temliliyin :
ad naf :

Timerna
Adiwenni i texdem Ghoul Zahia d  umaru Saɛid Cemmax ɣef  udlis: « Gar
zik d tura ». deg wass 18 avril 2015.
D  acu-t  yeswi-ik  mi  i  d-turid  ɣef  ubeddel  yellan  deg  tmetti,  ama  d  ayen
yeɛnan ansayen neɣ ayen yeɛnan idles ?
  Deg  tazwara,  amur  ameqqran  d  timucuha,  maci  d  timucuha  n  teryel  d
yiwaɣzniwen, d tullisin, maɛna-s d imdanen yedren i sneɣ, i d-mlalaɣ, llan-t
tid  i  d-ḥekkan  yemdukal-iw,  nudaɣ  fkiɣ-asent  aɣanib  aseklan,  nqaɛd-itent,
deg uzmam-a ad d-afeḍ tẓa n tullisin d sḍis n yeḍrisen nniḍen, ur ttunaḥsaben
ara  d  tullisin,  ɣef  yisem  «  Gar  zik  d  tura  »  nwala  belli  ɣas  akken  yettbedil
zman,  ɣas  aṭas  n  leḥwayej  i  d-yenulfan  ama  d  ayen  yeɛnan  la  micanic  neɣ
titiknulujiyin timaynutin, maca yella wayen d-yekkan nnig n yal zman, yella
wayen i d-izagren kul lewqat, tamusni-iw teqqim-d ɣas tettbedil tetiknulujit,
anect-a i bɣiɣ ad sbegneɣ deg yal tullist belli nezmer ad nesufeɣ ayen iwumi
ad nessami lewsayat.
Ayɣer tazwert n udlis-ik s tutlayt Tafransist i tt-id-yura Salem Chaker?
  Yebɣa ad tt-id yexdem s tutlayt Tafransist, ixadem-itt-id, maci d Tamaziɣt ur
yessin  ara,  yessen  ula  d  tamahaqt  d  tmaziɣt  n  waṭlas.  Aṭas  n  wuguren  i  d-
mlalaɣ akken ad d-yeffeɣ uzmam waḥdes, ala Asqamu Unnig n Timuzɣa i d-
iqqeblen  yeffeɣ-d  s  tutlayt  tamaziɣt,  llan  wid  d-yessutren  tisuqilin  ɣer
tefransist, ad d-ddun-t tid n tmaziɣt, ɣas akken s yedrimen-iw ugiɣ, nniɣ-asen
sɛiɣ  igerdasen  s  tefransist  imi  ala  ad  yeffeɣ  s  tmaziɣt,  win  yebɣan  ad  as-
neyaxdem tasuqilt ad asen-yexdem, tella yiwen n teqcict txedem-asen tasuqilt
ɣer Taɛrabt urɛad kkan i d-ffeɣen.
Amek textareḍ tawsit n tullist maci dayen-nniḍen?
  D win  isehlen aṭas, uriɣ tamedyazt, ungal, warǧin  i d-yeffeɣ  maca d tiki  iyi
sahlen,  arnu  tiki  dayen  zriɣ  ɣer  medden,  akken  d-yenna  At  Mangellet,  win
219
Timerna
iwumi ḥkiɣ ad yeḥku akter wayeḍ ad yernu ad yeḥku. Tina n « Ɛecrin n duru
»  d  yiwen  i  tt-id-yeḥkan  deg  Buɣni,  tullist  «  Tuɣalin  »  d  yiwen  deg  Tizi
Wezu  iyi-tt-id  yeḥkan  Daɣen,  ḥemlaɣ  tullisin  zik  mi  lliɣ  qqareɣ  Tafransist,
ḥemlaɣ aṭas Guy de Maupassant i d-ibanen s tullisin, daɣen ḥemlaɣ-tent ɣef
yiwet n tɣawsa, d timezyanin, amur ameqran ddant-d akk di tesɣunin, tiɣrin n
unelmad,  tasɣunt  tafsut,  tamaziɣt  tura,  yeshel  akken  ad  ten-t-id  seddud,
tamurt izuran n Salem Zinya, yiwen n usebter neɣ sin ad ten-id qqeblen.
Ayen  yeɛnan  isental,  ahat  nezmer  ad  d-nekkes  deg  tullist  «  Taninna  »
asentel agejdan d iɛewiqen n tudert n tlemẓit taqbaylit ?
   Iɛewiqen  n tlemzit  taqbaylit, Semaɣ-as Taninna ɣef tmacahut  n  leḍyur, ɣef
Tninna mi d-yeḥder ad tezweǧ, wamag taqcict tedder s tidet, taḥkayt teḍra mi
nruḥ seg Lzayyer tamanaɣt ɣer Bab Zwar, sneɣ-tt, sneɣ ansi i d-ɛedda, ɛedleɣ
yid-s, qesdeɣ ad aruɣ tamacahut-is acku ayen akk ansi d tt-ɛeddi ḥulfaɣ ula d
nekk iyi-s. walaɣ amek itt-dri-t almi d asmi tezweǧ, tuɣal s warraw-is, uɣalen
qrib rran-tt s tidet d tameṭṭut, awid kan baba-s mi yettḥarab fell-as akken d-
yedda deg tullist, tabrat i d-tura, tura-tt-id i nekk ɣer Pari.
Tabrat  i  d  yeddan  deg  tullist  «  Taninna  »,  ma  nexadem-as  tasleḍt
tasentalant d smaḥ i d-asentel-is ?
  Maci  d  smaḥ  kan,  bɣiɣ  ad  sbeggeneɣ  ɣas  akken  d  Tusnakt  i  tesɣara  tettaru
Tamaziɣt, tzamred ad tarud s tutlayt Tamaziɣt, ihi s leqraya-is tezmer ad taru
s Tmaziɣt anect-a si le passage à l’écrit.
Ma nuɣal ɣer tulist « Tuɣalin » asentel-is agejdan d tasertit ?
  Deg  juin  1988  aṭas  n  yimeḥbas  i  wumi  d-serḥen  seg  Lmaruk,  llan  wid  d-
yesɛeddan leḥebs dinna  azal n 150 deg-sen , ṭṭfen-ten seg 1976 deg Lmaruk
deg  Amgalla  lgira  n  Puli  Zaryu,  llan  wid  yesawḍen  snen  ula  d  tamaziɣt  ,
tacelḥit  deg  leḥbas  n  Maruk,  Tuɣalin  tettcabi  ɣer  tinna  n  Unri  de  belezak,
220
Timerna
meɛna  maci  d  taden,  ufiɣ-d  yiwen  seg  wid  d-yuɣalen,  fkan-as  axxam  deg
Tizi- Wezu yerra-tt kan i sekkran, yufa-d tameṭṭut-is yerra-tt gma-s, ɣur-sen
netta yemmut, acku cegɛen-asen-d asenduq yeččur d ijdi.
Deg tullist « Tuɣalin » Tameṭṭut n Meqran ur d bedred ara deg taggara ma
yerra-tt neɣ tullist-a ur tesɛi ara tagrayt ?
  Win  yeqqaren  yettekay  deg  tira,  la  lécture  c’est  une  partisipation  de
l’écriture,    llan  deg  kra  n  yisura  wid  deg  taggara  mzawaǧǧen,  xedmen
tameɣra n sebɛa wussan d wuḍan sɛan aṭas n derya am tmucuha n igelliden n
zik, yella wanda am deg yisura n wass-a deg tagara ad yemmet wasaḍ, ihi yal
yiwen  d  acu-tt  tegrayt  i  yexaṭir,  annect-a  yeqqim  ma  yeqqar  yiwen
tamacahut, yella yiwen n ugemaḍ  n uraǧǧu, ma yella nessen mliḥ ad nɣer ad
nettxayal amek ad tilli taggara-is, ahat akka neɣ akka.
Tullist « Tadyant n mmi-s n uciban » asentel-is d ttrebga di tmetti ?
  D yemma i tt-id-yeḥkan, tadyant-a teḍra deg taddart-nneɣ d tidet, di tazwara
ḥkiɣ-d  amek  i  tt-id  uwiɣ,  almi  d  asebter  wis  sin  ara  tebdu  teḥkayt,  mmi-s
uciban… , imi  mi itt-bdiɣ tadyant-a ḥekun-tt i warraw-nsen, nniɣ-d d acu-t le
contexte de recuil ambeɛd bdiɣ taḥkayt.
A yen yeɛnan tullist « Iminig », d acu yeǧǧan Meqran ad yebɣu ad yettu
temzi-is?
  Llant  kra  n  leḥwayeǧ  deg  temzi-is  ur  t-suɛdent  ara,  mi  d  yeḥder  yeffeɣ  ɣer
Fransa yufa ddunit mačči akken, macci d ayen i iɛac zik i yettɛici tura, yebɣa
akk ad yettu temzi-is n lḥif imi yemlal war asif.
Deg  tullist  «  Iminig  »  temmeslayeḍ-d  dakken  Meqran  iruḥ  s  axxam  n
Wenza, ur d tebḍireḍ ara d acu is-tettili Wenza akked gma-s i Meqran?
  D ameddakel-is yessen-it qbel akken ad yinig, labud fell-as ad yerzu fell-asen
ad asen-ibeqqi sslam akken ad iruḥ, acku dayen ur yettuɣal ara ad ten-izer.
221
Timerna
Di tullist « Tizqaqin n taddart », ayɣer i d-yeqqim Yidir di taddart weḥd-s ?
  Yeqqim-d acku  imeddukal-is akk ɣran,  ffɣen ɣer temdinin  ɣer  Fransa, netta
asmi  qqaren  medden  ur  yeɣri  ara  yelha-d  kan  d  wurar  wala,  asmi  i  iɛedda
lawan  yufa-d  lḥal  weḥd-s  yettezzi  di  tezqaqin-nni  n  taddart  deg  tama  n
Buɣni, yuɣal yendem mi ten-yettwali truḥun-d kan ɣer tmeɣriwin yiwen wass
deg  useggas  ma  yella  d  azɣal,  netta  yezga  dinna  yuɣal  amzun  d  aɛessas  ur
nettwaxelles ɣef tezqaqin-nni n taddart.
Deg  tullist  «  Tizqaqin  n  taddart»  temmeslayeḍ-d  ɣef  tin  i  iḥemmel  Yidir
fkan-tt imawlan-is, d acu n yizen i ɣer tebɣiḍ ad as-leḥqeḍ deg-s?
  Yezgel  kullec  imi  taqcict-nni  tedda  d  win  yeɣran  netta  yufa-d  iman-is  ulac
leqraya, kullec iruḥ-as yeqqim yettwali kan deg-s ma ad tɛeddi.
Deg tullist « ih! Lukan ad tezreḍ », ayɣer nɣan Jeǧǧiga deg useggas 1988?
  D taqsiḍt teḍra-d d sseḥ yakan, teḍra-d di  Lezzayer, dɣa aḍaris-nni  yeffeɣ-d
di  88,  n  Tizi  Raced  teqcict-agi,  ur  tt-nɣan  ara  s  tiɛemda,  mi  kkaten  s  rrsas
ḥuzan-tt s abalku, tenṭel di Tizi Raced.
Di tullist Taninna, tessexḍem-ḍ yiwet n tefyirt “yeffeɣ-d zun d ccix n ttarix,
acku macci seg wid i izemren ad sseɣren amezruy”. Dacu i d-qqasdad s sin
n wawalen, tarix, amezruy ?
  Ma as-tiniḍ i yiwen ɣriɣ s taɛrabt, ma as-tiniḍ i yiwen d ccix n ttarix maci d
ccix n umezruy, bɣiɣ ad d-iniɣ belli s taɛrabt i yeɣra, yeqqim kan di lḥebs-nni
n taɛrabt, s tiɛmada bac ad fehmen belli ulac akk assaɣ ɣur-s dayen kan i as-
yemla uɣerbaz azzayri.
Tenniḍ-d daɣen mi iḥuza uqcic-nni Taninna, “tzemreḍ ad tiniḍ seg wid-nni
i wumi qqaren aɣyul bu tlata n yetran”, d acu d qesḍeḍ seg aɣyul bu tlata
yetran?
222
Timerna
  D taḍsa fell-as dakken d aɣyul bu tlata n yetran, imi izad di teɣyulit-is, almi
ilaq as ɛellqen tlata n yetran am le militaire.
Deg  taggara  n  tullisin,  tesleḥqeḍ  ɣer  kra  n  yigemmaḍ,  d  acu  tzemreḍ  ad
textireḍ, d acu ik-iɛeǧben d timetti-nni n zik neɣ d tin n tura?
  Nekk ɣur-i lhan-t i snat, imi yiwet tesseɣr-iyi tayeḍ aqli qqareɣ deg-s.
223
Remdane  Lashab :  «  Gar  zik  d  tura  »de  Said  Chemmakh.le  01  Mai  2010.
Timerna

Awal ɣef « Ger zik d tura » n Mass Saɛid Cemmax: sɣur At Sliman Ḥamid
deg ass n 30 Wamber 2010.( www.tamazight.fr)
Deg  akka,  anebdu-agi  yezrin,  yefɣed  sɣur  tizrigin  Baɣdadi  yiwen  n
wamud  n  tullissin  yura  Mass  Saɛid  Chemakh  ddaw  yiwen  wezwel:  Ger  zik  d
Timerna
tura.
Amud-agi  deg  llan-t  tesɛa  n  tullisin  akked  setta  n  yeḍrisen  ufriḍen,
yettwarun  s  yiwen  uɣanib  yettmuddun  lebɣi  ɣer  taɣuri-nsen,  acku  timsal  ɣef
ayeg i d-yewwi d timsal yettḥazen amdan deg ixef-ines. "Ger zik d tura" d adlis i
d-yesfruruyen  tilufa  n  tmeddurt,  yettarra-tent-id  am  lemri  zdat  n  wallen-nneɣ
akken ad aten-t ɛabber, aten-t nektil , aten-t nessewzen di lmizan n tidmi-nneɣ ,
amer tifrat i tuttriwin inebccen di lbal, ad sen-t-id-nnaf tawwurt.
Ger Zik d tura, d tiqṣiḍin n yal ass i izemren ad ḍrun-t di yal tama di yal
lawan,  i  yal  yiwen  seg-nneɣ.  D  tiqṣiḍin  n  yemdanen  am  nekk  am  kunwi,  i
d-yekkren  deg  yirebbi  n  tmeti-nneɣ.  D  tiqṣiḍin  anida  yal  yiwen  ad  yeɛqel
iman-is deg-sent, acku uzlen-t ɣef lkaɣeḍ s umyaru i d-yewwin tikta deg ayen i
d-yennulfan naɣ i d-yettnulfun yal ass.
Ssaɛid Cemmax yewwi-d tugniwin n wayen i d-nettmager di tudert-nneɣ,
yesrezfaɣ ɣer telqay n tudert deg tudrin n tmurt n Leqbayel yeɛlulqen ɣef tuyat n
wedrar  werǧin  yeffiɣ  lhem  akked  d  ddel.  Maca,  xas  akken  iḍrisen  yellan  deg
amud-agi ur ddurin ara tacmet n tedyanin  ɣef ayeg  mderkalen yemdanen, tira s
wacu uran tugmed seg uɣbalu n leḥmala, imi Saɛid Cemmax ur icuḥ ara s tayri
yekseb  ɣer  ljiha  n  idurar.  Idurar  deg  nnif  yettemɛabbar  d  kennu,  deg  lɛez
yettnamar-it ddel, deg isaɣ yettucewwel s txaṣarin, deg addud yettili-d d ɣeluy.
Idurar  deg  ṣsber  tikwal  d  ddwa  n  tlufa,  di  nmara  d  abrid  ɣer  tnekra,  di
tmara d ussu n lehna. Idurar deg alluy yeqqen ɣer trusi, deg tehri d taxlijt n ddiq,
deg telqaq d takniwt n tewser, deg tumert d tarbibt n leḥzen, deg lehna tettlal-d s
229
cwal  am  waken  id  as  yenna  Ferḥat  deg  awal-is:  "Imesdurar  n  twaɣit,  tawaɣit
Timerna
tezzi-assen !"
Melba  cekk  adlis-agi  yewwi-d  ameynut  ɣer  tsekla  taqbaylit,  d  aẓru
iṣeḥḥan  ɣef  ayeg  ara  yers  uɣalad  n  tira  ara  d-illalen  deg  imal  i  d-iteddun.  D
tullisin  ara  ɣren  yemdanen  s  tuget  n  lferḥ,  acku  taqbaylit  s  wacu  uran-t  d  tin
wuɣur  iwɛa  yal  yiwen, d tin  yessazalen amyag  n Si Muḥend U Mḥend s lxefa.
Aya  meṛṛa d ayen ara yeǧǧen, ulac akk ccek, inelmaden n teqbaylit yella wacu
ar  ad  d-affen  d  aɣanib,  d  talɣa  akken  ad  neǧren  ula  d  nitini  amyaru-nsen  deg
webrid n tira yettawin tutlayt ɣer zdat, imi ala s tira i-yettili wadud n tɣermiwin!
230
Timerna
